  var APP_BASE = (function() {
    try {
      var qp = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
      var v = String(qp.get('app_base') || '').trim();
      if (!v) v = String(localStorage.getItem('bookdeck_user_app_url') || '').trim();
      if (v) return v;
    } catch (_e) {}
    var href = String(window.location.href || '');
    var bare = href.split('#')[0];
    return bare;
  })();
  var API_BASE = (function() {
    try {
      var qp = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
      var v = String(qp.get('api_base') || '').trim();
      if (v) {
        if (v.endsWith('/')) v = v.slice(0, -1);
        if (!v.endsWith('/api')) v = v + '/api';
        try { localStorage.setItem('bookdeck_api_base', v); } catch (_e1) {}
        try { sessionStorage.setItem('bookdeck_api_base', v); } catch (_e2) {}
        return v;
      }
      v = String(sessionStorage.getItem('bookdeck_api_base') || localStorage.getItem('bookdeck_api_base') || '').trim();
      if (!v) v = 'https://bukit-production.up.railway.app';
      if (v.endsWith('/')) v = v.slice(0, -1);
      if (v.endsWith('/api')) return v;
      return v + '/api';
    } catch (e) {
      return 'https://bukit-production.up.railway.app/api';
    }
  })();

    'RED': 'Red Stüdyo',
    'PODCAST': 'Podcast Stüdyo',
    'DUBBING': 'Dublaj Stüdyo',

    'PODCAST': 'PKEY-01',

    'BLUE': 'BKEY-01'

  function normalizeAdmAscii_(raw) {
    return String(raw || '')
      .toLowerCase()
      .replace(/[çÇ]/g, 'c')
      .replace(/[ğĞ]/g, 'g')
      .replace(/[ıİ]/g, 'i')
      .replace(/[öÖ]/g, 'o')
      .replace(/[şŞ]/g, 's')
      .replace(/[üÜ]/g, 'u');
  }

  function normalizeStudioCanonical_(raw) {
    var s = normalizeAdmAscii_(raw);
    if (!s) return '';
    if (s.indexOf('green') >= 0 || s.indexOf('gkey') >= 0 || s.indexOf('yesil') >= 0) return 'GREEN';
    if (s.indexOf('red') >= 0 || s.indexOf('rkey') >= 0 || s.indexOf('kirmizi') >= 0) return 'RED';
    if (s.indexOf('podcast') >= 0 || s.indexOf('pkey') >= 0) return 'PODCAST';
    if (s.indexOf('dubbing') >= 0 || s.indexOf('dublaj') >= 0 || s.indexOf('dkey') >= 0) return 'DUBBING';
    if (s.indexOf('blue') >= 0 || s.indexOf('bkey') >= 0 || s.indexOf('mavi') >= 0) return 'BLUE';
    return '';
  }

  function studioNameFromCanonical_(studioCanonical) {
    var k = String(studioCanonical || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    return STUDIO_NAME_BY_CANONICAL[k] || '';
  }

  function studioKeyCodeFromCanonical_(studioCanonical) {
    var k = String(studioCanonical || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    return STUDIO_KEY_CODE_BY_CANONICAL[k] || '';
  }

  function looksLikeStudioKey_(name, type, code) {
    var blob = normalizeAdmAscii_([name, type, code].join(' '));
    if (!blob) return false;
    if (/(\b|_)(gkey|rkey|pkey|dkey|bkey)[-_ ]?\d*/.test(blob)) return true;
    if (blob.indexOf('studio key') >= 0) return true;
    if (blob.indexOf('studyo anahtar') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('stüdyo anahtar') >= 0) return true;
    if (blob.indexOf('anahtar') >= 0 && normalizeStudioCanonical_(blob)) return true;
    return false;
  }

  function escAdm(s) {
    if (s == null || s === undefined) return '';
    var t = String(s);
    return t.replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;').replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
  }

  function escAttr(s) {
    if (s == null || s === undefined) return '';
    return String(s).replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
  }

  function isUuidLike_(v) {
    var s = String(v || '').trim();
    return /^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$/i.test(s);
  }

  function publicEquipmentId_(code, id) {
    var c = String(code || '').trim();
    var i = String(id || '').trim();
    if (c && !isUuidLike_(c)) return c.toUpperCase();
    if (i && !isUuidLike_(i)) return i.toUpperCase();
    return '';
  }

  function formatAdminCardDtTr_(raw) {
    var s = String(raw || '').trim();
    if (!s) return '—';
    // Saati timezone donusumu yapmadan, kayitli degeri oldugu gibi goster.
    // Ornek: 2026-04-20T13:00:00Z -> 20.04 / 13.00
    var iso = s.match(/^(\d{4})-(\d{2})-(\d{2})[T\s](\d{2}):(\d{2})/);
    if (iso) return iso[3] + '.' + iso[2] + ' / ' + iso[4] + '.' + iso[5];

    var d = new Date(s);
    if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return s;
    var dd = String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
    var mm = String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
    var hh = String(d.getHours()).padStart(2, '0');
    var mi = String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0');
    return dd + '.' + mm + ' / ' + hh + '.' + mi;
  }

  function formatAdminDateTimeSlashColon_(raw) {
    var s = String(raw || '').trim();
    if (!s) return '—';
    // Saati timezone donusumu yapmadan, kayitli degeri oldugu gibi goster.
    // Ornek: 2026-04-21T14:00:00+00:00 -> 21.04 / 14:00
    var iso = s.match(/^(\d{4})-(\d{2})-(\d{2})[T\s](\d{2})[:.](\d{2})/);
    if (iso) return iso[3] + '.' + iso[2] + ' / ' + iso[4] + ':' + iso[5];

    var d = new Date(s);
    if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return s;
    var dd = String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
    var mm = String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
    var hh = String(d.getHours()).padStart(2, '0');
    var mi = String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0');
    return dd + '.' + mm + ' / ' + hh + ':' + mi;
  }

  function splitRawIsoDateTime_(raw) {
    var s = String(raw || '').trim();
    if (!s) return { date: '', time: '' };
    var iso = s.match(/^(\d{4})-(\d{2})-(\d{2})[T\s](\d{2}):(\d{2})/);
    if (iso) return { date: iso[1] + '-' + iso[2] + '-' + iso[3], time: iso[4] + ':' + iso[5] };
    var d = new Date(s);
    if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return { date: '', time: '' };
    return {
      date: String(d.getFullYear()) + '-' + String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0'),
      time: String(d.getHours()).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')
    };
  }

  function adminApiRequest(path, opts) {
    if (!API_BASE) return Promise.reject(new Error('API base tanımlı değil. URL sonuna ?api_base=https://... ekleyin.'));
    var token = String(currentAuthToken || '').trim();
    if (!token) {
      try { token = String(localStorage.getItem('bookdeck_auth_token') || '').trim(); } catch (e1) { token = ''; }
    }
    if (!token) {
      try { token = String(sessionStorage.getItem('bookdeck_auth_token') || '').trim(); } catch (e2) { token = ''; }
    }
    if (token) currentAuthToken = token;
    if (!token) return Promise.reject(new Error('Oturum bulunamadı. Lütfen tekrar giriş yapın.'));
    var o = opts || {};
    var method = o.method || 'GET';
    var headers = { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token };
    if (method !== 'GET') headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';
    return fetch(API_BASE + path, {
      method: method,
      headers: headers,
      body: (method === 'GET' || o.body == null) ? undefined : JSON.stringify(o.body)
    }).then(function(res) {
      return res.text().then(function(txt) {
        var data = {};
        try { data = txt ? JSON.parse(txt) : {}; } catch (e) { data = { error: txt || 'JSON parse error' }; }
        var msg = (data && data.error) || ('HTTP ' + res.status);
        var msgLower = String(msg || '').toLowerCase();
        var tokenErr = /unauthorized|invalid token|jwt|token expired|session expired|forbidden/.test(msgLower);
        if (res.status === 401 || res.status === 403 || tokenErr) {
          try { localStorage.removeItem('bookdeck_auth_token'); } catch (e3) {}
          try { sessionStorage.removeItem('bookdeck_auth_token'); } catch (e4) {}
          currentAuthToken = '';
          showToast('Oturum süresi doldu. Admin giriş ekranına yönlendiriliyorsunuz.', 'error');
          setTimeout(function() {
            var loginUrl = buildAdminLoginUrl_();
            try { window.top.location.href = loginUrl; }
            catch (_eNav) { window.location.href = loginUrl; }
          }, 700);
          throw new Error('Session expired. Please sign in again.');
        }
        if (!res.ok || (data && data.ok === false)) {
          throw new Error(msg);
        }
        return data;
      });
    });
  }
  function adminApiPublicRequest(path, opts) {
    if (!API_BASE) return Promise.reject(new Error('API base tanımlı değil. URL sonuna ?api_base=https://... ekleyin.'));
    var o = opts || {};
    var method = o.method || 'GET';
    var headers = o.headers || {};
    if (method !== 'GET' && !headers['Content-Type']) headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';
    return fetch(API_BASE + path, {
      method: method,
      headers: headers,
      body: (method === 'GET' || o.body == null) ? undefined : JSON.stringify(o.body)
    }).then(function(res) {
      return res.text().then(function(txt) {
        var data = {};
        try { data = txt ? JSON.parse(txt) : {}; } catch (e) { data = { error: txt || 'JSON parse error' }; }
        if (!res.ok || (data && data.ok === false)) throw new Error((data && data.error) || ('HTTP ' + res.status));
        return data;
      });
    });
  }

      box.classList.remove('hidden');
    } else {
      box.classList.add('hidden');
    }
  }

  function installAdminApiScriptRunShim_() {
    function isActiveReservationStatus_(s) {
      var st = String(s || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      return st === 'pending' || st === 'approved' || st === 'approved_by_admin' || st === 'in_use' || st === 'checked_out' || st === 'picked_up' || st === 'key_out' || st === 'key_picked';
    }
    function buildScriptRunner(methodMap) {
      var onSuccess = null;
      var onFailure = null;
      var base = {
        withSuccessHandler: function(fn) { onSuccess = fn; return proxy; },
        withFailureHandler: function(fn) { onFailure = fn; return proxy; }
      };
      function doneSuccess(v) {
        var cb = onSuccess;
        onSuccess = null;
        onFailure = null;
        if (typeof cb === 'function') cb(v);
      }
      function doneFailure(err) {
        var cb = onFailure;
        onSuccess = null;
        onFailure = null;
        if (typeof cb === 'function') cb(err);
      }
      var proxy = new Proxy(base, {
        get: function(target, prop) {
          if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(target, prop)) return target[prop];
          return function() {
            var args = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
            var fn = methodMap[String(prop)];
            Promise.resolve()
              .then(function() {
                if (typeof fn !== 'function') throw new Error('No API mapping for ' + String(prop));
                return fn.apply(null, args);
              })
              .then(doneSuccess)
              .catch(doneFailure);
            return undefined;
          };
        }
      });
      return proxy;
    }
    function mapAccessFromProfile_(profile) {
      var p = profile || {};
      var role = String(p.role || '').trim().toLowerCase();

        isSuperAdmin: role === 'super_admin'
      };
    }
    function toIsoDateLocal_(raw) {
      var d = raw instanceof Date ? new Date(raw.getTime()) : new Date(String(raw || ''));
      if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return '';
      try {
        var parts = new Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-CA', {
          timeZone: 'Europe/Istanbul',
          year: 'numeric',
          month: '2-digit',
          day: '2-digit'
        }).formatToParts(d);
        var map = {};
        parts.forEach(function(p) { map[p.type] = p.value; });
        if (map.year && map.month && map.day) return map.year + '-' + map.month + '-' + map.day;
      } catch (_eFmtDate) {}
      var y = d.getFullYear();
      var m = String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
      var day = String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
      return y + '-' + m + '-' + day;
    }
    function hhmmFromIso_(raw) {
      var d = new Date(String(raw || ''));
      if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return '—';
      try {
        var parts = new Intl.DateTimeFormat('tr-TR', {
          timeZone: 'Europe/Istanbul',
          hour: '2-digit',
          minute: '2-digit',
          hour12: false
        }).formatToParts(d);
        var map = {};
        parts.forEach(function(p) { map[p.type] = p.value; });
        if (map.hour && map.minute) return map.hour + ':' + map.minute;
      } catch (_eFmtTime) {}
      return String(d.getHours()).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0');
    }
    function trafficActiveStatus_(status) {
      var s = String(status || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      if (!s) return false;
      if (s === 'pending' || s === 'approved' || s === 'approved_by_admin') return true;
      if (s === 'in_use' || s === 'checked_out' || s === 'picked_up' || s === 'key_out' || s === 'key_picked') return true;
      if (s === 'key_returned' || s === 'returned' || s === 'completed') return false;
      if (s.indexOf('cancel') >= 0 || s.indexOf('reject') >= 0) return false;
      if (s === 'onaylı' || s === 'onayli' || s === 'beklemede') return true;
      if (s.indexOf('approved') >= 0 || s.indexOf('pending') >= 0 || s.indexOf('onay') >= 0 || s.indexOf('bekle') >= 0) return true;
      if (s.indexOf('in_use') >= 0 || s.indexOf('kullanimda') >= 0 || s.indexOf('disarida') >= 0) return true;
      if (s.indexOf('picked') >= 0 || s.indexOf('checked') >= 0 || s.indexOf('key_picked') >= 0) return true;
      return false;
    }
    function trafficCanShowReturn_(status) {
      var raw = String(status || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      if (!raw) return false;
      var s = raw
        .replace(/[çÇ]/g, 'c')
        .replace(/[ğĞ]/g, 'g')
        .replace(/[ıİ]/g, 'i')
        .replace(/[öÖ]/g, 'o')
        .replace(/[şŞ]/g, 's')
        .replace(/[üÜ]/g, 'u')
        .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '_')
        .replace(/^_+|_+$/g, '');
      // Iade karti sadece fiilen teslim edilmis kayitlarda gorunsun.
      // pending/approved kayitlarda (ayni gun olsa bile) iade akisi acilmamali.
      var outStatuses = {
        in_use: true,
        checked_out: true,
        checkedout: true,
        picked_up: true,
        pickedup: true,
        key_picked: true,
        key_out: true,
        keyout: true,
        disarida: true,
        kullanimda: true,
        teslim_edildi: true
      };
      return outStatuses[s] === true;
    }
    function buildTrafficRows_(equipmentRows, studioRows, itemMetaById, studioMetaById, dayIso, qNorm) {
      var all = [];
      var studioMap = studioMetaById || {};
      (equipmentRows || []).forEach(function(r) {
        if (!trafficActiveStatus_(r && r.status)) return;
        var eqId = String((r && r.equipment_item_id) || '').trim();
        var meta = itemMetaById[eqId] || {};
        var prettyCode = publicEquipmentId_(meta.code, eqId);
        var prettyName = String(meta.name || '').trim();
        if (!prettyName || isUuidLike_(prettyName)) prettyName = prettyCode || 'Ekipman';
        var studioCanonical = normalizeStudioCanonical_([
          meta.studioKey,
          meta.studioName,
          meta.name,
          meta.type,
          meta.code,
          (r && r.note),
          (r && r.purpose)
        ].join(' '));
        var isStudioKeyRow = Boolean(meta.isStudioKey) || looksLikeStudioKey_(meta.name, meta.type, meta.code) || Boolean(studioCanonical);
        var keyCode = studioKeyCodeFromCanonical_(studioCanonical);
        if (!keyCode && /^[A-Z]KEY-\d+/i.test(String(prettyCode || ''))) keyCode = String(prettyCode || '').toUpperCase();
        if (!keyCode && /^[A-Z]KEY-\d+/i.test(String(meta.code || ''))) keyCode = String(meta.code || '').toUpperCase();
        var studioName = String(meta.studioName || '').trim() || studioNameFromCanonical_(studioCanonical) || 'Stüdyo';
        var item = {
          id: eqId,
          name: isStudioKeyRow ? (keyCode || 'STUDIO KEY') : prettyName,
          eqId: eqId,
          eqCode: isStudioKeyRow ? (keyCode || prettyCode || '') : (prettyCode || ''),
          eqType: isStudioKeyRow ? 'studio key' : String(meta.type || ''),
          isStudioKey: isStudioKeyRow,
          kind: isStudioKeyRow ? 'studio_key' : 'equipment_item',
          studioName: studioName,
          studioId: studioCanonical
        };
        var base = {
          id: String((r && r.id) || ''),
          kind: isStudioKeyRow ? 'studio' : 'equipment',
          trafficKind: isStudioKeyRow ? 'studio' : 'equipment',
          studioId: isStudioKeyRow ? studioCanonical : '',
          studioName: isStudioKeyRow ? studioName : '',
          userName: String((r && (r.requester_name || r.requester_email)) || '—'),
          email: String((r && r.requester_email) || ''),
          phone: '',
          handoverLabel: String((r && r.start_at) || ''),
          returnLabel: String((r && r.end_at) || ''),
          purpose: String((r && (r.note || r.purpose)) || ''),
          status: String((r && r.status) || ''),
          items: [item]
        };
        var eqNeedsReturn = trafficCanShowReturn_(base.status);
        if (!eqNeedsReturn) {
          all.push(Object.assign({}, base, { type: 'pickup', time: formatAdminCardDtTr_(base.handoverLabel) }));
        }
        if (eqNeedsReturn) {
          all.push(Object.assign({}, base, { type: 'return', time: formatAdminCardDtTr_(base.returnLabel) }));
        }
      });
      (studioRows || []).forEach(function(r) {
        if (!trafficActiveStatus_(r && r.status)) return;
        var sId = String((r && r.studio_id) || '').trim();
        var sMeta = studioMap[sId] || studioMap[String(sId || '').toUpperCase()] || {};
        var studioCanonical = normalizeStudioCanonical_([
          (sMeta && sMeta.canonical),
          sId,
          (r && r.studio_name),
          (sMeta && sMeta.name),
          (sMeta && sMeta.code)
        ].join(' '));
        var sName = String((r && (r.studio_name || r.studio_id)) || '').trim()
          || String((sMeta && sMeta.name) || '').trim()
          || studioNameFromCanonical_(studioCanonical)
          || 'Stüdyo';
        var sKeyCode = String((sMeta && sMeta.keyCode) || '').trim() || studioKeyCodeFromCanonical_(studioCanonical);
        var sItem = {
          id: sId || String((r && r.id) || ''),
          name: sKeyCode || 'STUDIO KEY',
          eqId: sId || String((r && r.id) || ''),
          eqCode: sKeyCode || sId || 'STUDIO',
          eqType: 'studio key',
          isStudioKey: true,
          kind: 'studio_key',
          studioId: studioCanonical || sId,
          studioName: sName
        };
        var baseSt = {
          id: String((r && r.id) || ''),
          kind: 'studio',
          trafficKind: 'studio',
          studioId: studioCanonical || sId,
          studioName: sName,
          userName: String((r && (r.requester_name || r.requester_email)) || '—'),
          email: String((r && r.requester_email) || ''),
          phone: '',
          handoverLabel: String((r && r.start_at) || ''),
          returnLabel: String((r && r.end_at) || ''),
          purpose: String((r && r.purpose) || ''),
          status: String((r && r.status) || ''),
          items: [sItem]
        };
        var stNeedsReturn = trafficCanShowReturn_(baseSt.status);
        if (!stNeedsReturn) {
          all.push(Object.assign({}, baseSt, { type: 'pickup', time: formatAdminCardDtTr_(baseSt.handoverLabel) }));
        }
        if (stNeedsReturn) {
          all.push(Object.assign({}, baseSt, { type: 'return', time: formatAdminCardDtTr_(baseSt.returnLabel) }));
        }
      });
      if (dayIso) {
        all = all.filter(function(x) {
          return x.type === 'pickup'
            ? toIsoDateLocal_(x.handoverLabel) === dayIso
            : toIsoDateLocal_(x.returnLabel) === dayIso;
        });
      }
      if (qNorm) {
        all = all.filter(function(x) {
          var blob = [
            x.userName,
            x.email,
            x.phone,
            x.id,
            x.purpose,
            x.studioName,
            (x.items || []).map(function(i) { return [i.name, i.eqCode, i.eqType].join(' '); }).join(' ')
          ].join(' ').toLowerCase();
          return blob.indexOf(String(qNorm || '').toLowerCase()) >= 0;
        });
      }
      return all.sort(function(a, b) {
        var aMs = new Date(String(a.type === 'pickup' ? a.handoverLabel : a.returnLabel) || '').getTime();
        var bMs = new Date(String(b.type === 'pickup' ? b.handoverLabel : b.returnLabel) || '').getTime();
        return bMs - aMs;
      });
    }
    var methods = {

          .then(function(res) { return mapAccessFromProfile_(res && res.profile); })
          .catch(function() { return { ok: false, isIiwPanelOnly: false, isSuperAdmin: false, name: 'Admin', role: 'admin' }; });
      },

              }

      adminCheckItemAvailabilityBridge: function(itemId, startIso, endIso) {
        var id = String(itemId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        return adminApiRequest('/equipment-reservations', { method: 'GET' }).then(function(res) {
          var rows = (res && res.data) || [];
          var sMs = new Date(String(startIso || '')).getTime();
          var eMs = new Date(String(endIso || '')).getTime();
          var busy = rows.some(function(r) {
            if (String((r && r.equipment_item_id) || '').trim().toUpperCase() !== id) return false;
            if (!isActiveReservationStatus_(r && r.status)) return false;
            var rs = new Date(String((r && r.start_at) || '')).getTime();
            var re = new Date(String((r && r.end_at) || '')).getTime();
            if (isNaN(rs) || isNaN(re)) return false;
            return rs < eMs && re > sMs;
          });
          return { ok: true, available: !busy };
        }).catch(function(err) {
          return { ok: false, available: false, error: (err && err.message) || 'Availability check failed.' };
        });
      },

      adminUserLookup: function(query) {
        return adminApiRequest('/admin/lookup-user', {
          method: 'POST',
          body: { query: String(query || '').trim() }
        }).then(function(res) {
          if (!res || res.ok === false) return { error: (res && res.error) || 'Lookup failed.', matches: [] };
          if (Array.isArray(res.matches)) return res;
          if (res.note === 'not_found') return { matches: [] };
          var loansRaw = Array.isArray(res.loans) ? res.loans : [];
          var loansOnHand = loansRaw.map(function(l) {
            return {
              name: String((l && l.name) || '').trim(),
              eqId: String((l && l.eqId) || '').trim(),
              due: String((l && l.due) || '').trim(),
              overdue: !!(l && l.overdue)
            };
          }).filter(function(l) { return !!(l.name || l.eqId || l.due); });
          var profile = {
            name: String(res.name || '').trim(),
            email: String(res.email || '').trim(),
            student_no: String(res.studentId || '').trim(),
            id: String(res.studentId || '').trim(),
            role: String(res.role || '').trim(),
            level: String(res.level || ''),
            department: String(res.department || '').trim(),
            phone: ''
          };
          return {
            matches: [{
              profile: profile,
              studentIdDisplay: profile.student_no,
              userTypeLabel: profile.level ? ('Seviye ' + profile.level) : '',
              equipmentHistory: [],
              pendingEquipmentApprovals: [],
              pendingStudioApprovals: [],
              equipmentRecent15d: [],
              loansOnHand: loansOnHand,
              responsibleForEquipment: []
            }]
          };
        });
      },
      getAdminReservationHistory: function() {
        return Promise.all([
          adminApiRequest('/equipment-reservations', { method: 'GET' }),
          adminApiRequest('/equipment-items', { method: 'GET' })
        ]).then(function(arr) {
          var eqRes = arr[0] || {};
          var invRes = arr[1] || {};
          var rows = Array.isArray(eqRes.data) ? eqRes.data : [];
          var inv = Array.isArray(invRes.data) ? invRes.data : [];
          var nameById = {};
          var codeById = {};
          inv.forEach(function(it) {
            var iid = String((it && it.id) || '').trim();
            if (!iid) return;
            nameById[iid] = String((it && it.name) || iid);
            codeById[iid] = String((it && (it.equipment_id || it.code)) || '').trim().toUpperCase();
          });
          return rows.map(function(r) {
            var eqId = String((r && r.equipment_item_id) || '').trim();
            return {
              resId: String((r && r.id) || ''),
              eqCode: codeById[eqId] || '',
              eqName: nameById[eqId] || eqId || '—',
              userName: String((r && (r.requester_name || r.requester_email)) || '—'),
              startDt: String((r && r.start_at) || ''),
              endDt: String((r && r.end_at) || ''),
              status: String((r && r.status) || '')
            };
          }).sort(function(a, b) {
            return new Date(String(b.startDt || '')).getTime() - new Date(String(a.startDt || '')).getTime();
          });
        }).catch(function() {
          return [];
        });
      },

        var ids = Array.isArray(equipmentIds) ? equipmentIds.map(function(x) { return String(x || '').trim(); }).filter(Boolean) : [];
        if (!ids.length) return Promise.resolve({ success: false, error: 'Seçim yok.', sent: 0, skipped: 0 });
        return adminApiRequest('/admin/overdue-reminders', {
          method: 'POST',

        }).then(function(res) {
          if (!res || res.ok === false || res.success === false) {
            return {
              success: false,
              error: (res && res.error) || 'Hatırlatma gönderimi başarısız.',
              sent: Number((res && res.sent) || 0),
              skipped: Number((res && res.skipped) || 0)
            };
          }
          return { success: true, sent: Number(res.sent || 0), skipped: Number(res.skipped || 0) };
        }).catch(function(err) {
          return { success: false, error: (err && err.message) || 'Hatırlatma gönderimi başarısız.', sent: 0, skipped: ids.length };
        });
      },

      getTrafficData: function(dateIso) {
        var dayIso = String(dateIso || '').trim();
        return Promise.all([
          adminApiRequest('/equipment-reservations', { method: 'GET' }),
          adminApiRequest('/studio-reservations', { method: 'GET' }),
          adminApiRequest('/equipment-items', { method: 'GET' }),
          adminApiRequest('/studios', { method: 'GET' })
        ]).then(function(arr) {
          var eqRows = (arr[0] && arr[0].data) || [];
          var stRows = (arr[1] && arr[1].data) || [];
          var invRows = (arr[2] && arr[2].data) || [];
          var studioRows = (arr[3] && arr[3].data) || [];
          var itemMetaById = {};
          (invRows || []).forEach(function(it) {
            var iid = String((it && it.id) || '').trim();
            if (!iid) return;
            var meta = {
              name: String((it && it.name) || iid),
              type: String((it && (it.category || it.type)) || ''),
              code: String((it && (it.equipment_id || it.id)) || iid),
              isStudioKey: looksLikeStudioKey_(it && it.name, it && (it.category || it.type), it && (it.equipment_id || it.id)),
              studioKey: normalizeStudioCanonical_([
                (it && it.name),
                (it && (it.category || it.type)),
                (it && (it.equipment_id || it.id))
              ].join(' ')),
              studioName: ''
            };
            itemMetaById[iid] = meta;
            var publicCode = String((it && it.equipment_id) || '').trim();
            if (publicCode) itemMetaById[publicCode] = meta;
          });
          var studioMetaById = {};
          (studioRows || []).forEach(function(st) {
            var sid = String((st && st.id) || '').trim();
            var canonical = normalizeStudioCanonical_([
              (st && st.id),
              (st && (st.studio_id || st.code || st.name))
            ].join(' '));
            var name = String((st && (st.name || st.studio_name || st.code || st.id)) || '').trim() || studioNameFromCanonical_(canonical) || 'Stüdyo';
            var metaSt = { canonical: canonical, name: name, keyCode: studioKeyCodeFromCanonical_(canonical), code: String((st && (st.code || st.studio_id || st.id)) || '').trim() };
            if (sid) studioMetaById[sid] = metaSt;
            if (canonical) studioMetaById[canonical] = metaSt;
          });
          return buildTrafficRows_(eqRows, stRows, itemMetaById, studioMetaById, dayIso, '');
        }).catch(function() { return []; });
      },
      getTrafficDataByNameOrStudent: function(q) {
        var qNorm = String(q || '').trim().toLowerCase();
        if (!qNorm) return Promise.resolve([]);
        return Promise.all([
          adminApiRequest('/equipment-reservations', { method: 'GET' }),
          adminApiRequest('/studio-reservations', { method: 'GET' }),
          adminApiRequest('/equipment-items', { method: 'GET' }),

          var stRows = (arr[1] && arr[1].data) || [];
          var invRows = (arr[2] && arr[2].data) || [];
          var studioRows = (arr[3] && arr[3].data) || [];
          var itemMetaById = {};
          (invRows || []).forEach(function(it) {
            var iid = String((it && it.id) || '').trim();
            if (!iid) return;
            var meta = {
              name: String((it && it.name) || iid),
              type: String((it && (it.category || it.type)) || ''),
              code: String((it && (it.equipment_id || it.id)) || iid),
              isStudioKey: looksLikeStudioKey_(it && it.name, it && (it.category || it.type), it && (it.equipment_id || it.id)),
              studioKey: normalizeStudioCanonical_([
                (it && it.name),
                (it && (it.category || it.type)),
                (it && (it.equipment_id || it.id))
              ].join(' ')),
              studioName: ''
            };
            itemMetaById[iid] = meta;
            var publicCode = String((it && it.equipment_id) || '').trim();
            if (publicCode) itemMetaById[publicCode] = meta;
          });
          var studioMetaById = {};
          (studioRows || []).forEach(function(st) {
            var sid = String((st && st.id) || '').trim();
            var canonical = normalizeStudioCanonical_([
              (st && st.id),
              (st && (st.studio_id || st.code || st.name))
            ].join(' '));

            var metaSt = { canonical: canonical, name: name, keyCode: studioKeyCodeFromCanonical_(canonical), code: String((st && (st.code || st.studio_id || st.id)) || '').trim() };
            if (sid) studioMetaById[sid] = metaSt;
            if (canonical) studioMetaById[canonical] = metaSt;
          });
          return buildTrafficRows_(eqRows, stRows, itemMetaById, studioMetaById, '', qNorm);
        }).catch(function() { return []; });
      },

  function closePdfViewModal() {
    var m = document.getElementById('pdf-view-modal');
    var f = document.getElementById('pdf-view-frame');
    if (f) f.src = 'about:blank';
    if (m) m.classList.add('hidden');
  }

  function closeAdminUiDialog() {
    var m = document.getElementById('admin-ui-dialog');
    if (m) m.classList.add('hidden');
    adminUiDialogCb = null;
  }

  function openAdminUiDialog(opts, cb) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var m = document.getElementById('admin-ui-dialog');
    var t = document.getElementById('admin-ui-dialog-title');
    var d = document.getElementById('admin-ui-dialog-desc');
    var w = document.getElementById('admin-ui-dialog-input-wrap');
    var i = document.getElementById('admin-ui-dialog-input');
    var dw = document.getElementById('admin-ui-dialog-datetime-wrap');
    var di = document.getElementById('admin-ui-dialog-date');
    var ti = document.getElementById('admin-ui-dialog-time');
    var e = document.getElementById('admin-ui-dialog-error');
    var ok = document.getElementById('admin-ui-dialog-ok');
    var ic = document.getElementById('admin-ui-dialog-icon');
    if (!m || !t || !d || !w || !i || !dw || !di || !ti || !e || !ok || !ic) return;
    t.innerText = String(opts.title || 'İşlem');
    d.innerText = String(opts.desc || '');
    var tone = String(opts.tone || 'info').toLowerCase();
    var iconMap = { info: 'ℹ️', warning: '⚠️', danger: '🗑️', success: '✅' };
    var btnClassMap = {
      info: 'bg-gray-900 hover:bg-black',
      warning: 'bg-amber-600 hover:bg-amber-700',
      danger: 'bg-[#e30613] hover:bg-red-700',
      success: 'bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-700'
    };
    var titleClassMap = {
      info: 'text-gray-900',
      warning: 'text-amber-700',
      danger: 'text-red-700',
      success: 'text-green-700'
    };
    if (!iconMap[tone]) tone = 'info';
    ic.innerText = iconMap[tone];
    t.className = 'text-lg font-black ' + titleClassMap[tone];
    ok.className = 'flex-1 text-white font-black py-3 rounded-xl text-xs transition ' + btnClassMap[tone];
    var needInput = !!opts.input;
    var inputMode = String(opts.inputMode || 'text').toLowerCase();
    var useDateTime = needInput && inputMode === 'datetime_split';
    var useText = needInput && !useDateTime;
    w.classList.toggle('hidden', !useText);
    dw.classList.toggle('hidden', !useDateTime);
    i.value = String(opts.defaultValue || '');
    i.placeholder = String(opts.placeholder || '');
    var seeded = splitRawIsoDateTime_(opts.defaultValue || '');
    di.value = String(opts.defaultDate || seeded.date || '');
    ti.value = String(opts.defaultTime || seeded.time || '');
    e.classList.add('hidden');
    ok.innerText = String(opts.okText || 'Onayla');
    adminUiDialogCb = function() {
      var val = '';
      if (useDateTime) {
        var dVal = String(di.value || '').trim();
        var tVal = String(ti.value || '').trim();
        if (opts.required && (!dVal || !tVal)) {
          e.innerText = String(opts.requiredMessage || 'Bu alan zorunlu.');
          e.classList.remove('hidden');
          if (!dVal) di.focus();
          else ti.focus();
          return;
        }
        val = (dVal && tVal) ? (dVal + 'T' + tVal + ':00') : '';
      } else {
        val = String(i.value || '').trim();
        if (needInput && opts.required && !val) {
          e.innerText = String(opts.requiredMessage || 'Bu alan zorunlu.');
          e.classList.remove('hidden');
          i.focus();
          return;
        }
      }
      var f = cb;
      closeAdminUiDialog();
      if (typeof f === 'function') f(val);
    };
    ok.onclick = function() { if (adminUiDialogCb) adminUiDialogCb(); };
    m.classList.remove('hidden');
    if (needInput) {
      setTimeout(function() {
        try {
          if (useDateTime) {
            if (!di.value) di.focus();
            else ti.focus();
          } else i.focus();
        } catch (_e) {}
      }, 10);
    }
  }

  function openAdminStudentPdfView(url) {
    var u = String(url || '').trim();
    if (!u) { showToast('PDF bağlantısı yok.', 'error'); return; }
    var ok = u.indexOf('http') === 0 || u.indexOf('data:application/pdf') === 0 || u.indexOf('data:') === 0;
    if (!ok) { showToast('PDF bağlantısı geçersiz.', 'error'); return; }
    var f = document.getElementById('pdf-view-frame');
    var m = document.getElementById('pdf-view-modal');
    if (!f || !m) return;
    f.src = u;
    m.classList.remove('hidden');
  }

  function printAdminPdfIframe(iframeId) {
    var f = document.getElementById(iframeId);
    try {
      if (f && f.contentWindow) {
        f.contentWindow.focus();
        f.contentWindow.print();
      }
    } catch (e0) { showToast('Yazdırma penceresi açılamadı.', 'error'); }
  }

  function openAdminStudentPdfFromBtn(el) {
    var u = el && el.getAttribute('data-pdf-url');
    if (u) openAdminStudentPdfView(u);
  }

  function trafficReturnStatusSelectHtml(actId, trafficKind, itemKey) {
    var id = 'traffic-return-status-' + actId + '-' + trafficSafeDomId(itemKey || 'item');
    var isStudio = (trafficKind === 'studio');
    var h = '<div class="pl-7 mt-1.5" onclick="event.stopPropagation();"><label class="block text-[8px] font-black text-gray-400 uppercase mb-0.5 tracking-wide">İade Teslim Durumu</label><select id="' + id + '" class="w-full max-w-xs text-[10px] border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-2 bg-white outline-none focus:border-[#e30613]" onclick="event.stopPropagation();">';
    h += '<option value="">— Seçin —</option>';
    if (!isStudio) {
      h += '<optgroup label="Ekipman (Condition In)">';
      h += '<option value="Excellent">Excellent</option>';
      h += '<option value="Minor Scratch">Minor Scratch</option>';
      h += '<option value="DAMAGED">DAMAGED</option>';
      h += '</optgroup>';
    }
    if (isStudio) {
      h += '<optgroup label="Stüdyo (İade Teslim Notu)">';
      h += '<option value="Sorunsuz-No Issues">Sorunsuz-No Issues</option>';
      h += '<option value="Duzensiz-Disorganized">Duzensiz-Disorganized</option>';
      h += '<option value="Eksik Ekipman-Missing Equipment">Eksik Ekipman-Missing Equipment</option>';
      h += '<option value="Hasarli Alan-Needs Repair">Hasarli Alan-Needs Repair</option>';
      h += '<option value="Kullanilamaz Durumda-Damaged Area">Kullanilamaz Durumda-Damaged Area</option>';
      h += '</optgroup>';
    }
    h += '</select></div>';
    return h;
  }

  function trafficStudioPickupStatusSelectHtml(actId) {
    var id = 'traffic-pickup-status-' + actId;
    var h = '<div class="mb-3"><label class="block text-[9px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1 tracking-wider">Teslim Durumu</label><select id="' + id + '" class="w-full text-xs border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-2.5 bg-white font-medium outline-none focus:border-[#e30613]">';
    h += '<option value="Sorunsuz-No Issues" selected>Sorunsuz-No Issues</option>';
    h += '<option value="Duzensiz-Disorganized">Duzensiz-Disorganized</option>';
    h += '<option value="Eksik Ekipman-Missing Equipment">Eksik Ekipman-Missing Equipment</option>';
    h += '<option value="Hasarli Alan-Needs Repair">Hasarli Alan-Needs Repair</option>';
    h += '<option value="Kullanilamaz Durumda-Damaged Area">Kullanilamaz Durumda-Damaged Area</option>';
    h += '</select></div>';
    return h;
  }

  function trafficSafeDomId(resId) {
    return String(resId || '').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]/g, '_');
  }

  function renderStudioEquipList() {
    var list = document.getElementById('sr-equip-list');
    var qEl = document.getElementById('sr-equip-q');
    var cnt = document.getElementById('sr-equip-count');
    if (!list) return;
    var q = qEl ? String(qEl.value || '').toLowerCase().trim() : '';
    var filtered = (studioEquipPool || []).filter(function(it) {
      var blob = (String(it.name || '') + ' ' + String(it.code || it.id || '') + ' ' + String(it.type || '')).toLowerCase();
      return !q || blob.indexOf(q) >= 0;
    });
    list.innerHTML = '';
    filtered.forEach(function(it) {
      var id = String(it.id || '');
      if (!id) return;
      var checked = studioEquipSelected[id] === true;
      list.innerHTML += '<label class="flex items-center gap-2 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-xl p-2 text-xs cursor-pointer">' +
        '<input type="checkbox" class="sr-eq-cb w-4 h-4" data-eqid="' + escAttr(id) + '"' + (checked ? ' checked' : '') + '>' +
        '<div class="min-w-0"><p class="font-bold text-gray-800 truncate">' + escAdm(it.name || id) + '</p><p class="text-[10px] text-gray-400 font-mono">' + escAdm(publicEquipmentId_(it.code, id)) + (it.type ? (' · ' + escAdm(it.type)) : '') + '</p></div>' +
        '</label>';
    });
    if (!list.innerHTML) list.innerHTML = '<p class="text-[10px] text-gray-400 p-2">Ekipman bulunamadı.</p>';
    if (cnt) {
      var total = (studioEquipPool || []).length;
      var sel = 0;
      (studioEquipPool || []).forEach(function(it) { if (studioEquipSelected[String(it.id || '')] === true) sel++; });
      cnt.innerText = sel + ' / ' + total + ' seçili';
    }
  }

  function loadStudioEquipmentAvailability() {
    var withEq = document.getElementById('sr-with-equip');
    if (!withEq || !withEq.checked) return;
    var date = document.getElementById('sr-date').value;
    var st = document.getElementById('sr-start').value;
    var en = document.getElementById('sr-end').value;
    if (!date || !st || !en) { showToast('Önce stüdyo teslim/iade saatlerini girin.', 'error'); return; }
    var startDt = date + 'T' + st;
    var endDt = date + 'T' + en;
    if (new Date(endDt).getTime() <= new Date(startDt).getTime()) { showToast('Bitiş saati başlangıçtan sonra olmalı.', 'error'); return; }
    adminApiRequest('/admin/equipment/forward-available', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: { start_at: startDt, end_at: endDt }
    }).then(function(r) {
      studioEquipPool = r.list || [];
      studioEquipSelected = {};
      renderStudioEquipList();
      showToast('Müsait ekipman: ' + String(studioEquipPool.length || 0), 'success');
    }).catch(function(e) {
      showToast((e && e.message) || 'Hata', 'error');
    });
  }

  function trafficRowMatchesQuery(item, q) {
    if (!q) return true;
    var n = String(q).toLowerCase().trim();
    if (!n) return true;
    var blob = [item.userName, item.email, item.phone || '', item.studentId || ''].map(function(x) { return String(x || '').toLowerCase(); }).join(' ');
    return blob.indexOf(n) !== -1;
  }

  function trafficCheckoutConditionOutMap(resId, itemIds) {
    var actId = trafficSafeDomId(resId);
    var m = {};
    (itemIds || []).forEach(function(eqId) {
      var sel = document.getElementById('traffic-co-' + actId + '-' + trafficSafeDomId(eqId));
      if (sel && sel.value) m[eqId] = sel.value;
    });
    return m;
  }

  function trafficCountByType_(type) {
    return (trafficAllRows || []).filter(function(x) {
      return String(x && x.type || '').toLowerCase() === String(type || '').toLowerCase();
    }).length;
  }

  function trafficRefreshTabUi_() {
    var pickupBtn = document.getElementById('traffic-tab-pickup');
    var returnBtn = document.getElementById('traffic-tab-return');
    var pickupCountEl = document.getElementById('traffic-tab-pickup-count');
    var returnCountEl = document.getElementById('traffic-tab-return-count');
    var pickupCount = trafficCountByType_('pickup');
    var returnCount = trafficCountByType_('return');
    if (pickupCountEl) pickupCountEl.textContent = String(pickupCount);
    if (returnCountEl) returnCountEl.textContent = String(returnCount);
    var baseBtn = 'px-4 py-2 rounded-xl text-xs font-black transition';
    if (pickupBtn) {
      pickupBtn.className = baseBtn + (trafficViewTab === 'pickup'
        ? ' bg-gray-900 text-white shadow-sm'
        : ' bg-white text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-50');
    }
    if (returnBtn) {
      returnBtn.className = baseBtn + (trafficViewTab === 'return'
        ? ' bg-gray-900 text-white shadow-sm'
        : ' bg-white text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-50');
    }
  }

  function setTrafficViewTab(tab) {
    trafficViewTab = String(tab || '').toLowerCase() === 'return' ? 'return' : 'pickup';
    trafficRefreshTabUi_();
    renderTrafficFromCache();
  }

  function renderTrafficFromCache() {
    var container = document.getElementById('traffic-container');
    if (!container) return;
    var qEl = document.getElementById('traffic-search-q');
    var q = qEl ? String(qEl.value || '') : '';
    var qNorm = q.toLowerCase().trim();
    if (qNorm.length >= 2) {
      if (trafficSearchMode !== 'global' || trafficGlobalQuery !== qNorm) {
        loadTrafficByQuery(qNorm);
        return;
      }
    } else if (trafficSearchMode === 'global') {
      loadTraffic();
      return;
    }
    trafficRefreshTabUi_();
    var filteredByQuery = (trafficAllRows || []).filter(function(item) { return trafficRowMatchesQuery(item, q); });
    var data = filteredByQuery.filter(function(item) {
      var t = String(item && item.type || '').toLowerCase();
      if (trafficViewTab === 'return') return t === 'return';
      return t === 'pickup';
    });
    trafficMetaByResId = {};
    if (!trafficAllRows.length) {
      container.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-2 text-center text-gray-400 italic mt-10 font-medium">İşlem kaydı yok.</div>';
      return;
    }
    if (!filteredByQuery.length) {
      container.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-2 text-center text-gray-400 italic mt-10 font-medium">Filtreye uygun kayıt yok.</div>';
      return;
    }
    if (!data.length) {
      container.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-2 text-center text-gray-400 italic mt-10 font-medium">' + (trafficViewTab === 'pickup' ? 'Depodan çıkış sekmesinde kayıt yok.' : 'Depoya iade sekmesinde kayıt yok.') + '</div>';
      return;
    }
    container.innerHTML = '';
    data.forEach(function(item) {
      var kindRaw = String(item.kind || item.trafficKind || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      var tKind = (kindRaw === 'studio' || kindRaw === 'studio_key') ? 'studio' : 'equipment';
      trafficMetaByResId[String(item.id || '')] = {
        kind: tKind,
        reservationIds: Array.isArray(item.reservationIds) ? item.reservationIds.slice() : [String(item.id || '')].filter(Boolean),
        primaryReservationId: String(item.primaryReservationId || item.id || '')
      };
      var isPickup = (item.type === 'pickup');
      var color = isPickup ? 'border-red-500' : 'border-green-500';
      var badgeColor = isPickup ? 'bg-red-100 text-red-700' : 'bg-green-100 text-green-700';
      var flowBadge = (function() {
        if (tKind === 'studio') return isPickup ? 'STÜDYO REZERVASYONU · ANAHTAR TESLİMİ' : 'STÜDYO REZERVASYONU · ANAHTAR İADESİ';
        return isPickup ? 'ÇIKIŞ İŞLEMİ' : 'İADE İŞLEMİ';
      })();
      var resAttr = String(item.id || '').replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
      var ridJs = String(item.id || '').replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
      var actId = trafficSafeDomId(item.id);
      var returnStatusHtml = '';
      var pickupStatusHtml = (isPickup && tKind === 'studio') ? trafficStudioPickupStatusSelectHtml(actId) : '';
      var itemsHtml = item.items.map(function(i) {
        var statusStr = String(i.invStatus || '').toUpperCase();
        // Pickup ekranında kalemler seçilebilir olmalı:
        // RESERVED/PENDING gibi ara durumlarda da admin kalemi çıkışa dahil edebilsin.
        // Sadece gerçekten teslime uygun olmayan envanter durumlarını kilitle.
        var pickupBlocked = (
          statusStr === 'IN_USE' || statusStr === 'IN USE' || statusStr === 'KULLANIMDA' || statusStr === 'DIŞARIDA' ||
          statusStr === 'DELETED' || statusStr === 'DAMAGED' || statusStr === 'HIDDEN'
        );
        var isReadyForPickup = isPickup && !pickupBlocked;
        // İade ekranında envanter statüsü sapmış olsa bile kalem seçilebilir olmalı.
        // Aksi halde kartlar silik/disabled kalıp "en az 1 ürün seçin" hatası üretiyor.
        var isReadyForReturn = !isPickup && (statusStr !== 'DELETED' && statusStr !== 'HIDDEN');
        var isCheckable = isReadyForPickup || isReadyForReturn;
        var statusBadge = '';
        if (isReadyForPickup) {
          if (statusStr === 'RESERVED' || statusStr === 'REZERVE') {
            statusBadge = '<span class="text-amber-700 bg-amber-50 px-2 py-0.5 rounded border border-amber-100">Rezerve</span>';
          } else {
            statusBadge = '<span class="text-green-600 bg-green-50 px-2 py-0.5 rounded border border-green-100">Depoda</span>';
          }
        }
        else if (isReadyForReturn) statusBadge = '<span class="text-red-600 bg-red-50 px-2 py-0.5 rounded border border-red-100">Dışarıda</span>';
        else statusBadge = '<span class="text-gray-500 bg-gray-100 px-2 py-0.5 rounded">' + statusStr + '</span>';
        var rawVid = String(i.id || '');
        var vid = rawVid.replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
        var isStudioKeyItem = (i.kind === 'studio_key') || (tKind === 'studio');
        var showCondOut = isPickup && isCheckable && !isStudioKeyItem;
        var coBlock = '';
        if (showCondOut) {
          var coId = 'traffic-co-' + actId + '-' + trafficSafeDomId(rawVid);
          coBlock = '<div class="pl-9 mt-1.5" onclick="event.stopPropagation();">' +
            '<label class="block text-[8px] font-black text-gray-400 uppercase mb-0.5 tracking-wide">Ekipman durumu (çıkış)</label>' +
            '<select id="' + coId + '" class="w-full max-w-xs text-[10px] border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-2 bg-white outline-none focus:border-[#e30613]" onclick="event.stopPropagation();">' +
            '<option value="Excellent" selected>Excellent</option>' +
            '<option value="Minor Scratch">Minor Scratch</option>' +
            '<option value="Missing Part">Missing Part</option>' +
            '<option value="DAMAGED">DAMAGED</option>' +
            '</select></div>';
        }
        var rowName = String(i.name || '').trim();
        if (!rowName || isUuidLike_(rowName)) {
          rowName = isStudioKeyItem ? (String(i.eqCode || '').trim() || 'STUDIO KEY') : 'Ekipman';
        }
        var rowCode = String(i.eqCode || '').trim();
        var returnBlock = '';
        if (!isPickup && isCheckable) {
          var returnKey = String((i && (i.eqId || i.id || i.eqCode || i.reservationId)) || '').trim();
          returnBlock = trafficReturnStatusSelectHtml(actId, tKind, returnKey);
        }
        return '<div class="rounded-lg border border-gray-100 bg-gray-50/50 p-2">' +
          '<label class="flex items-center gap-3 text-xs bg-white p-2 rounded-lg border border-gray-100 ' + (isCheckable ? 'cursor-pointer hover:bg-gray-50' : 'opacity-50') + '">' +
          '<input type="checkbox" ' + (isCheckable ? 'checked' : 'disabled') + ' class="w-4 h-4 text-blue-600 rounded" data-traffic-res="' + resAttr + '" value="' + vid + '">' +
          '<div class="flex-1 font-medium text-gray-800">' + escAdm(rowName) + (rowCode ? (' <span class="text-[9px] text-gray-400 ml-1">(' + escAdm(rowCode) + ')</span>') : '') + '</div>' +
          '<div class="text-[9px] font-bold">' + statusBadge + '</div></label>' + coBlock + returnBlock + '</div>';
      }).join('');
      var mainBtn = isPickup
        ? '<button type="button" onclick="submitPartialCheckout(\'' + ridJs + '\')" class="w-full bg-gray-900 text-white text-[10px] font-bold py-3 rounded-xl hover:bg-black transition shadow-sm">' + (tKind === 'studio' ? '🗝️ ANAHTAR TESLİM ET & STÜDYO FORMU ÜRET' : '📦 ÇIKIŞ YAP & PDF ÜRET') + '</button>'
        : '<button type="button" onclick="submitPartialCheckin(\'' + ridJs + '\')" class="w-full bg-green-600 text-white text-[10px] font-bold py-3 rounded-xl hover:bg-green-700 transition shadow-sm">' + (tKind === 'studio' ? '🗝️ ANAHTAR İADE AL (PDF yok)' : '📥 İADE AL (PDF yok)') + '</button>';
      var extraBtns = isPickup
        ? '<div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 mt-2">' +
          '<button type="button" onclick="adminTrafficCancelAct(\'' + ridJs + '\')" class="bg-white border border-red-100 text-red-700 text-[9px] font-black py-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-red-50">İptal</button>' +
          '<button type="button" onclick="adminTrafficTransferAct(\'' + ridJs + '\')" class="bg-white border border-gray-200 text-gray-800 text-[9px] font-black py-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-gray-50">Devret</button>' +
          '</div>'
        : '<div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 mt-2">' +
          '<button type="button" onclick="adminTrafficExtendAct(\'' + ridJs + '\')" class="bg-white border border-gray-200 text-gray-800 text-[9px] font-black py-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-gray-50">İadeyi uzat</button>' +
          '<button type="button" onclick="adminTrafficTransferAct(\'' + ridJs + '\')" class="bg-white border border-gray-200 text-gray-800 text-[9px] font-black py-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-gray-50">Devret</button>' +
          '</div>';
      var addUi = '';
      if (isPickup) {
        addUi = '<div class="mt-3 bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 rounded-xl p-2.5">' +
          '<p class="text-[9px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">Sepete ürün ekle</p>' +
          '<input id="traffic-extra-q-' + actId + '" type="text" oninput="trafficSearchInventoryForRes(\'' + ridJs + '\', this.value)" class="w-full bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg px-2.5 py-2 text-[11px] outline-none focus:border-[#e30613]" placeholder="Envanter ara: ad veya ID">' +
          '<div id="traffic-extra-search-' + actId + '" class="mt-2 space-y-1"></div>' +
          '</div>';
      }
      var buttonsHtml = '<div class="space-y-1">' + pickupStatusHtml + returnStatusHtml + mainBtn + extraBtns + addUi + '</div>';
      var trafContact = '<p class="text-[9px] text-gray-500 mt-0.5 [overflow-wrap:anywhere] break-words">' + escAdm(item.email || '') + '</p>';
      if (item.phone) trafContact += '<p class="text-[9px] text-gray-600 [overflow-wrap:anywhere] break-words">📞 ' + escAdm(item.phone) + '</p>';
      if (item.studentId) trafContact += '<p class="text-[9px] text-gray-500 [overflow-wrap:anywhere] break-words">🎓 ' + escAdm(item.studentId) + '</p>';
      var studioKeyLine = '';
      var studioPurposeLine = '';
      if (tKind === 'studio') {
        var stItem = (item.items && item.items.length) ? item.items[0] : null;
        var stCanonical = normalizeStudioCanonical_([
          item.studioId,
          item.studioName,
          (stItem && stItem.studioId),
          (stItem && stItem.studioName),
          (stItem && stItem.eqCode),
          (stItem && stItem.name)
        ].join(' '));
        var stNameRaw = String(item.studioName || (stItem && stItem.studioName) || '').trim();
        var stName = (!stNameRaw || isUuidLike_(stNameRaw))
          ? (studioNameFromCanonical_(stCanonical) || 'Stüdyo')
          : stNameRaw;
        var stKeyId = String((stItem && (stItem.eqCode || stItem.name)) || '').trim();
        if (!stKeyId || isUuidLike_(stKeyId)) stKeyId = studioKeyCodeFromCanonical_(stCanonical) || 'STUDIO KEY';
        var stFlow = isPickup ? 'Anahtar Teslimi' : 'Anahtar İadesi';
        studioKeyLine = '<p class="text-[10px] font-black text-indigo-700 mt-1.5">🎬 ' + escAdm(stName) + (stKeyId ? ' · 🔑 ' + escAdm(stKeyId) : '') + ' · ' + stFlow + '</p>';
        if (String(item.purpose || '').trim()) {
          studioPurposeLine = '<p class="text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-700 mt-1 [overflow-wrap:anywhere] break-words">📝 Proje: ' + escAdm(String(item.purpose || '').trim()) + '</p>';
        }
      }
      var handFmt = formatAdminCardDtTr_(item.handoverLabel || '');
      var retFmt = formatAdminCardDtTr_(item.returnLabel || '');
      var trafSched = (item.handoverLabel || item.returnLabel) ? '<p class="text-[11px] md:text-sm text-gray-600 mt-1"><span class="font-black">Teslim:</span> ' + escAdm(handFmt || '—') + ' <span class="font-black">· İade:</span> ' + escAdm(retFmt || '—') + '</p>' : '';
      var topTime = String(item.time || '').trim() || (isPickup ? handFmt : retFmt) || '—';
      container.innerHTML += '<div class="bg-gray-50 p-4 md:p-5 rounded-2xl border-l-8 ' + color + ' shadow-sm border border-gray-200"><div class="flex flex-col md:flex-row md:justify-between md:items-start gap-3 mb-3"><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><h4 class="font-bold text-sm text-gray-900 [overflow-wrap:anywhere] break-words">' + escAdm(item.userName) + '</h4>' + trafContact + studioKeyLine + studioPurposeLine + trafSched + '<span class="text-[9px] font-bold uppercase px-2 py-0.5 rounded ' + badgeColor + ' mt-1 inline-block">' + flowBadge + '</span></div><span class="shrink-0 self-start text-base md:text-lg font-black text-gray-700 bg-white px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md border border-gray-200">' + escAdm(topTime) + '</span></div><div class="space-y-2 mb-3" id="traffic-items-' + actId + '">' + itemsHtml + '</div><div class="mt-1" id="action-container-' + actId + '">' + buttonsHtml + '</div></div>';
      if (isPickup) trafficRenderExtraPicked_(String(item.id || ''));
    });
  }

  function initAdminAuthFromUrl() {
    try {
      var u = new URL(window.location.href);
      var at = (u.searchParams.get('at') || u.searchParams.get('token') || '').trim();
      if (at) {
        currentAuthToken = at;
        try { localStorage.setItem('bookdeck_auth_token', at); } catch (e0) {}
        try { sessionStorage.setItem('bookdeck_auth_token', at); } catch (e00) {}
        try {
          u.searchParams.delete('at');
          u.searchParams.delete('token');
          window.history.replaceState({}, document.title, u.pathname + (u.search ? u.search : '') + (u.hash ? u.hash : ''));
        } catch (_eClean) {}
      } else {
        try { currentAuthToken = localStorage.getItem('bookdeck_auth_token') || sessionStorage.getItem('bookdeck_auth_token') || ''; } catch (e1) { currentAuthToken = ''; }
      }
    } catch (e2) {
      try { currentAuthToken = localStorage.getItem('bookdeck_auth_token') || sessionStorage.getItem('bookdeck_auth_token') || ''; } catch (e3) { currentAuthToken = ''; }
    }
  }

  function getAdminToken_() {
    var t = String(currentAuthToken || '').trim();
    if (t) return t;
    try { t = String(localStorage.getItem('bookdeck_auth_token') || '').trim(); } catch (_eLs) { t = ''; }
    if (!t) {
      try { t = String(sessionStorage.getItem('bookdeck_auth_token') || '').trim(); } catch (_eSs) { t = ''; }
    }
    if (t) currentAuthToken = t;
    return t;
  }

  function ensureAdminToken_() {
    return !!getAdminToken_();
  }

  function buildAdminLoginUrl_() {
    var base = '/admin-login.html';
    var params = [];
    var apiBase = String(API_BASE || '').trim();
    var appBase = String(APP_BASE || '').trim();
    if (apiBase) params.push('api_base=' + encodeURIComponent(apiBase));
    if (appBase) params.push('app_base=' + encodeURIComponent(appBase));
    return params.length ? (base + '?' + params.join('&')) : base;
  }

// ═══ STÜDYO TAKVİM VERİLERİ ═══
  var STUDIO_CALENDARS = {
    'GREEN':   { icon: '🟢', calId: '6b1248a08f65098d73f62263382ed64f7d616887e36ce3d244e8a0169c3236ef@group.calendar.google.com', color: '%230B8043' }, // Yeşil

  var activeAdminStudioId = null;
  var activeAdminStudioName = '';
  var adminStudiosById = {};
  var adminStudioWeekStartIso = '';
  var adminStudioFocusIso = '';
  var adminStudioCalendarMode = 'week'; // week | month
  var adminStudioSelectedSlotKey = '';
  var adminStudioSlotDetailsCache = {};
  var adminStudioEventSelected = null;
  var adminStudioWeekGridInFlight = false;
  var religiousHolidays2026 = ['2026-03-19','2026-03-20','2026-03-21','2026-03-22','2026-05-26','2026-05-27','2026-05-28','2026-05-29','2026-05-30'];
  function isPublicHoliday(date) {
    var d = date instanceof Date ? date : new Date(String(date || ''));
    if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return false;
    var day = d.getDate(), month = d.getMonth() + 1, year = d.getFullYear();
    if (day === 1 && month === 1) return true;
    if (day === 23 && month === 4) return true;
    if (day === 1 && month === 5) return true;
    if (day === 19 && month === 5) return true;
    if (day === 15 && month === 7) return true;
    if (day === 30 && month === 8) return true;
    if (day === 28 && month === 10) return true;
    if (day === 29 && month === 10) return true;
    var ds = year + '-' + String(month).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + String(day).padStart(2, '0');
    return religiousHolidays2026.indexOf(ds) >= 0;
  }

  function applyFrameGuard_() {
    try {
      if (window.top === window.self) return;
      var allowedHosts = ['script.google.com', 'script.googleusercontent.com', 'docs.google.com', 'sites.google.com'];
      var refHost = '';
      try { refHost = document.referrer ? new URL(document.referrer).hostname.toLowerCase() : ''; } catch (eRef) { refHost = ''; }
      if (!refHost) return; // Referrer yoksa sessizce devam.
      var trusted = allowedHosts.some(function(h) { return refHost === h || refHost.endsWith('.' + h); });
      if (trusted) return;
      // Admin tarafinda popup ile bloklamayi kaldirdik; sadece sessiz bayrak.
      window.__bookdeckAdminUntrustedEmbed = true;
    } catch (e) {}
  }

  function bootAdminApp_() {
    initAdminAuthFromUrl();
    if (!ensureAdminToken_()) {
      window.location.replace(buildAdminLoginUrl_());
      return;
    }
    document.getElementById('traffic-date').valueAsDate = new Date();
    fillTimeDropdowns();
    fillStudioTimeDropdowns();
    fillForwardEquipTimeDropdowns();

    var qcPurpose = document.getElementById('qc-purpose');
    var qcPurposeCount = document.getElementById('qc-purpose-count');
    if (qcPurpose && qcPurposeCount) {
      qcPurpose.addEventListener('input', function() {
        qcPurposeCount.innerText = String(qcPurpose.value || '').length;
      });
    }
    var srPurpose = document.getElementById('sr-purpose');
    var srPurposeCount = document.getElementById('sr-purpose-count');
    function syncSrPurposeCount() {
      if (srPurpose && srPurposeCount) srPurposeCount.textContent = String(srPurpose.value || '').length + '/10';
    }
    if (srPurpose) {
      srPurpose.addEventListener('input', syncSrPurposeCount);
      srPurpose.addEventListener('paste', function() { setTimeout(syncSrPurposeCount, 0); });
      syncSrPurposeCount();
    }

    var periodEl = document.getElementById('sr-period');
    if (periodEl) {
      periodEl.addEventListener('change', function() {
        var info = document.getElementById('sr-period-info');
        var text = document.getElementById('sr-period-text');
        var endWrap = document.getElementById('sr-end-period-wrap');
        if (periodEl.value === 'once') { info.classList.add('hidden'); }
        else {
          info.classList.remove('hidden');
          if (periodEl.value === 'daily') text.innerText = '📋 Tekrar bitiş tarihine kadar günlük tekrar.';
          else if (periodEl.value === 'weekly') text.innerText = '📋 Tekrar bitiş tarihine kadar haftalık tekrar.';
          else if (periodEl.value === 'monthly') text.innerText = '📋 Tekrar bitiş tarihine kadar aylık tekrar.';
        }
        if (endWrap) endWrap.classList.toggle('hidden', periodEl.value === 'once');
      });
    }
    var srWithEquip = document.getElementById('sr-with-equip');
    var srEquipWrap = document.getElementById('sr-equip-wrap');
    if (srWithEquip && srEquipWrap) {
      srWithEquip.addEventListener('change', function() {
        srEquipWrap.classList.toggle('hidden', !srWithEquip.checked);
        if (srWithEquip.checked) loadStudioEquipmentAvailability();
      });
    }
    var srEquipQ = document.getElementById('sr-equip-q');
    if (srEquipQ) srEquipQ.addEventListener('input', renderStudioEquipList);
    var srEquipList = document.getElementById('sr-equip-list');
    if (srEquipList) {
      srEquipList.addEventListener('change', function(e) {
        var cb = e.target && e.target.closest ? e.target.closest('.sr-eq-cb') : null;
        if (!cb) return;
        studioEquipSelected[String(cb.getAttribute('data-eqid') || '')] = !!cb.checked;
        renderStudioEquipList();
      });
    }
    var srDateEl = document.getElementById('sr-date');
    var srStartEl = document.getElementById('sr-start');
    var srEndEl = document.getElementById('sr-end');
    [srDateEl, srStartEl, srEndEl].forEach(function(el) {
      if (!el) return;
      el.addEventListener('change', function() {
        if (srWithEquip && srWithEquip.checked) loadStudioEquipmentAvailability();
      });
    });
    // Stüdyo sekmesine hiç geçilmemiş olsa bile placeholder'da takılı kalmasın.
    loadAdminStudios();
    function adminSetCalendarModeUi_() {
      var w = document.getElementById('admin-cal-mode-week');
      var m = document.getElementById('admin-cal-mode-month');
      if (w) {
        w.className = 'px-2 py-1 rounded border text-xs font-bold ' + (adminStudioCalendarMode === 'week' ? 'text-white bg-gray-900 border-gray-900' : 'text-gray-700 hover:bg-white');
      }
      if (m) {
        m.className = 'px-2 py-1 rounded border text-xs font-bold ' + (adminStudioCalendarMode === 'month' ? 'text-white bg-gray-900 border-gray-900' : 'text-gray-700 hover:bg-white');
      }
    }
    var modeWeekBtn = document.getElementById('admin-cal-mode-week');
    if (modeWeekBtn) modeWeekBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      adminStudioCalendarMode = 'week';
      adminSetCalendarModeUi_();
      renderAdminStudioWeekCalendar();
    });
    var modeMonthBtn = document.getElementById('admin-cal-mode-month');
    if (modeMonthBtn) modeMonthBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      adminStudioCalendarMode = 'month';
      adminSetCalendarModeUi_();
      renderAdminStudioWeekCalendar();
    });
    var weekPrevBtn = document.getElementById('admin-week-prev');
    if (weekPrevBtn) weekPrevBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      if (adminStudioCalendarMode === 'month') {
        var d = new Date((adminStudioFocusIso || adminStudioWeekStartIso || mondayIsoFrom_(new Date())) + 'T00:00:00');
        if (isNaN(d.getTime())) d = new Date();
        d.setMonth(d.getMonth() - 1);
        adminStudioFocusIso = d.getFullYear() + '-' + String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '-01';
        adminStudioWeekStartIso = mondayIsoFrom_(d);
      } else {
        adminStudioWeekStartIso = shiftWeekIso_(adminStudioWeekStartIso, -1);
        adminStudioFocusIso = adminStudioWeekStartIso;
      }
      renderAdminStudioWeekCalendar();
    });
    var weekNextBtn = document.getElementById('admin-week-next');
    if (weekNextBtn) weekNextBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      if (adminStudioCalendarMode === 'month') {
        var d = new Date((adminStudioFocusIso || adminStudioWeekStartIso || mondayIsoFrom_(new Date())) + 'T00:00:00');
        if (isNaN(d.getTime())) d = new Date();
        d.setMonth(d.getMonth() + 1);
        adminStudioFocusIso = d.getFullYear() + '-' + String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '-01';
        adminStudioWeekStartIso = mondayIsoFrom_(d);
      } else {
        adminStudioWeekStartIso = shiftWeekIso_(adminStudioWeekStartIso, 1);
        adminStudioFocusIso = adminStudioWeekStartIso;
      }
      renderAdminStudioWeekCalendar();
    });
    adminSetCalendarModeUi_();

    var adminCalFrameEl = document.getElementById('admin-calendar-frame');
    if (adminCalFrameEl) {
      adminCalFrameEl.addEventListener('click', function(ev) {
        var btn = ev.target.closest('.admin-studio-slot');
        if (!btn) return;
        var ck = btn.getAttribute('data-cell-key');
        if (ck) {
          ev.preventDefault();
          var details = adminStudioSlotDetailsCache[ck] || [];
          if (!details.length) return;
          if (details.length === 1) {
            openAdminStudioEventModal(details[0]);
          } else {
            openAdminStudioEventPicker(details);
          }
          return;
        }
        var day = String(btn.getAttribute('data-day') || '');
        var start = String(btn.getAttribute('data-start') || '');
        if (!day || !start) return;
        adminStudioSelectedSlotKey = day + '|' + String((Number(start.split(':')[0]) * 60) + Number(start.split(':')[1] || 0));
        renderAdminStudioWeekCalendar();
        var endMs = new Date(day + 'T' + start + ':00').getTime() + 60 * 60000;
        var e = new Date(endMs);
        var end = String(e.getHours()).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(e.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0');
        var dEl = document.getElementById('sr-date');
        var sEl = document.getElementById('sr-start');
        var eEl = document.getElementById('sr-end');
        if (dEl) dEl.value = day;
        if (sEl) sEl.value = start;
        if (eEl) eEl.value = end;
        showToast('Slot seçildi: ' + day + ' ' + start + ' - ' + end, 'success');
        var form = document.getElementById('admin-studio-form');
        if (form) try { form.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' }); } catch (_e) {}
      });
    }

    var fePeriodEl = document.getElementById('fe-period');
    var feEndWrap = document.getElementById('fe-end-period-wrap');
    if (fePeriodEl && feEndWrap) {
      fePeriodEl.addEventListener('change', function() {
        feEndWrap.classList.toggle('hidden', fePeriodEl.value === 'once');
      });
    }
    ['fe-start-date', 'fe-start-time', 'fe-end-date', 'fe-end-time'].forEach(function(fid) {
      var fel = document.getElementById(fid);
      if (fel) fel.addEventListener('change', updateForwardHolidayWarning_);
    });

    function applyHeaderFromAccess(access) {
      document.getElementById('adminNameDisplay').innerText = access.name || 'Admin';
      document.getElementById('adminRoleDisplay').innerText = access.role || 'Super Admin';
    }
    function applyAdminNavVisibility() {
      var fullOnly = document.querySelectorAll('.nav-full-only');
      var superOnly = document.querySelectorAll('.nav-super-only');
      var navTraffic = document.getElementById('nav-traffic');
      var navIiw = document.getElementById('nav-iiw');
      var i;
      if (adminIsIiwOnly) {
        for (i = 0; i < fullOnly.length; i++) fullOnly[i].classList.add('hidden');
        for (i = 0; i < superOnly.length; i++) superOnly[i].classList.add('hidden');
        if (navTraffic) navTraffic.classList.remove('hidden');
        if (navIiw) navIiw.classList.remove('hidden');
      } else {
        for (i = 0; i < fullOnly.length; i++) fullOnly[i].classList.remove('hidden');
        if (adminIsSuper) {
          for (i = 0; i < superOnly.length; i++) superOnly[i].classList.remove('hidden');
        } else {
          for (i = 0; i < superOnly.length; i++) superOnly[i].classList.add('hidden');
        }
      }
    }
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(acc) {
      adminIsIiwOnly = !!(acc && acc.isIiwPanelOnly);
      adminIsSuper = !!(acc && acc.isSuperAdmin);
      applyAdminNavVisibility();
      if (adminIsIiwOnly) {
        document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item').forEach(function(i) { i.classList.remove('active'); });
        document.querySelectorAll('.view-section').forEach(function(s) { s.classList.remove('active'); });
        var ns = document.getElementById('nav-iiw');
        var ps = document.getElementById('page-iiw');
        if (ns) ns.classList.add('active');
        if (ps) ps.classList.add('active');
      }
    }).checkAdminAccessBridge(currentAuthToken || '');

    if (currentAuthToken) {
      google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(sess) {
        if (sess && sess.ok && sess.user) {
          var u = sess.user;
          document.getElementById('adminNameDisplay').innerText = u.name || sess.email || 'Admin';
          document.getElementById('adminRoleDisplay').innerText = u.role || 'Oturum';
        } else {
          google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(applyHeaderFromAccess).checkAdminAccessBridge(currentAuthToken || '');
        }
      }).withFailureHandler(function() {
        google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(applyHeaderFromAccess).checkAdminAccessBridge(currentAuthToken || '');
      }).authGetSession(currentAuthToken);
    } else {
      google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(applyHeaderFromAccess).checkAdminAccessBridge(currentAuthToken || '');
    }

    // Ağır yükleri ilk açılışta çağırma; sekmeye girince lazy-load.
    checkNewReservations();
    setInterval(checkNewReservations, 60000);
    var uq = document.getElementById('user-lookup-q');
    if (uq) {
      uq.addEventListener('keydown', function(ev) {
        if (ev.key === 'Enter') {
          ev.preventDefault();
          runUserLookup();
        }
      });
      uq.addEventListener('input', function() {
        var v = String(uq.value || '').trim();
        if (userLookupDebounceTimer) clearTimeout(userLookupDebounceTimer);
        if (v.length < 3) return;
        userLookupDebounceTimer = setTimeout(function() { runUserLookup(); }, 260);
      });
    }
  }

  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    applyFrameGuard_();
    checkAdminMaintenance_()
      .then(function(active) {
        if (active) return;
        bootAdminApp_();
      })
      .catch(function() {
        bootAdminApp_();
      });
  });

  function fillTimeDropdowns() {
    var qTime = document.getElementById('qc-return-time');
    if (!qTime) return;
    for (var i = 9; i <= 22; i++) {
      var h = (i < 10 ? '0' + i : String(i));
      qTime.innerHTML += '<option value="' + h + ':00">' + h + ':00</option>';
      qTime.innerHTML += '<option value="' + h + ':30">' + h + ':30</option>';
    }
  }

  function adminIsGreenStudio_(studioId, studioName) {
    var sid = String(studioId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    var sn = String(studioName || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!sn && sid) {
      var meta = adminStudiosById[String(studioId || '').trim()] || null;
      if (meta) sn = String(meta.name || meta.studio_name || meta.code || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    }
    if (!sn && sid && String(studioId || '').trim() === String(activeAdminStudioId || '').trim()) {
      sn = String(activeAdminStudioName || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    }
    return sid === 'GREEN' || sn === 'GREEN' || sn === 'GREEN STUDIO' || sn.indexOf('GREEN') >= 0;
  }

  function fillStudioTimeDropdowns() {
    var startEl = document.getElementById('sr-start');
    var endEl = document.getElementById('sr-end');
    if (!startEl || !endEl) return;
    var isGreen = adminIsGreenStudio_(activeAdminStudioId, activeAdminStudioName);
    var maxStartHour = isGreen ? 21 : 20;
    var maxEndHour = isGreen ? 22 : 21;
    startEl.innerHTML = '';
    endEl.innerHTML = '';
    for (var i = 9; i <= maxStartHour; i++) {
      var h = (i < 10 ? '0' + i : String(i));
      startEl.innerHTML += '<option value="' + h + ':00">' + h + ':00</option>';
      endEl.innerHTML += '<option value="' + h + ':00">' + h + ':00</option>';
    }
    var eh = (maxEndHour < 10 ? '0' + maxEndHour : String(maxEndHour));
    endEl.innerHTML += '<option value="' + eh + ':00">' + eh + ':00</option>';
    startEl.value = '09:00';
    endEl.value = '11:00';
  }

  /** Stüdyo ile aynı: yalnızca tam saatler (09:00–21:00). */
  function fillForwardEquipTimeDropdowns() {
    var startEl = document.getElementById('fe-start-time');
    var endEl = document.getElementById('fe-end-time');
    if (!startEl || !endEl) return;
    startEl.innerHTML = '';
    endEl.innerHTML = '';
    for (var i = 9; i <= 20; i++) {
      var h = (i < 10 ? '0' + i : String(i));
      startEl.innerHTML += '<option value="' + h + ':00">' + h + ':00</option>';
      endEl.innerHTML += '<option value="' + h + ':00">' + h + ':00</option>';
    }
    endEl.innerHTML += '<option value="21:00">21:00</option>';
    startEl.value = '09:00';
    endEl.value = '11:00';
  }

  function showToast(message, type) {
    type = type || 'success';
    var container = document.getElementById('toast-container');
    if (!container) return;
    var toast = document.createElement('div');
    var bgColor = type === 'success' ? 'bg-green-600' : (type === 'error' ? 'bg-red-600' : 'bg-blue-600');
    toast.className = 'transform transition-all duration-300 translate-y-10 opacity-0 flex items-center gap-3 ' + bgColor + ' text-white px-5 py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-2xl font-bold text-sm pointer-events-auto';
    toast.innerHTML = '<span>' + message + '</span>';
    container.appendChild(toast);
    setTimeout(function() { toast.classList.remove('translate-y-10', 'opacity-0'); }, 10);
    setTimeout(function() { toast.classList.add('translate-y-10', 'opacity-0'); setTimeout(function() { toast.remove(); }, 300); }, 4000);
  }

  function goPage(id) {
    var pageEl = document.getElementById('page-' + id);
    var navEl = document.getElementById('nav-' + id);
    if (!pageEl || !navEl) return;
    document.querySelectorAll('.view-section').forEach(function(s) { s.classList.remove('active'); });
    document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item').forEach(function(i) { i.classList.remove('active'); });
    pageEl.classList.add('active');
    navEl.classList.add('active');
    if (id === 'inventory') refreshInventoryData();
    if (id === 'checkout') {
      var qcList = document.getElementById('qc-list');
      if (qcList) qcList.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-full mt-8 text-center text-xs text-gray-400 animate-pulse">Envanter yükleniyor...</div>';
      refreshInventoryData();
    }
    if (id === 'pending') loadPending();
    if (id === 'traffic') loadTraffic();
    if (id === 'history') loadHistory();
    if (id === 'studios') loadAdminStudios();
    if (id === 'forward-equip') loadForwardEquipPage();
    if (id === 'overdue') loadOverdueList();
    if (id === 'penalties') loadPenaltiesAdmin();
    if (id === 'tickets') loadAdminTicketsList();
    if (id === 'bize') loadAdminBizeList();
    if (id === 'reports') loadAdminReports();
    if (id === 'special-access') { loadAdminSpecialAccessList(); loadAdminSpecialEquipmentOptions(); loadAdminSpecialEquipmentAccessList(); }
    if (id === 'iiw') loadIIWAdmin();
  }

  function goToUserAppAsMember() {
    var base = String(APP_BASE || '').split('#')[0];
    var target = base;
    if (currentAuthToken) {
      var sep = base.indexOf('?') >= 0 ? '&' : '?';
      target = base + sep + 'at=' + encodeURIComponent(currentAuthToken);
    }
    try {
      if (window.top && window.top !== window.self) {
        window.top.location.href = target;
        return;
      }
    } catch (_eTopNav) {}
    // Fallback: top erişimi kısıtlıysa aynı frame içinde yönlen.
    window.location.href = target;
  }

  function adminLogout() {
    var t = currentAuthToken;
    function redirectHome() {
      try { localStorage.removeItem('bookdeck_auth_token'); } catch (e) {}
      try { sessionStorage.removeItem('bookdeck_auth_token'); } catch (e2) {}
      currentAuthToken = '';
      var loginUrl = buildAdminLoginUrl_();
      try { window.top.location.href = loginUrl; }
      catch (_eTop) { window.location.href = loginUrl; }
    }
    if (t) {
      google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(redirectHome).withFailureHandler(redirectHome).authLogout(t);
    } else redirectHome();
  }

  function checkNewReservations() {
    if (document.visibilityState === 'hidden') return;
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(count) {
      var badge = document.getElementById('pending-count');
      if (count > 0) {
        badge.innerText = count; badge.classList.remove('hidden');
        if (count > lastPendingCount) try { document.getElementById('notif-sound').play(); } catch(e) {}
      } else badge.classList.add('hidden');
      lastPendingCount = count;
    }).getPendingCount(currentAuthToken);
  }

  function refreshInventoryData(done) {
    var list = document.getElementById('inv-list');
    if (list) list.innerHTML = '<div class="mt-12 text-center text-xs text-gray-400 animate-pulse">Envanter yükleniyor...</div>';
    var token = '';
    try { token = String(currentAuthToken || localStorage.getItem('bookdeck_auth_token') || sessionStorage.getItem('bookdeck_auth_token') || '').trim(); } catch (_eTok) { token = ''; }
    if (!token) {
      if (list) list.innerHTML = '<div class="mt-12 text-center text-xs text-red-500">Oturum bulunamadı. Lütfen tekrar giriş yapın.</div>';
      if (typeof done === 'function') done();
      return;
    }
    adminApiRequest('/equipment-items', { method: 'GET' }).then(function(res) {
      var rows = (res && res.data) ? res.data : [];
      allEq = (rows || []).map(function(r) {
        var itemId = String((r && r.id) || '').trim();
        var itemCode = String((r && r.equipment_id) || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        var status = String((r && r.status) || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        return {
          id: itemId,
          code: itemCode,
          name: String((r && r.name) || itemCode || itemId),
          type: String((r && (r.category || r.type)) || ''),
          photo: String((r && (r.photo_url || r.photo)) || ''),
          status: status,
          isStudioKey: itemCode.indexOf('STUDIO_KEY') === 0,
