          locationText: String((r && (r.location || r.location_text)) || ''),
          responsibleText: String((r && (r.responsible || r.responsible_text)) || '')
        };
      });
      syncInvCategoryButtons();
      filterInventory();
      filterQuickCheckout();
      if (typeof done === 'function') done();
    }).catch(function(err) {
      allEq = [];
      if (list) list.innerHTML = '<div class="mt-12 text-center text-xs text-red-600">Envanter yüklenemedi: ' + escAdm((err && err.message) || 'Bilinmeyen hata') + '</div>';
      showToast((err && err.message) || 'Envanter yüklenemedi.', 'error');
      if (typeof done === 'function') done();
    });
  }

  // ═══ ENVANTER ═══
  function inventoryCategoryForItem_(item) {
    if (!item) return 'CAM';
    if (item.isStudioKey || looksLikeStudioKey_(item.name, item.type, item.code)) return 'KEY';
    var blob = normalizeAdmAscii_([item.type, item.name, item.code].join(' '));
    if (!blob) return 'CAM';
    if (blob.indexOf('light stand') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('lighting stand') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('isik ayagi') >= 0) return 'GRIP';
    if (blob.indexOf('lens') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('optik') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('optic') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('filtre') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('filter') >= 0 || /\bops\b/.test(blob)) return 'LENS';
    if (blob.indexOf('sound') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('ses') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('audio') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('recorder') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('mic') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('mikrofon') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('yaka') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('boom') >= 0) return 'SOUND';
    if (blob.indexOf('grip') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('tripod') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('gimbal') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('stand') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('ayak') >= 0) return 'GRIP';
    if (blob.indexOf('light') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('isik') >= 0 || blob.indexOf('led') >= 0) return 'LIGHT';
    return 'CAM';
  }

  function syncInvCategoryButtons() {
    var current = String(invCategoryFilter || 'CAM').toUpperCase();
    document.querySelectorAll('#inv-category-buttons .inv-cat-btn').forEach(function(btn) {
      var cat = String(btn.getAttribute('data-cat') || '').toUpperCase();
      if (cat === current) {
        btn.classList.remove('bg-white', 'text-gray-700', 'border-gray-200');
        btn.classList.add('bg-[#e30613]', 'text-white', 'border-[#e30613]');
      } else {
        btn.classList.remove('bg-[#e30613]', 'text-white', 'border-[#e30613]');
        btn.classList.add('bg-white', 'text-gray-700', 'border-gray-200');
      }
    });
  }

  function setInvCategoryFilter(cat) {
    var next = String(cat || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    var allowed = { CAM: 1, LENS: 1, SOUND: 1, LIGHT: 1, KEY: 1, GRIP: 1 };
    invCategoryFilter = allowed[next] ? next : 'CAM';
    syncInvCategoryButtons();
    filterInventory();
  }

  function filterInventory() {
    var q = document.getElementById('inv-q').value.toLowerCase();
    var cat = String(invCategoryFilter || 'CAM').toUpperCase();
    var list = document.getElementById('inv-list');
    if (!list) return;
    list.innerHTML = '';
    syncInvCategoryButtons();
    allEq.filter(function(i) {
      var itemCat = inventoryCategoryForItem_(i);
      if (cat && itemCat !== cat) return false;
      var loc = String(i.locationText || '').toLowerCase();
      var resp = String(i.responsibleText || '').toLowerCase();
      var ty = String(i.type || '').toLowerCase();
      var code = String(i.code || '').toLowerCase();
      return (i.name && i.name.toLowerCase().includes(q)) || (code && code.includes(q)) || (ty && ty.includes(q)) || (loc && loc.includes(q)) || (resp && resp.includes(q));
    }).forEach(function(item) {
      var isAvailable = (item.status === 'AVAILABLE');
      var eid = String(item.id || '').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
      var code = String(item.code || item.id || '');
      var photo = String(item.photo || '').trim() || 'https://via.placeholder.com/240x140?text=BUKit';
      list.innerHTML += '<div onclick="showInvDetail(\'' + eid + '\')" class="p-3 bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm cursor-pointer hover:border-[#e30613] transition">' +
        '<div class="relative mb-2 overflow-hidden rounded-xl border border-gray-100 bg-gray-50">' +
          '<img src="' + escAttr(photo) + '" alt="' + escAttr(item.name || code) + '" class="w-full h-24 object-contain bg-white p-1">' +
          '<span class="absolute top-2 right-2 w-2 h-2 rounded-full ' + (isAvailable ? 'bg-green-500' : 'bg-red-500') + '"></span>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<p class="text-[9px] text-gray-500 font-bold uppercase truncate">' + escAdm(item.type || '') + '</p>' +
        '<h3 class="text-xs font-bold text-gray-800 line-clamp-2 min-h-[2rem]">' + escAdm(item.name) + '</h3>' +
        '<p class="mt-1 text-[10px] font-mono text-gray-400 bg-gray-50 px-1.5 py-0.5 inline-block rounded">' + escAdm(code) + '</p>' +
      '</div>';
    });
  }

  function showInvDetail(id) {
    lastInvDetailId = id;
    var panel = document.getElementById('inv-detail-panel');
    panel.innerHTML = '<div class="mt-20 text-center animate-pulse text-gray-400 text-sm font-medium">Yükleniyor...</div>';
    var token = '';
    try { token = String(currentAuthToken || localStorage.getItem('bookdeck_auth_token') || sessionStorage.getItem('bookdeck_auth_token') || '').trim(); } catch (_eTok) { token = ''; }
    if (!token) {
      panel.innerHTML = '<div class="mt-20 text-center text-red-600 text-sm font-medium">Oturum bulunamadı. Lütfen tekrar giriş yapın.</div>';
      return;
    }
    adminApiRequest('/admin/equipment/' + encodeURIComponent(id) + '/detail', { method: 'GET' }).then(function(data) {
      var rawStatus = String(data.status || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      var statusEnNorm = String(data.statusEnglish || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      var isAvailable = (rawStatus === 'AVAILABLE' || statusEnNorm === 'available');
      var isMaintenanceLike =
        rawStatus === 'MAINTENANCE' ||
        rawStatus === 'MAINTANENCE' ||
        rawStatus === 'BROKEN' ||
        rawStatus === 'DAMAGED' ||
        rawStatus === 'HASARLI' ||
        rawStatus === 'BOZUK' ||
        statusEnNorm === 'maintenance' ||
        statusEnNorm === 'damaged';
      var statusBoxClass = isAvailable
        ? 'bg-green-50 border-green-200 text-green-800'
        : (isMaintenanceLike ? 'bg-amber-50 border-amber-200 text-amber-800' : 'bg-red-50 border-red-200 text-red-800');
      var statusLabelTr = isAvailable
        ? 'DEPOLAMADA'
        : (isMaintenanceLike ? 'ARIZALI / BAKIMDA' : 'DIŞARIDA / KULLANIMDA');
      var historyHtml = data.history && data.history.length ? data.history.map(function(h) { return '<div class="py-2 border-b border-gray-50 flex justify-between"><div><p class="text-[11px] font-bold">' + escAdm(h.user) + '</p><p class="text-[9px] text-gray-400">' + escAdm(h.date) + '</p></div><span class="text-[9px] font-bold ' + (String(h.status).includes('Approve') ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-red-600') + '">' + escAdm(h.status) + '</span></div>'; }).join('') : '<p class="text-xs text-gray-400">Kayıt yok.</p>';
      var currentUserHtml = data.currentUser ? '<div class="mt-3 pt-3 border-t border-gray-100"><p class="text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">Şu an / son çıkış</p><p class="text-xs font-bold">👤 ' + escAdm(data.currentUser.name) + '</p><p class="text-xs font-black text-[#e30613] mt-1">Planlanan iade: ' + escAdm(formatAdminDateTimeSlashColon_(data.currentUser.returnDate)) + '</p></div>' : '';
      var prevHtml = data.previousUser && data.previousUser.name ? '<div class="mt-2 text-[10px] text-gray-600"><span class="font-black">Önceki:</span> ' + escAdm(data.previousUser.name) + ' · ' + escAdm(data.previousUser.date) + ' · ' + escAdm(data.previousUser.status) + '</div>' : '';
      var locLine = '<p class="text-[10px] mt-2"><span class="font-black text-gray-500">Konum:</span> ' + escAdm(data.locationPhysical || data.location || '-') + '</p>';
      var respLine = '<p class="text-[10px]"><span class="font-black text-gray-500">Sorumlu:</span> ' + escAdm(data.responsiblePhysical || '-') + '</p>';
      var condLine = '<p class="text-[10px]"><span class="font-black text-gray-500">Kondisyon:</span> ' + escAdm(data.condition || '-') + '</p>';
      var levelLine = '<p class="text-[10px]"><span class="font-black text-gray-500">Seviye:</span> ' + escAdm(data.level || '-') + '</p>';
      var statEn = '<p class="text-[10px]"><span class="font-black text-gray-500">Durum (EN):</span> ' + escAdm(data.statusEnglish || '') + '</p>';
      var editBox = '' +
        '<div class="mt-4 p-4 bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200">' +
          '<div class="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">' +
            '<p class="text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">Envanter Düzenle</p>' +
            '<button type="button" onclick="toggleInvEditPanel()" class="text-[10px] font-black text-[#e30613] hover:underline">Edit</button>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div id="inv-edit-wrap" class="hidden space-y-2">' +
            '<input type="text" id="inv-edit-location" class="w-full text-xs border rounded-lg p-2" placeholder="Konum" value="' + escAttr(data.locationPhysical || '') + '">' +
            '<input type="text" id="inv-edit-responsible" class="w-full text-xs border rounded-lg p-2" placeholder="Sorumlu" value="' + escAttr(data.responsiblePhysical || '') + '">' +
            '<select id="inv-edit-condition-in" class="w-full text-xs border rounded-lg p-2">' +
              '<option value="">Condition In (boş)</option>' +
              '<option value="Excellent"' + ((String(data.conditionIn || '').trim() === 'Excellent') ? ' selected' : '') + '>Excellent</option>' +
              '<option value="Minor Scratch"' + ((String(data.conditionIn || '').trim() === 'Minor Scratch') ? ' selected' : '') + '>Minor Scratch</option>' +
              '<option value="DAMAGED"' + ((String(data.conditionIn || '').trim().toUpperCase() === 'DAMAGED') ? ' selected' : '') + '>DAMAGED</option>' +
            '</select>' +
            '<select id="inv-edit-status" class="w-full text-xs border rounded-lg p-2">' +
              '<option value="">Status (değiştirme)</option>' +
              '<option value="AVAILABLE"' + ((String(data.status || '').toUpperCase() === 'AVAILABLE') ? ' selected' : '') + '>AVAILABLE</option>' +
              '<option value="IN_USE"' + ((String(data.status || '').toUpperCase() === 'IN_USE') ? ' selected' : '') + '>IN_USE</option>' +
              '<option value="BROKEN"' + ((String(data.status || '').toUpperCase() === 'BROKEN') ? ' selected' : '') + '>BROKEN</option>' +
              '<option value="MAINTENANCE"' + ((String(data.status || '').toUpperCase() === 'MAINTENANCE') ? ' selected' : '') + '>MAINTENANCE</option>' +
              '<option value="MAINTANENCE"' + ((String(data.status || '').toUpperCase() === 'MAINTANENCE') ? ' selected' : '') + '>MAINTANENCE</option>' +
            '</select>' +
            '<select id="inv-edit-level" class="w-full text-xs border rounded-lg p-2">' +
              '<option value="">Seviye (değiştirme)</option>' +
              '<option value="1"' + ((String(data.level || '').trim() === '1') ? ' selected' : '') + '>1</option>' +
              '<option value="2"' + ((String(data.level || '').trim() === '2') ? ' selected' : '') + '>2</option>' +
              '<option value="3"' + ((String(data.level || '').trim() === '3') ? ' selected' : '') + '>3</option>' +
              '<option value="4"' + ((String(data.level || '').trim() === '4') ? ' selected' : '') + '>4</option>' +
              '<option value="5"' + ((String(data.level || '').trim() === '5') ? ' selected' : '') + '>5</option>' +
            '</select>' +
            '<button type="button" onclick="saveInvMetaChanges()" class="w-full bg-gray-900 text-white text-[10px] font-black py-2 rounded-lg">Kaydet</button>' +
            '<p id="inv-edit-result" class="text-[10px] text-gray-600"></p>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>';
      var availBox = '<div class="mt-4 p-4 bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200"><p class="text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase mb-2">İleri tarihli müsaitlik</p><div class="grid grid-cols-1 gap-2"><input type="datetime-local" id="inv-avail-start" class="w-full text-xs border rounded-lg p-2"><input type="datetime-local" id="inv-avail-end" class="w-full text-xs border rounded-lg p-2"></div><button type="button" onclick="runInvAvailabilityCheck()" class="mt-2 w-full bg-gray-900 text-white text-[10px] font-black py-2 rounded-lg">Sorgula</button><p id="inv-avail-result" class="text-[10px] mt-2 text-gray-600"></p></div>';
      var canEdit = !!token;
      panel.innerHTML = '<div class="space-y-4"><img src="' + (data.photo || 'https://via.placeholder.com/400x250') + '" class="w-full h-40 object-contain bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border border-gray-100 p-1"><div><p class="text-[10px] font-black text-gray-400 uppercase">' + escAdm(data.type || '') + ' · ' + escAdm(data.equipmentCode || data.id) + '</p><h2 class="text-lg font-black">' + escAdm(data.name) + '</h2></div>' + locLine + respLine + condLine + levelLine + statEn + '<div class="p-4 rounded-2xl border ' + statusBoxClass + '"><p class="text-[9px] font-black uppercase mb-1">Durum</p><p class="text-base font-black uppercase">' + statusLabelTr + '</p>' + currentUserHtml + prevHtml + '</div><div><h3 class="font-black text-[10px] uppercase text-gray-400 mb-2">Son hareketler</h3><div class="bg-white rounded-xl border border-gray-100 p-3 max-h-40 overflow-y-auto">' + historyHtml + '</div></div>' + (canEdit ? (editBox + availBox) : '<p class="text-[11px] text-amber-700 bg-amber-50 border border-amber-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2">Düzenleme ve ileri tarih kontrolü için admin oturumu gerekli.</p>') + '</div>';
    }).catch(function(e) {
      panel.innerHTML = '<div class="mt-20 text-center text-red-600 text-sm font-medium">' + escAdm((e && e.message) || 'Detay yüklenemedi.') + '</div>';
    });
  }

  function toggleInvEditPanel() {
    var el = document.getElementById('inv-edit-wrap');
    if (!el) return;
    el.classList.toggle('hidden');
  }

  function saveInvMetaChanges() {
    if (!lastInvDetailId) return;
    var out = document.getElementById('inv-edit-result');
    var payload = {
      location: document.getElementById('inv-edit-location') ? document.getElementById('inv-edit-location').value.trim() : '',
      responsible: document.getElementById('inv-edit-responsible') ? document.getElementById('inv-edit-responsible').value.trim() : '',
      condition_in: document.getElementById('inv-edit-condition-in') ? document.getElementById('inv-edit-condition-in').value : '',
      status: document.getElementById('inv-edit-status') ? document.getElementById('inv-edit-status').value : '',
      required_level: document.getElementById('inv-edit-level') && document.getElementById('inv-edit-level').value
        ? Number(document.getElementById('inv-edit-level').value)
        : undefined
    };
    if (out) { out.textContent = 'Kaydediliyor...'; out.className = 'text-[10px] text-blue-700'; }
    function onSaveOk() {
      if (out) { out.textContent = 'Kaydedildi.'; out.className = 'text-[10px] text-green-700'; }
      refreshInventoryData();
      showInvDetail(lastInvDetailId);
    }
    function onSaveErr(e) {
      if (out) { out.textContent = (e && e.message) || 'Hata'; out.className = 'text-[10px] text-red-600'; }
    }
    adminApiRequest('/admin/equipment/' + encodeURIComponent(lastInvDetailId) + '/meta', {
      method: 'PATCH',
      body: payload
    }).then(onSaveOk).catch(function(firstErr) {
      // Some edge deployments/proxies block PATCH; retry with POST on same endpoint.
      adminApiRequest('/admin/equipment/' + encodeURIComponent(lastInvDetailId) + '/meta', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: payload
      }).then(onSaveOk).catch(function(secondErr) {
        onSaveErr(secondErr || firstErr);
      });
    });
  }

  function runInvAvailabilityCheck() {
    var id = lastInvDetailId;
    var s = document.getElementById('inv-avail-start');
    var e = document.getElementById('inv-avail-end');
    var out = document.getElementById('inv-avail-result');
    if (!id || !s || !e || !out) return;
    if (!s.value || !e.value) { out.textContent = 'Başlangıç ve bitiş seçin.'; out.className = 'text-[10px] mt-2 text-red-600'; return; }
    if (!ensureAdminToken_()) { out.textContent = 'Oturum jetonu gerekli.'; return; }
    out.textContent = 'Kontrol…';
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) {
      if (r.error) { out.textContent = r.error; out.className = 'text-[10px] mt-2 text-red-600'; return; }
      out.textContent = r.available ? 'Seçilen aralıkta çakışma görünmüyor (müsait).' : ('Çakışma: ' + JSON.stringify(r.conflict || {}));
      out.className = 'text-[10px] mt-2 ' + (r.available ? 'text-green-700' : 'text-amber-800');
    }).adminCheckItemAvailabilityBridge(id, s.value, e.value, currentAuthToken);
  }

  // ═══ HIZLI ÇIKIŞ ═══
  function filterQuickCheckout() {
    var q = document.getElementById('qc-q').value.toLowerCase();
    var list = document.getElementById('qc-list');
    if (!list) return;
    list.innerHTML = '';
    allEq.filter(function(i) {
      var ty = String(i.type || '').toLowerCase();
      var code = String(i.code || '').toLowerCase();
      return (i.name && i.name.toLowerCase().includes(q)) || (code && code.includes(q)) || (ty && ty.includes(q));
    }).forEach(function(item) {
      var isAvailable = (item.status === 'AVAILABLE');
      var eid = String(item.id || '').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
      var tyQc = item.type ? '<p class="text-[9px] text-gray-500 mt-0.5">' + escAdm(item.type) + '</p>' : '';
      list.innerHTML += '<div onclick="' + (isAvailable ? "addToQCCart('" + eid + "')" : '') + '" class="p-4 bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm ' + (isAvailable ? 'cursor-pointer hover:border-[#e30613]' : 'opacity-40') + ' transition"><div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-2"><h3 class="text-xs font-bold ' + (isAvailable ? 'text-gray-800' : 'text-gray-500') + ' pr-2 leading-tight">' + escAdm(item.name) + '</h3>' + (item.isStudioKey ? '<span class="text-[8px] font-black text-amber-700 bg-amber-50 px-1 rounded">ANAHTAR</span>' : '') + '</div><p class="text-[9px] text-gray-400 font-mono">' + escAdm(publicEquipmentId_(item.code, item.id)) + '</p>' + tyQc + '</div>';
    });
  }

  function addToQCCart(id) { if (qcCart.includes(id)) return; qcCart.push(id); renderQCCart(); }
  function removeFromQCCart(id) { qcCart = qcCart.filter(function(i) { return i !== id; }); renderQCCart(); }

  function renderQCCart() {
    var container = document.getElementById('qc-cart');
    container.innerHTML = qcCart.length ? '' : '<p class="text-center text-gray-400 text-xs mt-10 italic">Sepet boş</p>';
    qcCart.forEach(function(id) {
      var item = allEq.find(function(i) { return i.id === id; });
      if (item) container.innerHTML += '<div class="flex justify-between items-center bg-white p-3 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 shadow-sm"><div class="min-w-0"><p class="text-[11px] font-bold truncate text-gray-800">' + item.name + '</p><p class="text-[9px] font-mono text-gray-400">' + publicEquipmentId_(item.code, item.id) + '</p></div><button onclick="removeFromQCCart(\'' + String(id).replace(/'/g, "\\'") + '\')" class="text-red-400 font-bold text-lg px-2">×</button></div>';
    });
  }

  function resolveQuickCheckoutUser() {
    var raw = document.getElementById('qc-user-query');
    var q = raw ? raw.value.trim() : '';
    if (!q) { showToast('Öğrenci no veya e-posta girin.', 'error'); return; }
    adminApiRequest('/admin/lookup-user', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: { query: q }
    }).then(function(lu) {
      if (!lu || !lu.ok) { showToast((lu && lu.error) || 'Çözülemedi', 'error'); return; }
      var em = String(lu.email || '').trim();
      if (!em || em.indexOf('@') < 0) { showToast('E-posta bulunamadı; geçerli e-posta girin veya noyu kontrol edin.', 'error'); return; }
      document.getElementById('qc-resolved-email').value = em;
      var dn = document.getElementById('qc-display-name');
      if (dn && lu.name && !dn.value.trim()) dn.value = lu.name;
      showToast('Kullanıcı: ' + em, 'info');
    }).catch(function(err) { showToast((err && err.message) || 'Hata', 'error'); });
  }

  function submitQuickCheckout() {
    var resolved = document.getElementById('qc-resolved-email');
    var email = (resolved && resolved.value) ? resolved.value.trim() : '';
    if (!email) { showToast('Önce «Çöz» ile e-postayı doğrulayın veya geçerli kayıt girin.', 'error'); return; }
    var date = document.getElementById('qc-return-date').value;
    var time = document.getElementById('qc-return-time').value;
    var displayName = document.getElementById('qc-display-name') ? document.getElementById('qc-display-name').value.trim() : '';
    var projectPurpose = document.getElementById('qc-purpose') ? document.getElementById('qc-purpose').value.trim() : '';
    if (!qcCart.length) { showToast('Sepete ürün ekleyin.', 'error'); return; }
    var fullReturnDate = date ? date + 'T' + time + ':00' : null;
    var actionArea = document.getElementById('qc-action-area');
    actionArea.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center p-4 bg-gray-100 rounded-xl text-blue-600 font-bold text-xs animate-pulse">FORM HAZIRLANIYOR...</div>';
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      showToast('Teslim formu hazır. Yazdırıp «Sonraki işlem» ile sıfırlayın.');
      refreshInventoryData();
      if (!res || !res.url) {
        actionArea.innerHTML = '<button id="qc-btn" onclick="submitQuickCheckout()" class="w-full bg-[#e30613] text-white font-bold py-4 rounded-xl shadow-lg hover:bg-red-700 transition">TESLİM ET VE FORM OLUŞTUR</button>';
        return;
      }
      var src = escAttr(res.url);
      actionArea.innerHTML = '<div class="space-y-3">' +
        '<iframe id="qc-inline-pdf" class="w-full h-[480px] max-h-[55vh] border border-gray-200 rounded-xl bg-gray-100" src="' + src + '"></iframe>' +
        '<div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-2">' +
        '<button type="button" onclick="printQcInlinePdf()" class="flex-1 bg-gray-900 text-white font-black py-3 rounded-xl text-xs hover:bg-black">YAZDIR</button>' +
        '<button type="button" onclick="finishQcInlineReset()" class="flex-1 bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 text-gray-800 font-black py-3 rounded-xl text-xs hover:bg-gray-50">Sonraki işlem (sıfırla)</button>' +
        '</div></div>';
      setTimeout(function() { try { printQcInlinePdf(); } catch (_e) {} }, 600);
    }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      showToast(err.message, "error");
      actionArea.innerHTML = '<button id="qc-btn" onclick="submitQuickCheckout()" class="w-full bg-[#e30613] text-white font-bold py-4 rounded-xl shadow-lg hover:bg-red-700 transition">TESLİM ET VE FORM OLUŞTUR</button>';
    }).processQuickCheckout(qcCart, email, fullReturnDate, displayName, projectPurpose, currentAuthToken);
  }

  function printQcInlinePdf() {
    var f = document.getElementById('qc-inline-pdf');
    try {
      if (f && f.contentWindow) {
        f.contentWindow.focus();
        f.contentWindow.print();
      }
    } catch (e0) { showToast('Yazdırma penceresi açılamadı; PDF üzerinden deneyin.', 'error'); }
  }

  function finishQcInlineReset() {
    qcCart = [];
    renderQCCart();
    var uq = document.getElementById('qc-user-query'); if (uq) uq.value = '';
    var rem = document.getElementById('qc-resolved-email'); if (rem) rem.value = '';
    var dn = document.getElementById('qc-display-name'); if (dn) dn.value = '';
    var pu = document.getElementById('qc-purpose'); if (pu) { pu.value = ''; var cc = document.getElementById('qc-purpose-count'); if (cc) cc.innerText = '0'; }
    var rd = document.getElementById('qc-return-date'); if (rd) rd.value = '';
    var actionArea = document.getElementById('qc-action-area');
    if (actionArea) {
      actionArea.innerHTML = '<button id="qc-btn" onclick="submitQuickCheckout()" class="w-full bg-[#e30613] text-white font-bold py-4 rounded-xl shadow-lg hover:bg-red-700 transition">TESLİM ET VE FORM OLUŞTUR</button>';
    }
    refreshInventoryData();
    showToast('Form sıfırlandı.', 'info');
  }

  // ═══ BEKLEYEN ONAYLAR ═══
  function applyPendingPayloadToUi_(payload) {
    var list = (payload && payload.list) ? payload.list : (Array.isArray(payload) ? payload : []);
    pendingRowsCache = groupPendingRows_(list);
    var dup = (payload && payload.duplicateEqWarnings) ? payload.duplicateEqWarnings : [];
    var ban = document.getElementById('pending-dup-banner');
    if (ban) {
      if (dup && dup.length) {
        ban.classList.remove('hidden');
        ban.innerHTML = '⚠️ <strong>Aynı ekipman birden fazla bekleyen talepte.</strong> Hangisini onaylayacağınıza siz karar verin.<br>' + dup.map(function(d) {
          return '<span class="block mt-1 font-mono">' + escAdm(d.eqId) + ' → Rez: ' + (d.reservationIds || []).map(function(x) { return escAdm(x); }).join(', ') + '</span>';
        }).join('');
      } else {
        ban.classList.add('hidden');
        ban.innerHTML = '';
      }
    }
    filterPendingLocal();
    updatePendingBadgeFromCache_();
  }

  function pendingGroupKey_(row) {
    var r = row || {};
    var kind = String(r.kind || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    if (kind !== 'equipment') return kind + '|' + String(r.id || '');
    return [
      'equipment',
      String(r.email || '').trim().toLowerCase(),
      String(r.userName || '').trim().toLowerCase(),
      String(r.handoverLabel || '').trim(),
      String(r.returnLabel || '').trim(),
      String(r.purpose || '').trim().toLowerCase()
    ].join('|');
  }

  function groupPendingRows_(rows) {
    var src = Array.isArray(rows) ? rows : [];
    var map = {};
    var out = [];
    src.forEach(function(raw) {
      var row = raw || {};
      var key = pendingGroupKey_(row);
      var kind = String(row.kind || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      if (!map[key]) {
        var seed = Object.assign({}, row);
        seed.reservationIds = [String(row.id || '').trim()].filter(Boolean);
        seed.items = [];
        seed.__itemSeen = {};
        map[key] = seed;
        out.push(seed);
      }
      var g = map[key];
      var rid = String(row.id || '').trim();
      if (rid && g.reservationIds.indexOf(rid) < 0) g.reservationIds.push(rid);
      var rowItems = Array.isArray(row.items) ? row.items : [];
      rowItems.forEach(function(it) {
        var eqId = String((it && it.eqId) || '').trim();
        var seenKey = (rid || '') + '|' + (eqId || '');
        if (g.__itemSeen[seenKey]) return;
        g.__itemSeen[seenKey] = true;
        var nextIt = Object.assign({}, it || {});
        nextIt.reservationId = rid || String(nextIt.reservationId || '').trim();
        g.items.push(nextIt);
      });
      if (kind !== 'equipment' && !g.items.length && rowItems.length) g.items = rowItems.slice();
    });
    return out.map(function(g) {
      var cleaned = Object.assign({}, g);
      try { delete cleaned.__itemSeen; } catch (_e) {}
      return cleaned;
    });
  }

  function pendingPruneByReservationIds_(ids) {
    var set = {};
    (Array.isArray(ids) ? ids : []).forEach(function(x) {
      var k = String(x || '').trim();
      if (k) set[k] = true;
    });
    pendingRowsCache = (pendingRowsCache || []).map(function(r) {
      var row = Object.assign({}, r || {});
      var rs = Array.isArray(row.reservationIds) ? row.reservationIds.slice() : [String(row.id || '').trim()].filter(Boolean);
      var kept = rs.filter(function(x) { return !set[String(x || '').trim()]; });
      if (!kept.length) return null;
      row.reservationIds = kept;
      row.id = String(row.id || '').trim() || kept[0];
      if (Array.isArray(row.items)) {
        row.items = row.items.filter(function(it) {
          var rid = String((it && it.reservationId) || '').trim();
          return !rid || kept.indexOf(rid) >= 0;
        });
      }
      return row;
    }).filter(Boolean);
  }

  function updatePendingBadgeFromCache_() {
    var badge = document.getElementById('pending-count');
    if (!badge) return;
    var n = pendingRowsCache.length;
    if (n > 0) {
      badge.innerText = n;
      badge.classList.remove('hidden');
    } else {
      badge.classList.add('hidden');
    }
    lastPendingCount = n;
  }

  /** Sunucudan tam liste; yükleme yazısı yok — onay/red sonrası sessiz senkron için. */
  function reloadPendingSilent() {
    adminApiRequest('/admin/pending').then(function(payload) {
      applyPendingPayloadToUi_(payload);
    }).catch(function() { /* optimistic UI kalsın */ });
  }

  function removePendingFromCacheById_(resId) {
    var id = String(resId || '').trim();
    if (!id) return;
    pendingRowsCache = pendingRowsCache.filter(function(r) { return String(r.id || '').trim() !== id; });
  }

  function loadPending() {
    var container = document.getElementById('pending-cards-container');
    if (!container) return;
    container.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-20 text-gray-400">Yükleniyor...</div>';
    adminApiRequest('/admin/pending').then(function(payload) {
      applyPendingPayloadToUi_(payload);
    }).catch(function(err) {
      container.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-20 text-red-500">' + escAdm((err && err.message) || 'Hata') + '</div>';
    });
  }

  function filterPendingLocal() {
    var container = document.getElementById('pending-cards-container');
    if (!container) return;
    var qEl = document.getElementById('pending-search-q');
    var q = (qEl && qEl.value) ? qEl.value.toLowerCase().trim() : '';
    var data = pendingRowsCache;
    if (q) {
      data = pendingRowsCache.filter(function(res) {
        var blob = (res.userName || '') + ' ' + (res.email || '') + ' ' + (res.phone || '') + ' ' + (res.id || '') + ' ' + (res.handoverLabel || '') + ' ' + (res.returnLabel || '') + ' ' + (res.purpose || '');
        (res.items || []).forEach(function(it) { blob += ' ' + (it.name || '') + ' ' + (it.eqId || '') + ' ' + (it.eqType || ''); });
        return blob.toLowerCase().indexOf(q) >= 0;
      });
    }
    renderPendingCards(data);
  }

  function renderPendingCards(data) {
    var container = document.getElementById('pending-cards-container');
    if (!container) return;
    if (!data || !data.length) {
      container.innerHTML = '<div class="bg-white p-20 text-center rounded-3xl shadow-sm border border-gray-100"><p class="text-gray-400 font-bold">Bekleyen işlem yok.</p></div>';
      return;
    }
    container.innerHTML = '';
    data.forEach(function(res) {
      var pid = String(res.id || '');
      var ridClick = pid.replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
      var ridAttr = pid.replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
      var isStudio = (res.kind === 'studio');
      var stUi = STUDIO_PENDING_UI[String(res.studio_id || '').toUpperCase()] || { border: 'border-indigo-600', bg: 'bg-indigo-50', chip: (res.studio_name ? String(res.studio_name) : 'Stüdyo') };
      var outerClass = isStudio
        ? ('p-6 rounded-3xl border-l-8 ' + stUi.border + ' ' + stUi.bg + ' border border-gray-200 shadow-lg mb-4')
        : 'bg-white p-6 rounded-3xl border border-gray-200 shadow-sm mb-4';
      var studioHdr = isStudio
        ? ('<div class="mb-4 flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2"><span class="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-wider bg-gray-900 text-white px-3 py-1.5 rounded-full">🎬 STÜDYO REZERVASYONU</span><span class="text-[10px] font-black px-2 py-1 rounded-lg border ' + stUi.border + ' bg-white/80">' + escAdm(stUi.chip) + '</span></div>')
        : '';
      var badgeHtml = isStudio
        ? '<span class="text-[10px] font-black bg-indigo-600 text-white px-3 py-1 rounded-full uppercase">Stüdyo · Bekliyor</span>'
        : '<span class="text-[10px] font-black bg-orange-50 text-orange-600 px-3 py-1 rounded-full uppercase">Bekliyor</span>';
      var mergedItems = (function() {
        var base = (res.items || []).slice();
        var extra = pendingExtraItemsByRes[pid] || [];
        var seen = {};
        base.forEach(function(it) { seen[String(it.eqId || '').toUpperCase()] = true; });
        extra.forEach(function(it) {
          var k = String(it.eqId || '').toUpperCase();
          if (!k || seen[k]) return;
          seen[k] = true;
          base.push(it);
        });
        return base;
      })();
      var itemsHtml = mergedItems.map(function(item) {
        var vid = String(item.eqId || '').replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
        var typeLn = item.eqType ? '<span class="text-[10px] text-gray-500 block mt-0.5">' + escAdm(item.eqType) + '</span>' : '';
        var cardName = String(item.name || '').trim();
        if (!cardName || isUuidLike_(cardName)) cardName = 'Ekipman';
        var cardCode = String(item.eqCode || '').trim();
        var codeHtml = cardCode ? ('<span class="text-[10px] text-gray-400 font-mono">' + escAdm(cardCode) + '</span>') : '';
        return '<label class="flex items-center gap-4 text-xs bg-white/90 p-3 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 cursor-pointer hover:bg-gray-50"><input type="checkbox" checked class="w-5 h-5 rounded text-[#e30613]" data-res="' + ridAttr + '" value="' + vid + '"><div class="flex-1"><span class="font-bold text-gray-800 text-sm block">' + escAdm(cardName) + '</span>' + codeHtml + typeLn + '</div></label>';
      }).join('');
      var schedBlock = '';
      if (res.handoverLabel || res.returnLabel) {
        var handoverFmt = formatAdminCardDtTr_(res.handoverLabel);
        var returnFmt = formatAdminCardDtTr_(res.returnLabel);
        schedBlock = '<div class="mt-2 pt-2 border-t border-gray-100/80 text-[10px] text-gray-700 space-y-1"><p><span class="font-black text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wide">Teslim</span> · ' + escAdm(handoverFmt) + '</p><p><span class="font-black text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wide">İade</span> · ' + escAdm(returnFmt) + '</p></div>';
      }
      var phoneLine = res.phone ? '<p class="text-xs text-gray-600 mt-1">📞 ' + escAdm(res.phone) + '</p>' : '';
      var purposeBlock = res.purpose ? '<p class="text-[11px] text-gray-600 mt-2 whitespace-pre-wrap">' + escAdm(res.purpose) + '</p>' : '';
      var pdfU = String(res.studentPdfUrl || '').trim();
      var pdfBtn = (pdfU.indexOf('http') === 0) ? '<button type="button" data-pdf-url="' + escAttr(pdfU) + '" onclick="openAdminStudentPdfFromBtn(this)" class="bg-blue-50 text-blue-700 font-bold py-4 px-4 rounded-xl text-xs border border-blue-200 hover:bg-blue-100 whitespace-nowrap">📄 Öğrenci PDF</button>' : '';
      var actionsRow = '<div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3 flex-wrap">' +
        '<button onclick="approveReservation(\'' + ridClick + '\')" class="flex-1 min-w-[140px] bg-green-600 text-white font-bold py-4 rounded-xl text-xs shadow-md">✅ ONAYLA</button>' +
        (!isStudio ? '<button onclick="pendingAddItemPrompt(\'' + ridClick + '\')" class="bg-gray-900 text-white font-bold py-4 px-4 rounded-xl text-xs">➕ KALEM EKLE</button>' : '') +
        (pdfBtn || '') +
        '<button onclick="rejectReservation(\'' + ridClick + '\')" class="bg-red-50 text-red-600 font-bold py-4 px-6 rounded-xl text-xs border border-red-200">❌ REDDET</button></div>';
      container.innerHTML += '<div class="' + outerClass + '">' + studioHdr + '<div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-4 border-b border-gray-100/80 pb-4"><div><h3 class="font-black text-gray-900 text-lg">' + escAdm(res.userName) + '</h3><p class="text-xs text-gray-400">' + escAdm(res.email) + '</p>' + phoneLine + schedBlock + purposeBlock + '</div>' + badgeHtml + '</div><div class="space-y-2 mb-6">' + itemsHtml + '</div>' + actionsRow + '</div>';
    });
  }

  function approveReservation(resId) {
    var rid = String(resId || '').trim();
    var checks = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('input[data-res]')).filter(function(c) { return c.getAttribute('data-res') === rid && c.checked; }).map(function(c) { return c.value; });
    var row = (pendingRowsCache || []).find(function(r) { return String(r.id || '').trim() === rid; }) || null;
    var isStudioPending = !!(row && row.kind === 'studio');
    if (!checks.length && !isStudioPending) { showToast("En az bir cihaz seçin.", "error"); return; }
    if (!checks.length && isStudioPending) { checks = ['__studio_key__']; }
    showToast("İşlem yapılıyor...", "info");
    var endpoint = (row && row.kind === 'studio')
      ? '/admin/studio-reservations/approve'
      : '/admin/equipment-reservations/approve';
    var rowReservationIds = (row && Array.isArray(row.reservationIds) && row.reservationIds.length)
      ? row.reservationIds.slice()
      : [rid];
    var targetIds = rowReservationIds.slice();
    if (!isStudioPending && row && Array.isArray(row.items) && checks.length) {
      var selected = {};
      checks.forEach(function(x) { selected[String(x || '').trim().toUpperCase()] = true; });
      targetIds = row.items
        .filter(function(it) { return selected[String((it && it.eqId) || '').trim().toUpperCase()]; })
        .map(function(it) { return String((it && it.reservationId) || '').trim(); })
        .filter(Boolean);
      if (!targetIds.length) targetIds = rowReservationIds.slice();
    }
    var uniq = {};
    targetIds = targetIds.filter(function(x) {
      var k = String(x || '').trim();
      if (!k || uniq[k]) return false;
      uniq[k] = true;
      return true;
    });
    Promise.all(targetIds.map(function(oneId) {
      return adminApiRequest(endpoint, { method: 'POST', body: { id: oneId } });
    })).then(function(results) {
      showToast("Onaylandı!");
      var result = (results && results[0]) || null;
      if (result && result.studioFormUrl) window.open(result.studioFormUrl, '_blank');
      pendingPruneByReservationIds_(targetIds);
      filterPendingLocal();
      updatePendingBadgeFromCache_();
      reloadPendingSilent();
      refreshInventoryData();
    }).catch(function(err) { showToast("Hata: " + ((err && err.message) || 'Bilinmeyen hata'), "error"); });
  }

  function pendingAddItemPrompt(resId) {
    openAdminUiDialog({
      title: 'Kalem Ekle',
      desc: 'Equipment ID girin (örn: CAM12). Müsaitse bu bekleyen isteğe eklenir.',
      tone: 'info',
      input: true,
      required: true,
      requiredMessage: 'Equipment ID zorunlu.',
      placeholder: 'Equipment ID',
      okText: 'Ekle'
    }, function(eqIdRaw) {
      var eqId = String(eqIdRaw || '').trim();
      if (!eqId) return;
      google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) {
        if (!r || r.error || !r.item) { showToast((r && r.error) || 'Ekipman bulunamadı.', 'error'); return; }
        if (String(r.item.status || '').toUpperCase() !== 'AVAILABLE') { showToast('Ekipman müsait değil.', 'error'); return; }
        if (!pendingExtraItemsByRes[resId]) pendingExtraItemsByRes[resId] = [];
        var exists = pendingExtraItemsByRes[resId].some(function(x) { return String(x.eqId || '').toUpperCase() === String(r.item.eqId || '').toUpperCase(); });
        if (!exists) pendingExtraItemsByRes[resId].push({ eqId: r.item.eqId, name: r.item.name || r.item.eqId, eqType: r.item.eqType || '' });
        showToast('Kalem eklendi: ' + (r.item.eqId || ''), 'success');
        filterPendingLocal();
      }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
        showToast('Hata: ' + (err && err.message ? err.message : 'Unknown'), 'error');
      }).adminPendingLookupInventoryItem(eqId, currentAuthToken);
    });
  }

  function rejectReservation(resId) {
    document.getElementById('confirm-reason').value = '';
    document.getElementById('confirm-modal').classList.remove('hidden');
    document.getElementById('confirm-action-btn').onclick = function() {
      var reason = (document.getElementById('confirm-reason') && document.getElementById('confirm-reason').value) ? document.getElementById('confirm-reason').value.trim() : '';
      closeConfirmModal();
      showToast("İşlem yapılıyor...", "info");
      var rid = String(resId || '').trim();
      var row = (pendingRowsCache || []).find(function(r) { return String(r.id || '').trim() === rid; }) || null;
      var endpoint = (row && row.kind === 'studio')
        ? '/admin/studio-reservations/reject'
        : '/admin/equipment-reservations/reject';
      var rowReservationIds = (row && Array.isArray(row.reservationIds) && row.reservationIds.length)
        ? row.reservationIds.slice()
        : [rid];
      Promise.all(rowReservationIds.map(function(oneId) {
        return adminApiRequest(endpoint, { method: 'POST', body: { id: oneId, note: reason } });
      })).then(function() {
        showToast("Rezervasyon reddedildi.");
        pendingPruneByReservationIds_(rowReservationIds);
        filterPendingLocal();
        updatePendingBadgeFromCache_();
        reloadPendingSilent();
      }).catch(function(err) { showToast("Hata: " + ((err && err.message) || 'Bilinmeyen hata'), "error"); });
    };
  }

  function closeConfirmModal() {
    document.getElementById('confirm-modal').classList.add('hidden');
  }

  // ═══ GÜNLÜK TRAFİK ═══
  function trafficSelectedEqIds(resId) {
    var selected = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('input[data-traffic-res]')).filter(function(c) {
      return c.getAttribute('data-traffic-res') === resId && c.checked;
    }).map(function(c) { return c.value; });
    var seen = {};
    return selected.filter(function(id) {
      var key = String(id || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      if (!key || seen[key]) return false;
      seen[key] = true;
      return true;
    });
  }

  function groupTrafficRows_(rows) {
    var src = Array.isArray(rows) ? rows : [];
    var out = [];
    var map = {};
    src.forEach(function(raw) {
      var row = raw || {};
      var kindRaw = String(row.kind || row.trafficKind || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      var isStudio = (kindRaw === 'studio' || kindRaw === 'studio_key');
      var rid = String(row.id || '').trim();
      var key = isStudio
        ? ('studio|' + String(row.type || '') + '|' + rid)
        : [
          'equipment',
          String(row.type || '').trim().toLowerCase(),
          String(row.email || '').trim().toLowerCase(),
          String(row.userName || '').trim().toLowerCase(),
          String(row.handoverLabel || '').trim(),
          String(row.returnLabel || '').trim(),
          String(row.purpose || '').trim().toLowerCase()
        ].join('|');
      if (!map[key]) {
        var seed = Object.assign({}, row);
        seed.primaryReservationId = rid;
        seed.reservationIds = rid ? [rid] : [];
        seed.items = [];
        seed.__itemSeen = {};
        map[key] = seed;
        out.push(seed);
      }
      var g = map[key];
      if (rid && g.reservationIds.indexOf(rid) < 0) g.reservationIds.push(rid);
      var items = Array.isArray(row.items) ? row.items : [];
      items.forEach(function(it) {
        var eq = String((it && (it.eqId || it.id || it.eqCode)) || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        var itemRid = String((it && it.reservationId) || rid || '').trim();
        var seenKey = itemRid + '|' + eq;
        if (g.__itemSeen[seenKey]) return;
        g.__itemSeen[seenKey] = true;
        var nextIt = Object.assign({}, it || {});
        nextIt.reservationId = itemRid;
        g.items.push(nextIt);
      });
    });
    return out.map(function(g) {
      var cleaned = Object.assign({}, g);
      try { delete cleaned.__itemSeen; } catch (_e) {}
      return cleaned;
    });
  }

  function trafficSelectedReservationIds_(resId) {
    var rid = String(resId || '').trim();
    var row = (trafficAllRows || []).find(function(x) { return String((x && x.id) || '') === rid; }) || null;
    if (!row) return rid ? [rid] : [];
    var selectedEq = trafficSelectedEqIds(rid).map(function(x) { return String(x || '').trim().toUpperCase(); });
    var baseIds = (Array.isArray(row.reservationIds) && row.reservationIds.length)
      ? row.reservationIds.slice()
      : [String(row.primaryReservationId || row.id || '').trim()].filter(Boolean);
    if (!selectedEq.length) return baseIds;
    var selSet = {};
    selectedEq.forEach(function(x) { selSet[x] = true; });
    var chosen = [];
    (row.items || []).forEach(function(it) {
      var eq = String((it && (it.eqId || it.id || it.eqCode)) || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      if (!selSet[eq]) return;
      var oneId = String((it && it.reservationId) || '').trim();
      if (oneId) chosen.push(oneId);
    });
    if (!chosen.length) return baseIds;
    var seen = {};
    return chosen.filter(function(x) {
      var k = String(x || '').trim();
      if (!k || seen[k]) return false;
      seen[k] = true;
      return true;
    });
  }

  function trafficPrimaryReservationId_(resId) {
    var rid = String(resId || '').trim();
    var row = (trafficAllRows || []).find(function(x) { return String((x && x.id) || '') === rid; }) || null;
    if (!row) return rid;
    return String(row.primaryReservationId || row.id || rid).trim();
  }

  function trafficEnsureInventoryLoaded_(done) {
    if (Array.isArray(allEq) && allEq.length) { done(); return; }
    refreshInventoryData(function() { done(); });
  }

  function trafficNormalizeConditionOut_(v) {
    var s = String(v || '').trim();
    if (!s) return 'Excellent';
    if (s === 'Excellent' || s === 'Minor Scratch' || s === 'Missing Part' || s === 'DAMAGED' || s === 'Damaged') {
      return (s === 'Damaged') ? 'DAMAGED' : s;
    }
    var low = s.toLowerCase();
    if (low.indexOf('minor') >= 0 && low.indexOf('scratch') >= 0) return 'Minor Scratch';
    if (low.indexOf('missing') >= 0) return 'Missing Part';
    if (low.indexOf('damage') >= 0 || low.indexOf('hasar') >= 0) return 'DAMAGED';
    return 'Excellent';
  }

  function trafficAddExtraItem(resId, itemId, itemName, defaultConditionOut) {
    var rid = String(resId || '').trim();
    var iid = String(itemId || '').trim();
    if (!rid || !iid) return;
    if (!trafficExtraByRes[rid]) trafficExtraByRes[rid] = [];
    var arr = trafficExtraByRes[rid];
    if (arr.some(function(x) { return String(x.id || '').toUpperCase() === iid.toUpperCase(); })) return;
    arr.push({
      id: iid,
      name: String(itemName || iid).trim(),
      conditionOut: trafficNormalizeConditionOut_(defaultConditionOut)
    });
    var q = document.getElementById('traffic-extra-q-' + trafficSafeDomId(rid));
    if (q) q.value = '';
    trafficRenderExtraPicked_(rid);
    trafficSearchInventoryForRes(rid, '');
  }

  function trafficRemoveExtraItem(resId, itemId) {
    var rid = String(resId || '').trim();
    var iid = String(itemId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!rid || !iid || !trafficExtraByRes[rid]) return;
    trafficExtraByRes[rid] = trafficExtraByRes[rid].filter(function(x) { return String(x.id || '').trim().toUpperCase() !== iid; });
    trafficRenderExtraPicked_(rid);
  }

  function trafficRenderExtraPicked_(resId) {
    var rid = String(resId || '').trim();
    var actId = trafficSafeDomId(rid);
    var box = document.getElementById('traffic-items-' + actId);
    if (!box) return;
    var arr = trafficExtraByRes[rid] || [];
    Array.from(box.querySelectorAll('[data-traffic-extra-row="1"]')).forEach(function(n) {
      if (n && n.parentNode) n.parentNode.removeChild(n);
    });
    if (!arr.length) return;
    var resAttr = rid.replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
    arr.forEach(function(it) {
      var id = String(it.id || '').trim();
      var nm = String(it.name || id).trim();
      var ridJs = rid.replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
      var idJs = id.replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
      var idAttr = id.replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
      var coId = 'traffic-co-' + actId + '-' + trafficSafeDomId(id);
      var condSel = trafficNormalizeConditionOut_(it.conditionOut || it.condition || it.condition_in || it.conditionIn || it.lastCondition || '');
      box.innerHTML += '<div data-traffic-extra-row="1" class="rounded-lg border border-[#e30613]/20 bg-red-50/40 p-2">' +
        '<label class="flex items-center gap-3 text-xs bg-white p-2 rounded-lg border border-red-100 cursor-pointer hover:bg-gray-50">' +
        '<input type="checkbox" checked class="w-4 h-4 text-blue-600 rounded" data-traffic-res="' + resAttr + '" value="' + idAttr + '">' +
        '<div class="flex-1 font-medium text-gray-800">' + escAdm(nm) + ' <span class="text-[9px] text-gray-400 ml-1">(' + escAdm(id) + ')</span></div>' +
        '<div class="text-[9px] font-black text-[#e30613]">EK</div></label>' +
        '<div class="pl-7 pt-1.5">' +
        '<label class="block text-[8px] font-black text-gray-400 uppercase mb-0.5 tracking-wide">Ekipman durumu (çıkış)</label>' +
        '<select id="' + coId + '" class="w-full max-w-xs text-[10px] border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-2 bg-white outline-none focus:border-[#e30613]">' +
        '<option value="Excellent"' + (condSel === 'Excellent' ? ' selected' : '') + '>Excellent</option>' +
        '<option value="Minor Scratch"' + (condSel === 'Minor Scratch' ? ' selected' : '') + '>Minor Scratch</option>' +
        '<option value="Missing Part"' + (condSel === 'Missing Part' ? ' selected' : '') + '>Missing Part</option>' +
        '<option value="DAMAGED"' + (condSel === 'DAMAGED' ? ' selected' : '') + '>DAMAGED</option>' +
        '</select></div>' +
        '<div class="pl-7 pt-1"><button type="button" onclick="trafficRemoveExtraItem(\'' + ridJs + '\',\'' + idJs + '\')" class="text-red-600 text-[10px] font-black px-1">Çıkar</button></div>' +
        '</div>';
    });
  }

  function trafficSearchInventoryForRes(resId, q) {
    var rid = String(resId || '').trim();
    var box = document.getElementById('traffic-extra-search-' + trafficSafeDomId(rid));
    if (!box) return;
    var needle = String(q || '').toLowerCase().trim();
    if (needle.length < 2) { box.innerHTML = ''; return; }
    trafficEnsureInventoryLoaded_(function() {
      var existing = {};
      Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('input[data-traffic-res]')).forEach(function(c) {
        if (c.getAttribute('data-traffic-res') === rid) existing[String(c.value || '').trim().toUpperCase()] = true;
      });
      (trafficExtraByRes[rid] || []).forEach(function(it) { existing[String(it.id || '').trim().toUpperCase()] = true; });
      var rows = (allEq || []).filter(function(it) {
        if (!it || it.isStudioKey) return false;
        var id = String(it.id || '').trim();
        if (!id || existing[id.toUpperCase()]) return false;
        var st = String(it.status || '').toUpperCase();
        if (!(st === 'AVAILABLE' || st === 'MÜSAİT' || st === 'UYGUN')) return false;
        var blob = (String(it.name || '') + ' ' + String(it.code || id) + ' ' + String(it.type || it.type_desc || '')).toLowerCase();
        return blob.indexOf(needle) >= 0;
      }).slice(0, 12);
      if (!rows.length) {
        box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-[10px] text-gray-400">Sonuç yok.</p>';
        return;
      }
      var ridJs = rid.replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
      box.innerHTML = rows.map(function(it) {
        var id = String(it.id || '').trim();
        var nm = String(it.name || id).trim();
        var idJs = id.replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
        var nmJs = nm.replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
        var condGuess = trafficNormalizeConditionOut_(it.conditionOut || it.condition || it.condition_in || it.conditionIn || it.lastCondition || '');
        return '<button type="button" onclick="trafficAddExtraItem(\'' + ridJs + '\',\'' + idJs + '\',\'' + nmJs + '\',\'' + condGuess + '\')" class="w-full text-left bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg px-2 py-1.5 hover:border-[#e30613]">' +
          '<p class="text-[10px] font-semibold text-gray-800 truncate">' + escAdm(nm) + '</p><p class="text-[9px] font-mono text-gray-400">' + escAdm(it.code || id) + '</p></button>';
      }).join('');
    });
  }

  function trafficActionContainer(resId) {
    return document.getElementById('action-container-' + trafficSafeDomId(resId));
  }

  function trafficPickedUpToastText_(resId) {
    var rid = String(resId || '').trim();
    if (!rid) return 'PICKED UP';
    var row = (trafficAllRows || []).find(function(x) { return String(x.id || '') === rid && String(x.type || '') === 'pickup'; })
      || (trafficAllRows || []).find(function(x) { return String(x.id || '') === rid; });
    if (!row) return 'PICKED UP';
    var kindRaw = String(row.kind || row.trafficKind || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    if (kindRaw === 'studio' || kindRaw === 'studio_key') {
      var first = (row.items && row.items.length) ? row.items[0] : null;
      var keyCode = String((first && (first.eqCode || first.name)) || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      if (!keyCode) keyCode = 'GKEY';
      return keyCode + ' PICKED UP';
    }
    return 'PICKED UP';
  }

  function trafficDropPickedUpRows_(resId) {
    var rid = String(resId || '').trim();
    if (!rid) return false;
    var before = (trafficAllRows || []).length;
    trafficAllRows = (trafficAllRows || []).filter(function(x) {
      return !(String(x.id || '') === rid && String(x.type || '') === 'pickup');
    });
    return before !== (trafficAllRows || []).length;
  }

  function loadTraffic() {
    var date = document.getElementById('traffic-date').value;
    var container = document.getElementById('traffic-container');
    if (!container) return;
    container.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-2 text-center py-10 text-gray-400">Yükleniyor...</div>';
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
      trafficSearchMode = 'daily';
      trafficGlobalQuery = '';
      trafficAllRows = groupTrafficRows_(data || []);
      renderTrafficFromCache();
    }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      container.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-2 text-center py-10 text-red-500">Veri alınamadı: ' + escAdm((err && err.message) || 'Bilinmeyen hata') + '</div>';
    }).getTrafficData(date, currentAuthToken);
  }

  function loadTrafficByQuery(qNorm) {
    var container = document.getElementById('traffic-container');
    if (!container) return;
    if (trafficSearchTimer) clearTimeout(trafficSearchTimer);
    trafficSearchTimer = setTimeout(function() {
      trafficSearchTimer = null;
      container.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-2 text-center py-10 text-gray-400">Genel arama yapılıyor…</div>';
      google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
        trafficSearchMode = 'global';
        trafficGlobalQuery = String(qNorm || '');
        trafficAllRows = groupTrafficRows_(data || []);
        renderTrafficFromCache();
      }).withFailureHandler(function() {
        container.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-2 text-center py-10 text-red-500">Arama sırasında hata oluştu.</div>';
      }).getTrafficDataByNameOrStudent(qNorm, currentAuthToken);
    }, 220);
  }

  function adminTrafficPdfAct(resId) {
    var checks = trafficSelectedEqIds(resId);
    if (!checks.length) { showToast('En az bir kalem seçin.', 'error'); return; }
    var primaryId = trafficPrimaryReservationId_(resId);
    openAdminUiDialog({
      title: 'PDF Notu',
      desc: 'Stüdyo anahtar teslim notu (opsiyonel).',
      tone: 'info',
      input: true,
      required: false,
      placeholder: 'Not (boş bırakılabilir)',
      okText: 'PDF Oluştur'
    }, function(note) {
      var container = trafficActionContainer(resId);
      if (!container) return;
      var oldContent = container.innerHTML;
      container.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center p-2 text-[10px] font-bold text-blue-600 animate-pulse">PDF…</div>';
      google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) {
        if (r && r.success) {
          if (r.url) {
            openAdminStudentPdfView(r.url);
            showToast('PDF hazır. Modalda önizleyebilir veya yazdırabilirsiniz.', 'info');
          }
          container.innerHTML = oldContent;
          refreshInventoryData();
          loadTraffic();
        } else { container.innerHTML = oldContent; showToast((r && r.error) || 'Hata', 'error'); }
      }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { container.innerHTML = oldContent; showToast(err.message, 'error'); }).adminTrafficPrintPdf(primaryId, checks, note || '', trafficCheckoutConditionOutMap(resId, checks), currentAuthToken);
    });
  }

  function adminTrafficExtendAct(resId) {
    var checks = trafficSelectedEqIds(resId);
    if (!checks.length) { showToast('Kalem seçin.', 'error'); return; }
    var targetIds = trafficSelectedReservationIds_(resId);
    var rid = String(resId || '').trim();
    var row = (trafficAllRows || []).find(function(x) { return String(x.id || '') === rid && String(x.type || '').toLowerCase() === 'return'; })
      || (trafficAllRows || []).find(function(x) { return String(x.id || '') === rid; })
      || null;
    var seed = splitRawIsoDateTime_((row && (row.returnLabel || row.time)) || '');
    openAdminUiDialog({
      title: 'Yeni İade Zamanı',
      desc: 'Yeni iade tarihini ve saatini seçin.',
      tone: 'warning',
      input: true,
      inputMode: 'datetime_split',
      required: true,
      requiredMessage: 'Yeni iade tarihi ve saati zorunlu.',
      defaultDate: seed.date,
      defaultTime: seed.time,
      okText: 'Güncelle'
    }, function(nd) {
      Promise.all(targetIds.map(function(oneId) {
        return adminApiRequest('/admin/traffic/extend', {
          method: 'POST',
          body: { id: String(oneId || '').trim(), new_end_at: String(nd || '').trim() }
        });
      })).then(function() {
        showToast('Güncellendi');
        loadTraffic();
      }).catch(function(err) {
        showToast((err && err.message) || 'Hata', 'error');
      });
    });
  }

  function adminTrafficCancelAct(resId) {
    var checks = trafficSelectedEqIds(resId);
    if (!checks.length) { showToast('Kalem seçin.', 'error'); return; }
    var targetIds = trafficSelectedReservationIds_(resId);
    openAdminUiDialog({
      title: 'Kalemleri İptal Et',
      desc: 'Seçilen rezervasyon kalemleri iptal edilecek. Devam edilsin mi?',
      tone: 'danger',
      input: false,
      okText: 'İptal Et'
    }, function() {
      Promise.all(targetIds.map(function(oneId) {
        return adminApiRequest('/admin/traffic/cancel', {
          method: 'POST',
          body: { id: String(oneId || '').trim() }
        });
      })).then(function() {
        showToast('İptal edildi');
        loadTraffic();
        refreshInventoryData();
      }).catch(function(err) {
        showToast((err && err.message) || 'Hata', 'error');
      });
    });
  }

  function adminTrafficTransferAct(resId) {
    var checks = trafficSelectedEqIds(resId);
    if (!checks.length) { showToast('Kalem seçin.', 'error'); return; }
    var targetIds = trafficSelectedReservationIds_(resId);
    openAdminUiDialog({
      title: 'Rezervasyonu Devret',

      required: true,

        });
      })).then(function() {

      }).catch(function(err) {
        showToast((err && err.message) || 'Hata', 'error');
      });

  }

  function submitPartialCheckout(resId) {
    var checks = trafficSelectedEqIds(resId);
    if (!checks.length) { showToast("Çıkış yapmak için en az bir cihaz seçin.", "error"); return; }
    var primaryId = trafficPrimaryReservationId_(resId);
    var meta = trafficMetaByResId[String(resId || '')] || {};
    var studioHandoverNote = '';
    if (meta.kind === 'studio') {
      var actId = trafficSafeDomId(resId);
      var sel = document.getElementById('traffic-pickup-status-' + actId);
      studioHandoverNote = sel ? String(sel.value || '').trim() : '';
      if (!studioHandoverNote) {
        showToast("Teslim durumunu seçin.", "error");
        return;
      }
    }
    var container = trafficActionContainer(resId);
    if (!container) return;
    var oldContent = container.innerHTML;
    container.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center p-3 text-xs font-bold text-blue-600 animate-pulse">PDF Hazırlanıyor...</div>';
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) {
      if (r.success) {
        showToast(trafficPickedUpToastText_(resId));
        trafficDropPickedUpRows_(resId);
        renderTrafficFromCache();
        if (r.url) {
          openAdminStudentPdfView(r.url);
          setTimeout(function() { loadTraffic(); }, 500);
        } else {
          loadTraffic();
        }
        refreshInventoryData();
      } else { container.innerHTML = oldContent; showToast("Hata: " + r.error, "error"); }
    }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { container.innerHTML = oldContent; showToast("Sistem Hatası: " + err.message, "error"); }).adminProcessPartialCheckout(primaryId, checks, studioHandoverNote, trafficCheckoutConditionOutMap(resId, checks), currentAuthToken);
  }

  function submitPartialCheckin(resId) {
    var checks = trafficSelectedEqIds(resId);
    if (!checks.length) { showToast("İade almak için en az bir cihaz seçin.", "error"); return; }
    var selectedEqSet = {};
    checks.forEach(function(eqId) { selectedEqSet[String(eqId || '').trim().toUpperCase()] = true; });
    var rid = String(resId || '').trim();
    var row = (trafficAllRows || []).find(function(x) { return String((x && x.id) || '') === rid; }) || null;
    var targetIds = trafficSelectedReservationIds_(resId);
    var actId = trafficSafeDomId(resId);
    var handoverByResId = {};
    var missing = [];
    (row && row.items ? row.items : []).forEach(function(it) {
      var eq = String((it && (it.eqId || it.id || it.eqCode)) || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      if (!eq || !selectedEqSet[eq]) return;
      var oneResId = String((it && it.reservationId) || '').trim();
      if (!oneResId) return;
      var itemKey = String((it && (it.eqId || it.id || it.eqCode || it.reservationId)) || '').trim();
      var sel = document.getElementById('traffic-return-status-' + actId + '-' + trafficSafeDomId(itemKey));
      var v = sel ? String(sel.value || '').trim() : '';
      if (!v) {
        missing.push(itemKey || eq || oneResId);
        return;
      }
      handoverByResId[oneResId] = v;
    });
    if (missing.length) { showToast('Seçili her ürün için iade teslim durumu seçin.', 'error'); return; }
    var container = trafficActionContainer(resId);
    if (!container) return;
    var oldContent = container.innerHTML;
    container.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center p-3 text-xs font-bold text-green-600 animate-pulse">İade İşleniyor...</div>';
    Promise.all(targetIds.map(function(oneId) {
      var handover = String(handoverByResId[String(oneId || '').trim()] || '').trim();
      if (!handover) {
        var first = Object.keys(handoverByResId || {})[0];
        handover = first ? String(handoverByResId[first] || '').trim() : '';
      }
      return adminApiRequest('/admin/traffic/checkin', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: { id: String(oneId || '').trim(), studio_handover_note: String(handover || '').trim() }
      });
    })).then(function() {
      showToast("İade Alındı!");
      loadTraffic();
      refreshInventoryData();
    }).catch(function(err) {
      container.innerHTML = oldContent;
      showToast("Sistem Hatası: " + ((err && err.message) || 'Hata'), "error");
    });
  }

  // ═══ STÜDYO TAKVİMİ ═══
  function loadAdminStudios() {
    var container = document.getElementById('admin-studio-selector');
    if (container) container.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-full text-center text-gray-400 animate-pulse py-4 text-xs">Stüdyolar yükleniyor...</div>';
    adminApiRequest('/studios', { method: 'GET' }).then(function(payload) {
      var studios = (payload && payload.data) ? payload.data : [];
      var container = document.getElementById('admin-studio-selector');
      if (!container) return;
      if (!studios || !studios.length) { container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400 col-span-full text-center py-4">Stüdyo bulunamadı.</p>'; return; }
      adminStudiosById = {};
      (studios || []).forEach(function(s0) {
        var sid0 = String((s0 && s0.id) || '').trim();
        if (sid0) adminStudiosById[sid0] = s0;
      });
      populateStudioLockStudioSelect_(studios);
      container.innerHTML = '';
      studios.forEach(function(s) {
        var calData = STUDIO_CALENDARS[s.id] || { icon: '🎬' };
        var isActive = (activeAdminStudioId === s.id);
        var activeClass = isActive ? 'border-[#e30613] bg-red-50 ring-2 ring-[#e30613] ring-opacity-30' : 'border-gray-200 bg-white hover:border-gray-300 hover:shadow-md';
        var sidJs = String(s.id || '').replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
        var snameJs = String(s.name || '').replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
        container.innerHTML += '<div onclick="selectAdminStudio(\'' + sidJs + '\', \'' + snameJs + '\')" class="cursor-pointer rounded-2xl border-2 ' + activeClass + ' p-4 text-center transition-all"><span class="text-2xl block mb-2">' + calData.icon + '</span><h4 class="font-black text-xs text-gray-900">' + escAdm(s.name) + '</h4>' + (isActive ? '<span class="text-[8px] font-bold text-[#e30613] uppercase mt-1 block">Seçili</span>' : '') + '</div>';
      });
    }).catch(function(err) {
      var container = document.getElementById('admin-studio-selector');
      if (container) container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-500 col-span-full text-center py-4">' + escAdm((err && err.message) || 'Stüdyo listesi alınamadı.') + '</p>';
    });
  }

  function selectAdminStudio(id, name) {
    activeAdminStudioId = id;
    activeAdminStudioName = String(name || '');
    var calData = STUDIO_CALENDARS[id] || { icon: '🎬', calId: '' };
    loadAdminStudios();
    var calWrapper = document.getElementById('admin-calendar-wrapper');
    calWrapper.classList.remove('hidden');
    document.getElementById('cal-studio-name').innerText = name;
    document.getElementById('cal-studio-icon').innerText = calData.icon;
    if (!adminStudioWeekStartIso) adminStudioWeekStartIso = mondayIsoFrom_(new Date());
    if (!adminStudioFocusIso) adminStudioFocusIso = adminStudioWeekStartIso;
    renderAdminStudioWeekCalendar();
    var form = document.getElementById('admin-studio-form');
    form.classList.remove('hidden');
    document.getElementById('form-studio-name').innerText = name;
    fillStudioTimeDropdowns();
    var lockStudioEl = document.getElementById('sl-studio-id');
    if (lockStudioEl) lockStudioEl.value = String(id || '');
    setTimeout(function() { calWrapper.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' }); }, 200);
  }

  function populateStudioLockStudioSelect_(studios) {
    var sel = document.getElementById('sl-studio-id');
    if (!sel) return;
    var current = String(sel.value || '');
    sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Stüdyo seçin</option>';
    (studios || []).forEach(function(s) {
      var sid = String((s && s.id) || '').trim();
      var sname = String((s && s.name) || sid || '').trim();
      if (!sid) return;
      sel.innerHTML += '<option value="' + escAttr(sid) + '">' + escAdm(sname) + '</option>';
    });
    if (current && sel.querySelector('option[value="' + current + '"]')) sel.value = current;
    else if (activeAdminStudioId && sel.querySelector('option[value="' + String(activeAdminStudioId) + '"]')) sel.value = String(activeAdminStudioId);
  }

  function submitStudioLockRange() {
    var studioId = String((document.getElementById('sl-studio-id') || {}).value || '').trim();
    var reason = String((document.getElementById('sl-reason') || {}).value || '').trim();
    var startDate = String((document.getElementById('sl-start-date') || {}).value || '').trim();
    var endDate = String((document.getElementById('sl-end-date') || {}).value || '').trim();
    if (!studioId) { showToast('Stüdyo seçin.', 'error'); return; }
    if (!reason) { showToast('Kilitleme nedeni zorunlu.', 'error'); return; }
    if (!startDate || !endDate) { showToast('Başlangıç ve bitiş günlerini girin.', 'error'); return; }
    if (endDate < startDate) { showToast('Bitiş günü başlangıçtan önce olamaz.', 'error'); return; }
    var btn = document.getElementById('sl-submit-btn');
    var old = btn ? btn.innerText : '';
    if (btn) { btn.disabled = true; btn.innerText = 'KİLİTLENİYOR...'; }
    adminApiRequest('/admin/studio-locks', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: { studio_id: studioId, reason: reason, start_date: startDate, end_date: endDate }
    }).then(function(res) {
      if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.innerText = old || 'STÜDYOYU KİLİTLE'; }
      var sync = res && res.calendar_sync ? res.calendar_sync : null;
      if (sync && sync.ok === false) {
        showToast('Kilit kaydedildi; Google Takvim senkronu atlandı (' + String(sync.skipped || 'unknown') + ').', 'info');
      } else {
        showToast('Stüdyo takvimi kilitlendi.', 'success');
      }
      if (String(activeAdminStudioId || '') !== String(studioId || '')) {
        var st = adminStudiosById[String(studioId || '').trim()] || null;
        selectAdminStudio(studioId, String((st && st.name) || studioId));
      } else {
        renderAdminStudioWeekCalendar();
      }
    }).catch(function(err) {
      if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.innerText = old || 'STÜDYOYU KİLİTLE'; }
      showToast('Hata: ' + ((err && err.message) || 'Bilinmeyen hata'), 'error');
    });
  }

  function submitStudioUnlockRange() {
    var studioId = String((document.getElementById('sl-studio-id') || {}).value || '').trim();
    var reason = String((document.getElementById('sl-reason') || {}).value || '').trim();
    var startDate = String((document.getElementById('sl-start-date') || {}).value || '').trim();
    var endDate = String((document.getElementById('sl-end-date') || {}).value || '').trim();
    if (!studioId) { showToast('Stüdyo seçin.', 'error'); return; }
    if (!startDate || !endDate) { showToast('Başlangıç ve bitiş günlerini girin.', 'error'); return; }
    if (endDate < startDate) { showToast('Bitiş günü başlangıçtan önce olamaz.', 'error'); return; }
    var btn = document.getElementById('sl-unlock-btn');
    var old = btn ? btn.innerText : '';
    if (btn) { btn.disabled = true; btn.innerText = 'KALDIRILIYOR...'; }
    adminApiRequest('/admin/studio-locks/unlock', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: { studio_id: studioId, reason: reason, start_date: startDate, end_date: endDate }
    }).then(function(res) {
      if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.innerText = old || 'KİLİDİ KALDIR'; }
      var unlocked = Number((res && res.unlocked) || 0);
      if (unlocked > 0) showToast('Kilit kaldırıldı: ' + unlocked + ' kayıt.', 'success');
      else showToast('Bu aralıkta kaldırılacak kilit bulunamadı.', 'info');
      if (String(activeAdminStudioId || '') !== String(studioId || '')) {
        var st = adminStudiosById[String(studioId || '').trim()] || null;
        selectAdminStudio(studioId, String((st && st.name) || studioId));
      } else {
        renderAdminStudioWeekCalendar();
      }
    }).catch(function(err) {
      if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.innerText = old || 'KİLİDİ KALDIR'; }
      showToast('Hata: ' + ((err && err.message) || 'Bilinmeyen hata'), 'error');
    });
  }

  function mondayIsoFrom_(d) {
    var x = d instanceof Date ? new Date(d.getTime()) : new Date(String(d || ''));
    if (isNaN(x.getTime())) x = new Date();
    x.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
    var day = x.getDay();
    var diff = (day === 0 ? -6 : (1 - day));
    x.setDate(x.getDate() + diff);
    return x.getFullYear() + '-' + String(x.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + String(x.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
  }

  function shiftWeekIso_(iso, delta) {
    var d = new Date(String(iso || '') + 'T00:00:00');
    if (isNaN(d.getTime())) d = new Date();
    d.setDate(d.getDate() + (delta * 7));
    return mondayIsoFrom_(d);
  }

  function closeAdminStudioEventModal() {
    var modal = document.getElementById('admin-studio-event-modal');
    if (modal) modal.classList.add('hidden');
  }

  var adminStudioEventPickList = [];

  function formatAdminStudioDt_(iso) {
    try {
      var d = new Date(iso);
      if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return String(iso || '—');
      return d.toLocaleString('tr-TR', { dateStyle: 'short', timeStyle: 'short' });
    } catch (e) {
      return String(iso || '—');
    }
  }

  function openAdminStudioEventModal(ev) {
    adminStudioEventSelected = ev || null;
    var modal = document.getElementById('admin-studio-event-modal');
    var inner = document.getElementById('admin-studio-event-modal-inner');
    if (!modal || !inner || !ev) return;
    var uname = String(ev.user_name || '').trim() || '—';
    var purpose = String(ev.purpose || '').trim() || '—';
    var st = String(ev.status || '').trim();
    inner.innerHTML =
      '<div class="flex justify-between items-start gap-3 mb-4">' +
      '<div class="min-w-0">' +
      '<p class="text-[10px] font-black uppercase text-gray-400 tracking-wider">Etkinlik</p>' +
      '<h3 class="text-lg font-black text-gray-900 leading-tight break-words">' + escAdm(purpose) + '</h3>' +
      '<p class="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">' + escAdm(uname) + '</p>' +
      '<p class="text-[10px] font-mono text-gray-400 mt-1 break-all">' + escAdm(String(ev.id || '')) + '</p></div>' +
      '<button type="button" onclick="closeAdminStudioEventModal()" class="shrink-0 text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-800 text-2xl leading-none px-2 -mt-1" aria-label="Kapat">&times;</button></div>' +
      '<div class="rounded-xl bg-gray-50 border border-gray-100 p-3 mb-4 text-sm">' +
      '<p class="text-[10px] font-black text-gray-400 uppercase mb-1">Zaman</p>' +
      '<p class="font-bold text-gray-800">' + escAdm(formatAdminStudioDt_(ev.start_dt)) + ' → ' + escAdm(formatAdminStudioDt_(ev.end_dt)) + '</p>' +
      '<p class="text-[10px] text-gray-500 mt-2">Durum: <span class="font-bold">' + escAdm(st) + '</span></p></div>' +
      '<div class="flex flex-col gap-2">' +
      '<button type="button" onclick="adminStudioEventOpenEdit()" class="w-full py-3 rounded-xl bg-gray-900 text-white font-black text-sm hover:bg-black transition">Düzenle</button>' +
      '<button type="button" onclick="adminStudioEventOpenDeleteChoice()" class="w-full py-3 rounded-xl border-2 border-red-200 bg-white font-black text-sm text-red-700 hover:bg-red-50 transition">Sil</button>' +
      '</div>';
    modal.classList.remove('hidden');
  }

  function openAdminStudioEventPicker(details) {
    details = details || [];
    adminStudioEventPickList = details;
    var modal = document.getElementById('admin-studio-event-modal');
    var inner = document.getElementById('admin-studio-event-modal-inner');
    if (!modal || !inner) return;
    var rows = details.map(function(it, idx) {
      var line = String(it.user_name || '').trim() + (it.purpose ? (' · ' + String(it.purpose).trim()) : '');
      return '<button type="button" onclick="adminStudioEventPickOne(' + idx + ')" class="w-full text-left py-3 px-3 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 hover:border-[#e30613] hover:bg-red-50/40 transition text-sm font-bold text-gray-800">' + escAdm(line || 'Kayıt') + '<span class="block text-[10px] font-mono text-gray-400 mt-0.5">' + escAdm(formatAdminStudioDt_(it.start_dt)) + '</span></button>';
    }).join('');
    inner.innerHTML =
      '<div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-4">' +
      '<h3 class="text-base font-black text-gray-900">Birden fazla etkinlik</h3>' +
      '<button type="button" onclick="closeAdminStudioEventModal()" class="text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-800 text-2xl leading-none px-2" aria-label="Kapat">&times;</button></div>' +
      '<p class="text-xs text-gray-500 mb-3">Düzenlemek veya silmek için birini seçin.</p>' +
      '<div class="flex flex-col gap-2">' + rows + '</div>';
    modal.classList.remove('hidden');
  }

  function adminStudioEventPickOne(idx) {
    var it = adminStudioEventPickList[idx];
    if (it) openAdminStudioEventModal(it);
  }

  function adminStudioEventOpenDeleteChoice() {
    var inner = document.getElementById('admin-studio-event-modal-inner');
    if (!inner || !adminStudioEventSelected) return;
    inner.innerHTML =
      '<div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-3">' +
      '<h3 class="text-base font-black text-red-800">Silme</h3>' +
      '<button type="button" onclick="openAdminStudioEventModal(adminStudioEventSelected)" class="text-xs font-bold text-[#e30613] hover:underline">Geri</button></div>' +
      '<p class="text-sm text-gray-700 mb-4">Ne silinsin?</p>' +
      '<div class="flex flex-col gap-2">' +
      '<button type="button" onclick="adminStudioEventDeleteConfirm(\'single\')" class="w-full py-3 rounded-xl border-2 border-gray-200 font-black text-sm text-gray-800 hover:bg-gray-50">Sadece bu etkinlik</button>' +
      '<button type="button" onclick="adminStudioEventDeleteConfirm(\'following\')" class="w-full py-3 rounded-xl border-2 border-red-200 font-black text-sm text-red-800 hover:bg-red-50">Bu tarihten sonraki tüm eşleşen tekrarlar</button>' +
      '<button type="button" onclick="closeAdminStudioEventModal()" class="w-full py-2 text-xs font-bold text-gray-500">Vazgeç</button></div>' +
      '<p class="text-[10px] text-gray-400 mt-3">Tekrarlar: aynı kullanıcı, stüdyo, başlık ve yerel başlangıç/bitiş saatleriyle eşleşen kayıtlar (ör. haftalık dizi).</p>';
  }

  function adminStudioEventDeleteConfirm(mode) {
    var ev = adminStudioEventSelected;
    if (!ev || !ev.id) return;
    adminApiRequest('/admin/studio-reservations/delete', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: { id: String(ev.id), mode: String(mode || 'single') }
    }).then(function(res) {
      showToast('Silindi (' + (res && res.deleted != null ? res.deleted : 1) + ' kayıt).', 'success');
      closeAdminStudioEventModal();
      renderAdminStudioWeekCalendar();
    }).catch(function(err) {
      showToast('Hata: ' + (err && err.message ? err.message : ''), 'error');
    });
  }

  function fillStudioEventEditTimeDropdowns_(studioId) {
    var startEl = document.getElementById('se-edit-start');
    var endEl = document.getElementById('se-edit-end');
    if (!startEl || !endEl) return;
    var isGreen = adminIsGreenStudio_(studioId, '');
    var maxStartHour = isGreen ? 21 : 20;
    var maxEndHour = isGreen ? 22 : 21;
    startEl.innerHTML = '';
    endEl.innerHTML = '';
    var i, h;
    for (i = 9; i <= maxStartHour; i++) {
      h = (i < 10 ? '0' + i : String(i));
      startEl.innerHTML += '<option value="' + h + ':00">' + h + ':00</option>';
      endEl.innerHTML += '<option value="' + h + ':00">' + h + ':00</option>';
    }
    h = (maxEndHour < 10 ? '0' + maxEndHour : String(maxEndHour));
    endEl.innerHTML += '<option value="' + h + ':00">' + h + ':00</option>';
  }

  function padHourFromDate_(d) {
    var hh = String(d.getHours()).padStart(2, '0');
    var mm = String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0');
    return mm === '00' ? (hh + ':00') : (hh + ':' + mm);
  }

  function adminStudioEventOpenEdit() {
    var ev = adminStudioEventSelected;
    var inner = document.getElementById('admin-studio-event-modal-inner');
    if (!ev || !inner) return;
    var ds = new Date(ev.start_dt);
    var de = new Date(ev.end_dt);
    if (isNaN(ds.getTime()) || isNaN(de.getTime())) {
      showToast('Geçersiz tarih bilgisi.', 'error');
      return;
    }
    var y = ds.getFullYear();
    var m = String(ds.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
    var dd = String(ds.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
    var dateVal = y + '-' + m + '-' + dd;
    inner.innerHTML =
      '<div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-4">' +
      '<h3 class="text-base font-black text-gray-900">Düzenle</h3>' +
      '<button type="button" onclick="openAdminStudioEventModal(adminStudioEventSelected)" class="text-xs font-bold text-[#e30613] hover:underline">Geri</button></div>' +
      '<label class="block text-[10px] font-black text-gray-400 uppercase mb-1">Başlık (max 20)</label>' +
      '<div class="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3">' +
