      '<input type="text" id="se-edit-purpose" maxlength="20" class="flex-1 p-3 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 text-sm font-mono font-bold" />' +
      '<span id="se-edit-purpose-count" class="text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-400 tabular-nums">0/20</span></div>' +
      '<label class="block text-[10px] font-black text-gray-400 uppercase mb-1">Tarih</label>' +
      '<input type="date" id="se-edit-date" class="w-full p-3 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 text-sm font-bold mb-3" />' +
      '<div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 mb-4">' +
      '<div><label class="block text-[10px] font-black text-gray-400 uppercase mb-1">Başlangıç</label>' +
      '<select id="se-edit-start" class="w-full p-3 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 text-sm font-bold"></select></div>' +
      '<div><label class="block text-[10px] font-black text-gray-400 uppercase mb-1">Bitiş</label>' +
      '<select id="se-edit-end" class="w-full p-3 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 text-sm font-bold"></select></div></div>' +
      '<button type="button" onclick="submitAdminStudioEventEdit()" class="w-full py-3 rounded-xl bg-[#e30613] text-white font-black text-sm hover:bg-red-700">Kaydet</button>';
    fillStudioEventEditTimeDropdowns_(String(ev.studio_id || ''));
    document.getElementById('se-edit-date').value = dateVal;
    document.getElementById('se-edit-purpose').value = String(ev.purpose || '').trim().substring(0, 20);
    var stSel = padHourFromDate_(ds);
    var enSel = padHourFromDate_(de);
    var sEl = document.getElementById('se-edit-start');
    var eEl = document.getElementById('se-edit-end');
    if (sEl && sEl.querySelector && !sEl.querySelector('option[value="' + stSel + '"]')) {
      sEl.innerHTML += '<option value="' + escAttr(stSel) + '">' + escAdm(stSel) + '</option>';
    }
    if (eEl && eEl.querySelector && !eEl.querySelector('option[value="' + enSel + '"]')) {
      eEl.innerHTML += '<option value="' + escAttr(enSel) + '">' + escAdm(enSel) + '</option>';
    }
    if (sEl) sEl.value = stSel;
    if (eEl) eEl.value = enSel;
    var pc = document.getElementById('se-edit-purpose-count');
    var pi = document.getElementById('se-edit-purpose');
    function syncCt() {
      if (pc && pi) pc.textContent = String(pi.value.length) + '/20';
    }
    syncCt();
    if (pi) pi.addEventListener('input', syncCt);
  }

  function submitAdminStudioEventEdit() {
    var ev = adminStudioEventSelected;
    if (!ev || !ev.id) return;
    var dateEl = document.getElementById('se-edit-date');
    var sEl = document.getElementById('se-edit-start');
    var eEl = document.getElementById('se-edit-end');
    var pEl = document.getElementById('se-edit-purpose');
    var date = dateEl ? dateEl.value : '';
    var st = sEl ? sEl.value : '';
    var en = eEl ? eEl.value : '';
    var purpose = String(pEl && pEl.value || '').trim().substring(0, 20);
    if (!date || !st || !en) { showToast('Tarih ve saatleri doldurun.', 'error'); return; }
    var startDt = date + 'T' + st;
    var endDt = date + 'T' + en;
    if (new Date(endDt).getTime() <= new Date(startDt).getTime()) {
      showToast('Bitiş, başlangıçtan sonra olmalı.', 'error');
      return;
    }
    adminApiRequest('/admin/studio-reservations/update', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: { id: String(ev.id), start_dt: startDt, end_dt: endDt, purpose: purpose }
    }).then(function() {
      showToast('Güncellendi.', 'success');
      closeAdminStudioEventModal();
      renderAdminStudioWeekCalendar();
    }).catch(function(err) {
      showToast('Hata: ' + (err && err.message ? err.message : ''), 'error');
    });
  }

  function toIsoLocalDate_(d) {
    return d.getFullYear() + '-' + String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
  }

  function adminStudioWeekendAllowed_(studioId) {
    var st = adminStudiosById[String(studioId || '').trim()] || null;
    var sid = String(studioId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    // GREEN stüdyo varsayılan olarak hafta sonu açık.
    var sName = String((st && (st.name || st.studio_name || st.code)) || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!sName && String(studioId || '').trim() === String(activeAdminStudioId || '').trim()) {
      sName = String(activeAdminStudioName || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    }
    if (sid === 'GREEN' || sName === 'GREEN' || sName === 'GREEN STUDIO' || sName.indexOf('GREEN') >= 0) return true;
    if (!st) return false;
    var v = (st.weekendOk != null) ? st.weekendOk : (st.weekend_ok != null ? st.weekend_ok : st.weekend);
    return v === true || v === 1 || String(v || '').toLowerCase() === 'true';
  }

  function adminStudioDayKind_(studioId, d) {
    if (isPublicHoliday(d)) return 'closed';
    var wd = d.getDay();
    if (!adminStudioWeekendAllowed_(studioId) && (wd === 0 || wd === 6)) return 'closed';
    return 'open';
  }

  function fetchAdminStudioReservationsRange_(fromIso, untilIso) {
    return adminApiRequest('/studio-reservations?from=' + encodeURIComponent(fromIso) + '&to=' + encodeURIComponent(untilIso), { method: 'GET' })
      .then(function(payload) {
        return (payload && payload.data) ? payload.data : [];
      });
  }

  function fetchAdminStudioWeekGridViaApi_(studioId, weekStartIso) {
    var wk = String(weekStartIso || '').trim() || mondayIsoFrom_(new Date());
    var start = new Date(wk + 'T00:00:00');
    if (isNaN(start.getTime())) start = new Date();
    start.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
    var end = new Date(start.getTime());
    end.setDate(end.getDate() + 7);
    var fromIso = toIsoLocalDate_(start);
    var untilIso = toIsoLocalDate_(end);
    return fetchAdminStudioReservationsRange_(fromIso, untilIso).then(function(rows) {
      var days = [];
      for (var di = 0; di < 7; di++) {
        var d = new Date(start.getTime());
        d.setDate(start.getDate() + di);
        days.push({ iso: toIsoLocalDate_(d), day: d.getDate(), month: d.getMonth() + 1, dow: d.getDay() });
      }
      var isGreenStudio = adminIsGreenStudio_(studioId, activeAdminStudioName);
      var maxStartMins = (isGreenStudio ? 21 : 20) * 60;
      var slots = [];
      for (var mins = 9 * 60; mins <= maxStartMins; mins += 30) {
        slots.push({ mins: mins, label: String(Math.floor(mins / 60)).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(mins % 60).padStart(2, '0') });
      }
      if (isGreenStudio) {
        slots.push({ mins: 22 * 60, label: '22:00', boundary: true });
      }
      var cells = {};
      var slotDetails = {};
      var cellAdminCaption = {};
      function studioSlotTitleFromRow_(row) {
        var purposeRaw = String((row && row.purpose) || '').trim();
        var purpose = purposeRaw.replace(/\s*\[gcal:[^\]]+\]\s*$/i, '').trim();
        return purpose || 'Dolu';
      }
      slots.forEach(function(s) {
        days.forEach(function(d) {
          var dayDate = new Date(d.iso + 'T00:00:00');
          if (s.boundary) {
            cells[d.iso + '|' + s.mins] = 'closed';
          } else {
            cells[d.iso + '|' + s.mins] = (adminStudioDayKind_(studioId, dayDate) === 'open') ? 'free' : 'closed';
          }
        });
      });
      (rows || []).forEach(function(r) {
        var rid = String(r.studio_id || '').trim();
        if (rid !== String(studioId || '').trim()) return;
        var status = String(r.status || '').toLowerCase();
        if (['cancelled', 'cancelled_by_user', 'rejected', 'rejected_by_admin', 'returned', 'key_returned', 'completed', 'no_show'].indexOf(status) >= 0) return;
        var sd = new Date(r.start_at);
        var ed = new Date(r.end_at);
        if (isNaN(sd.getTime()) || isNaN(ed.getTime()) || ed <= sd) return;
        slots.forEach(function(s) {
          days.forEach(function(d) {
            var key = d.iso + '|' + s.mins;
            if (String(cells[key]) === 'closed') return;
            var cellStart = new Date(d.iso + 'T' + String(Math.floor(s.mins / 60)).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(s.mins % 60).padStart(2, '0') + ':00');
            var cellEnd = new Date(cellStart.getTime() + 30 * 60 * 1000);
            if (sd < cellEnd && ed > cellStart) {
              cells[key] = 'busy';
              if (!slotDetails[key]) slotDetails[key] = [];
              slotDetails[key].push(r);
              if (!cellAdminCaption[key]) {
                cellAdminCaption[key] = studioSlotTitleFromRow_(r);
              }
            }
          });
        });
      });
      return {
        week_start: wk,
        days: days,
        slots: slots,
        cells: cells,
        slot_details: slotDetails,
        cell_admin_caption: cellAdminCaption
      };
    });
  }

  function fetchAdminStudioMonthGridViaApi_(studioId, focusIso) {
    var base = new Date(String(focusIso || '') + 'T00:00:00');
    if (isNaN(base.getTime())) base = new Date();
    base = new Date(base.getFullYear(), base.getMonth(), 1);
    var monthStart = new Date(base.getTime());
    var monthEnd = new Date(base.getFullYear(), base.getMonth() + 1, 1);
    var fromIso = toIsoLocalDate_(monthStart);
    var untilIso = toIsoLocalDate_(monthEnd);
    return fetchAdminStudioReservationsRange_(fromIso, untilIso).then(function(rows) {
      var days = [];
      for (var d = 1; d <= new Date(base.getFullYear(), base.getMonth() + 1, 0).getDate(); d++) {
        var cur = new Date(base.getFullYear(), base.getMonth(), d);
        var iso = toIsoLocalDate_(cur);
        var kind = adminStudioDayKind_(studioId, cur);
        var list = (rows || []).filter(function(r) {
          if (String(r.studio_id || '').trim() !== String(studioId || '').trim()) return false;
          var st = String(r.status || '').toLowerCase();
          if (['cancelled', 'cancelled_by_user', 'rejected', 'rejected_by_admin', 'returned', 'key_returned', 'completed', 'no_show'].indexOf(st) >= 0) return false;
          var rs = new Date(String(r.start_at || '')).getTime();
          var re = new Date(String(r.end_at || '')).getTime();
          var ds = new Date(iso + 'T00:00:00').getTime();
          var de = ds + (24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
          if (isNaN(rs) || isNaN(re)) return false;
          return rs < de && re > ds;
        });
        days.push({ iso: iso, day: d, dow: cur.getDay(), kind: kind, count: list.length, details: list });
      }
      return { month_start: fromIso, month: base.getMonth() + 1, year: base.getFullYear(), days: days };
    });
  }

  function renderAdminStudioWeekCalendar() {
    if (!activeAdminStudioId) return;
    if (adminStudioWeekGridInFlight) return;
    adminStudioWeekGridInFlight = true;
    var frame = document.getElementById('admin-calendar-frame');
    if (!frame) { adminStudioWeekGridInFlight = false; return; }
    frame.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-gray-400 py-10 text-xs animate-pulse">Takvim yükleniyor...</div>';
    if (!adminStudioFocusIso) adminStudioFocusIso = adminStudioWeekStartIso || mondayIsoFrom_(new Date());
    var req = (adminStudioCalendarMode === 'month')
      ? fetchAdminStudioMonthGridViaApi_(activeAdminStudioId, adminStudioFocusIso)
      : fetchAdminStudioWeekGridViaApi_(activeAdminStudioId, adminStudioWeekStartIso);
    req.then(function(res) {
      adminStudioWeekGridInFlight = false;
      if (!res || res.error) {
        frame.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-red-500 py-10 text-xs">' + escAdm((res && res.error) || 'Hata') + '</div>';
        return;
      }
      var labelEl = document.getElementById('admin-week-label');
      if (adminStudioCalendarMode === 'month') {
        if (labelEl) labelEl.textContent = String(res.month || '') + '/' + String(res.year || '');
        var first = new Date((res.month_start || adminStudioFocusIso) + 'T00:00:00');
        var startOffset = (first.getDay() + 6) % 7; // monday=0
        var cells = [];
        for (var b = 0; b < startOffset; b++) cells.push('<div class="h-20 rounded-lg border border-transparent"></div>');
        (res.days || []).forEach(function(d) {
          var cls = d.kind === 'closed'
            ? 'bg-gray-100 border-gray-200 text-gray-400'
            : (d.count > 0 ? 'bg-rose-50 border-rose-200 text-rose-900 cursor-pointer hover:bg-rose-100' : 'bg-emerald-50 border-emerald-200 text-emerald-900 cursor-pointer hover:bg-emerald-100');
          var info = d.kind === 'closed' ? 'Kapalı' : (d.count > 0 ? (String(d.count) + ' rezervasyon') : 'Müsait');
          var click = d.kind === 'closed' ? '' : (' onclick="adminOpenWeekFromMonthDay(\'' + escAttr(d.iso) + '\')" ');
          cells.push('<button type="button"' + click + ' class="h-20 rounded-lg border p-2 text-left flex flex-col justify-between ' + cls + '"><span class="text-xs font-black">' + escAdm(String(d.day || '')) + '</span><span class="text-[10px] font-bold">' + escAdm(info) + '</span></button>');
        });
        frame.innerHTML = '<div class="p-3 pb-6"><div class="grid grid-cols-7 gap-2 mb-2 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500"><div>Pzt</div><div>Sal</div><div>Çar</div><div>Per</div><div>Cum</div><div>Cmt</div><div>Paz</div></div><div class="grid grid-cols-7 gap-2">' + cells.join('') + '</div><p class="mt-3 text-[10px] text-gray-500">Ay görünümünde bir güne tıklayarak haftalık zaman çizelgesine geçebilirsiniz.</p></div>';
        return;
      }
      adminStudioWeekStartIso = String(res.week_start || adminStudioWeekStartIso || '').trim() || adminStudioWeekStartIso;
      adminStudioFocusIso = adminStudioWeekStartIso;
      if (labelEl) labelEl.textContent = adminStudioWeekStartIso;
      var days = res.days || [];
      var slots = res.slots || [];
      var cells = res.cells || {};
      var slotDetails = res.slot_details || {};
      var cellAdminCaption = res.cell_admin_caption || {};
      adminStudioSlotDetailsCache = {};
      var wk = ['Paz','Pzt','Sal','Çar','Per','Cum','Cmt'];
      var th = '<tr><th class="p-1 w-10"></th>' + days.map(function(d){ return '<th class="p-1 text-[9px] font-bold text-gray-600 border-b border-gray-200 min-w-[40px]">' + String(d.day).padStart(2,'0') + '.' + String(d.month).padStart(2,'0') + '<br><span class="text-gray-400 font-semibold">' + wk[d.dow] + '</span></th>'; }).join('') + '</tr>';
      var rows = slots.map(function(s) {
        var line = days.map(function(d) {
          var k = d.iso + '|' + s.mins;
          var st = String(cells[k] || 'closed');
          var isSel = (k === adminStudioSelectedSlotKey);
          var details = Array.isArray(slotDetails[k]) ? slotDetails[k] : [];
          if (st === 'busy' && details.length) adminStudioSlotDetailsCache[k] = details;
          var cls = st === 'free' ? 'bg-emerald-100 hover:bg-emerald-200 cursor-pointer' : (st === 'busy' ? 'bg-rose-200' : 'bg-gray-200');
          if (st === 'busy' && details.length) cls += ' cursor-pointer hover:brightness-95 active:brightness-90 transition';
          if (isSel) cls += ' ring-2 ring-[#e30613] shadow-sm';
          var data = st === 'free' ? (' data-day="' + escAttr(d.iso) + '" data-start="' + escAttr(s.label) + '"') : '';
          var busyKey = (st === 'busy' && details.length) ? (' data-cell-key="' + escAttr(k) + '"') : '';
          var detailTitle = '';
          if (st === 'busy' && details.length) {
            detailTitle = details.map(function(it) {
              var uname = String(it.user_name || '').trim() || 'Bilinmeyen kullanıcı';
              var purpose = String(it.purpose || '').trim().replace(/\s*\[gcal:[^\]]+\]\s*$/i, '').trim();
              return purpose ? (uname + ' - ' + purpose) : uname;
            }).join('\n');
            detailTitle += (detailTitle ? '\n' : '') + 'Tıklayın: düzenle / sil';
          } else if (st === 'free') {
            detailTitle = 'Müsait - tıklayıp seçebilirsiniz';
          } else {
            detailTitle = st === 'closed' ? 'Kapalı' : 'Sınır slotu';
          }
          var cap = String(cellAdminCaption[k] || '').trim();
          var inner = (st === 'busy' && cap) ? ('<span class="block leading-tight text-[10px] md:text-[11px] font-bold text-rose-950/95 px-0.5 line-clamp-3 text-left [overflow-wrap:anywhere]">' + escAdm(cap) + '</span>') : '';
          return '<td class="p-0.5 border-b border-gray-100"><button type="button"' + data + busyKey + ' class="admin-studio-slot w-full min-h-[2.2rem] md:min-h-[2.5rem] py-0.5 rounded-sm flex items-center justify-center ' + cls + '" title="' + escAttr(detailTitle) + '">' + inner + '</button></td>';
        }).join('');
        return '<tr><td class="pr-1 py-0.5 text-[8px] text-gray-500 font-mono">' + escAdm(s.label) + '</td>' + line + '</tr>';
      }).join('');
      var slotLabel = adminStudioSelectedSlotKey ? ('Seçili: ' + adminStudioSelectedSlotKey.replace('|', ' ')) : 'Seçili slot yok';
      frame.innerHTML = '<div class="overflow-x-auto p-3 pb-6"><table class="w-full border-collapse text-center"><thead>' + th + '</thead><tbody>' + rows + '</tbody></table><p class="mt-2 mb-2 text-[10px] font-semibold text-gray-500">' + escAdm(slotLabel) + '</p></div>';
    }).catch(function(err) {
      adminStudioWeekGridInFlight = false;
      frame.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-red-500 py-10 text-xs">' + escAdm((err && err.message) || 'Hata') + '</div>';
    });
  }

  function adminOpenWeekFromMonthDay(dayIso) {
    var d = new Date(String(dayIso || '') + 'T00:00:00');
    if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return;
    adminStudioCalendarMode = 'week';
    adminStudioWeekStartIso = mondayIsoFrom_(d);
    adminStudioFocusIso = toIsoLocalDate_(d);
    var w = document.getElementById('admin-cal-mode-week');
    var m = document.getElementById('admin-cal-mode-month');
    if (w) w.click();
    else renderAdminStudioWeekCalendar();
    if (m) {
      // week mode button click updates styles; ensure month button passive.
      m.className = 'px-2 py-1 rounded border text-xs font-bold text-gray-700 hover:bg-white';
    }
  }

  function clearStudioForm() {
    document.getElementById('sr-email').value = '';
    document.getElementById('sr-date').value = '';
    document.getElementById('sr-period').value = 'once';
    document.getElementById('sr-start').value = '09:00';
    document.getElementById('sr-end').value = '11:00';
    document.getElementById('sr-end-period-date').value = '';
    document.getElementById('sr-purpose').value = '';
    try {
      var _spc = document.getElementById('sr-purpose-count');
      if (_spc) _spc.textContent = '0/10';
    } catch (_eSpc) {}
    document.getElementById('sr-with-equip').checked = false;
    document.getElementById('sr-equip-wrap').classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('sr-equip-q').value = '';
    studioEquipPool = [];
    studioEquipSelected = {};
    renderStudioEquipList();
    document.getElementById('sr-period-info').classList.add('hidden');
    document.getElementById('sr-end-period-wrap').classList.add('hidden');
  }

  function submitAdminStudioReservation() {
    if (!activeAdminStudioId) { showToast('Lütfen bir stüdyo seçin.', 'error'); return; }
    var email = document.getElementById('sr-email').value;
    var date = document.getElementById('sr-date').value;
    var period = document.getElementById('sr-period').value;
    var startTime = document.getElementById('sr-start').value;
    var endTime = document.getElementById('sr-end').value;
    var endPeriodDate = document.getElementById('sr-end-period-date').value;
    var purpose = String(document.getElementById('sr-purpose').value || '').trim().substring(0, 20);
    var withEquip = !!(document.getElementById('sr-with-equip') && document.getElementById('sr-with-equip').checked);
    if (!email) { showToast('E-posta adresi zorunludur.', 'error'); return; }
    if (!date) { showToast('Tarih seçiniz.', 'error'); return; }
    var startDt = date + 'T' + startTime;
    var endDt = date + 'T' + endTime;
    if (new Date(endDt).getTime() <= new Date(startDt).getTime()) { showToast('Bitiş saati başlangıçtan sonra olmalı.', 'error'); return; }
    if (isPublicHoliday(new Date(startDt))) { showToast('Resmi tatillerde rezervasyon kapalıdır.', 'error'); return; }
    var endPeriodDt = '';
    if (period !== 'once') {
      if (!endPeriodDate) { showToast('Tekrarlı rezervasyonda tekrar bitiş tarihi zorunlu.', 'error'); return; }
      endPeriodDt = endPeriodDate;
      if (new Date(endPeriodDate + 'T23:59:59').getTime() < new Date(startDt).getTime()) { showToast('Tekrar bitiş tarihi başlangıçtan önce olamaz.', 'error'); return; }
    }
    var selectedEquipIds = [];
    if (withEquip) {
      studioEquipPool.forEach(function(it) {
        var eid = String(it.id || '');
        if (eid && studioEquipSelected[eid] === true) selectedEquipIds.push(eid);
      });
      if (!selectedEquipIds.length) { showToast('Ekipmanlı teslim için en az bir ekipman seçin.', 'error'); return; }
    }
    if (withEquip && selectedEquipIds.length) {
      showToast('Not: Stüdyoya bağlı ekipman ekleme bu endpoint paketinde henüz aktif değil.', 'info');
    }
    var buildWeeklySlots = function(baseDate, startHm, endHm, untilDate) {
      var out = [];
      var cur = new Date(baseDate + 'T00:00:00');
      var lim = new Date(untilDate + 'T00:00:00');
      if (isNaN(cur.getTime()) || isNaN(lim.getTime())) return out;
      while (cur.getTime() <= lim.getTime()) {
        var y = cur.getFullYear();
        var m = String(cur.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
        var d = String(cur.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
        var isoDay = y + '-' + m + '-' + d;
        out.push({ start_at: isoDay + 'T' + startHm, end_at: isoDay + 'T' + endHm });
        cur.setDate(cur.getDate() + 7);
      }
      return out;
    };
    var slots = (period === 'weekly')
      ? buildWeeklySlots(date, startTime, endTime, endPeriodDt)
      : [{ start_at: startDt, end_at: endDt }];
    if (!slots.length) { showToast('Tekrarlı rezervasyon tarihleri oluşturulamadı.', 'error'); return; }
    var validSlots = slots.filter(function(sl) { return !isPublicHoliday(new Date(String(sl.start_at || ''))); });
    if (!validSlots.length) { showToast('Seçilen tarih aralığındaki tüm tekrarlar resmi tatile denk geliyor.', 'error'); return; }

    var btn = document.getElementById('sr-submit-btn');
    var originalText = btn.innerText;
    btn.innerText = 'OLUŞTURULUYOR...'; btn.disabled = true;
    showToast('Rezervasyon(lar) oluşturuluyor...', 'info');
    var created = 0;
    var failed = 0;
    var firstErr = '';
    var seq = Promise.resolve();
    validSlots.forEach(function(sl) {
      seq = seq.then(function() {
        var payload = { studio_id: activeAdminStudioId, start_at: sl.start_at, end_at: sl.end_at, purpose: purpose };
        return adminApiRequest('/studio-reservations', { method: 'POST', body: payload })
          .then(function() { created += 1; })
          .catch(function(err) {
            failed += 1;
            if (!firstErr) firstErr = String((err && err.message) || 'Bilinmeyen hata');
          });
      });
    });
    seq.then(function() {
      btn.innerText = originalText; btn.disabled = false;
      if (created > 0 && failed === 0) {
        showToast('Başarılı! ' + created + ' adet stüdyo rezervasyonu oluşturuldu.', 'success');
        clearStudioForm();
        renderAdminStudioWeekCalendar();
        return;
      }
      if (created > 0 && failed > 0) {
        showToast('Kısmi tamamlandı: ' + created + ' oluşturuldu, ' + failed + ' oluşturulamadı. ' + (firstErr || ''), 'info');
        renderAdminStudioWeekCalendar();
        return;
      }
      showToast('Hata: ' + (firstErr || 'Bilinmeyen hata'), 'error');
    }).catch(function(err) {
      btn.innerText = originalText; btn.disabled = false;
      showToast('Hata: ' + ((err && err.message) || 'Bilinmeyen hata'), 'error');
    });
  }

  // ═══ GEÇMİŞ ═══
  function loadHistory() {
    var tbody = document.getElementById('history-table-body');
    var statusFilterEl = document.getElementById('history-status-filter');
    var userFilterEl = document.getElementById('history-user-filter');
    var eqFilterEl = document.getElementById('history-eq-filter');
    var statusFilter = statusFilterEl ? String(statusFilterEl.value || '').trim() : '';
    var userFilter = userFilterEl ? String(userFilterEl.value || '').trim().toLowerCase() : '';
    var eqFilter = eqFilterEl ? String(eqFilterEl.value || '').trim().toLowerCase() : '';
    if (!tbody) return;
    tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="p-8 text-center text-gray-400 animate-pulse">Yükleniyor...</td></tr>';
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
      if (!data || !data.length) { tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="p-8 text-center text-gray-400">Kayıt bulunamadı.</td></tr>'; return; }
      tbody.innerHTML = '';
      var statusMap = { 'Pending': 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-700', 'Approved': 'bg-green-100 text-green-700', 'Rejected': 'bg-red-100 text-red-700', 'Rejected (Removed)': 'bg-red-100 text-red-700', 'Cancelled': 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-500', 'Picked Up': 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-700', 'Returned': 'bg-emerald-100 text-emerald-700' };
      var statusLabelTr = { 'Pending': 'Onay Bekliyor', 'Approved': 'Onaylandı', 'Picked Up': 'Teslim Alındı', 'Returned': 'İade Geldi' };
      var visible = 0;
      data.forEach(function(r) {
        var stRaw = String(r.status || '').trim();
        if (statusFilter && stRaw !== statusFilter) return;
        if (userFilter && String(r.userName || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(userFilter) === -1) return;
        if (eqFilter) {
          var eqBlob = (String(r.eqName || '') + ' ' + String(r.eqCode || '') + ' ' + String(r.resId || '')).toLowerCase();
          if (eqBlob.indexOf(eqFilter) === -1) return;
        }
        visible++;
        var badgeClass = statusMap[stRaw] || 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600';
        var stShow = statusLabelTr[stRaw] || stRaw || '-';
        var fmtDt = function(dt) { try { return dt ? new Date(dt).toLocaleString('tr-TR', { day: '2-digit', month: 'short', year: 'numeric', hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' }) : '-'; } catch(e) { return dt || '-'; } };
        tbody.innerHTML += '<tr class="border-b border-gray-50 hover:bg-gray-50 transition"><td class="px-5 py-3 text-[10px] font-mono text-gray-400">' + (r.eqCode || '-') + '</td><td class="px-5 py-3 text-[11px] font-bold text-gray-800">' + (r.eqName || '-') + '</td><td class="px-5 py-3 text-[11px] text-gray-600">' + (r.userName || '-') + '</td><td class="px-5 py-3 text-[10px] text-gray-500">' + fmtDt(r.startDt) + '</td><td class="px-5 py-3 text-[10px] text-gray-500">' + fmtDt(r.endDt) + '</td><td class="px-5 py-3"><span class="px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full text-[9px] font-black ' + badgeClass + '">' + stShow + '</span></td></tr>';
      });
      if (!visible) tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="p-8 text-center text-gray-400">Filtreye uygun kayıt bulunamadı.</td></tr>';
    }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" class="p-8 text-center text-red-500">Hata: ' + (err.message || '') + '</td></tr>';
    }).getAdminReservationHistory(currentAuthToken);
  }

  // ═══ İLERİ TARİHLİ EKİPMAN REZERVASYONU ═══
  var forwardCart = [];
  var forwardPool = [];
  function loadForwardEquipPage() {
    forwardCart = [];
    forwardPool = [];
    renderForwardCart();
    var feEmail = document.getElementById('fe-email');
    var fePurpose = document.getElementById('fe-purpose');
    var feQ = document.getElementById('fe-q');
    var feStartDate = document.getElementById('fe-start-date');
    var feEndDate = document.getElementById('fe-end-date');
    var feStartTime = document.getElementById('fe-start-time');
    var feEndTime = document.getElementById('fe-end-time');
    var fep = document.getElementById('fe-period');
    var few = document.getElementById('fe-end-period-wrap');
    var fed = document.getElementById('fe-end-period-date');
    if (feEmail) feEmail.value = '';
    if (fePurpose) fePurpose.value = '';
    if (feQ) feQ.value = '';
    if (feStartDate) feStartDate.value = '';
    if (feEndDate) feEndDate.value = '';
    if (feStartTime && feStartTime.options && feStartTime.options.length) feStartTime.selectedIndex = 0;
    if (feEndTime && feEndTime.options && feEndTime.options.length) feEndTime.selectedIndex = 0;
    if (fep) fep.value = 'once';
    if (few) few.classList.add('hidden');
    if (fed) fed.value = '';
    updateForwardHolidayWarning_();
    refreshInventoryData(function() {
      forwardPool = (allEq || []).filter(function(i) { return !i.isStudioKey && i.status === 'AVAILABLE'; });
      filterForwardEquip();
    });
  }
  function forwardHolidayDatesInRange_(startIso, endIso) {
    var s = new Date(String(startIso || ''));
    var e = new Date(String(endIso || ''));
    if (isNaN(s.getTime()) || isNaN(e.getTime()) || e <= s) return [];
    var cur = new Date(s.getTime());
    cur.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
    var last = new Date(e.getTime() - 1);
    last.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
    var out = [];
    while (cur <= last) {
      if (isPublicHoliday(cur)) out.push(String(cur.getDate()).padStart(2, '0') + '.' + String(cur.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '.' + cur.getFullYear());
      cur.setDate(cur.getDate() + 1);
    }
    return out;
  }
  function updateForwardHolidayWarning_() {
    var d1 = document.getElementById('fe-start-date');
    var t1 = document.getElementById('fe-start-time');
    var d2 = document.getElementById('fe-end-date');
    var t2 = document.getElementById('fe-end-time');
    var warn = document.getElementById('fe-holiday-warning');
    var btn = document.getElementById('fe-submit-btn');
    if (!warn || !btn || !d1 || !t1 || !d2 || !t2) return false;
    var sd = d1.value && t1.value ? (d1.value + 'T' + t1.value) : '';
    var ed = d2.value && t2.value ? (d2.value + 'T' + t2.value) : '';
    var blocked = forwardHolidayDatesInRange_(sd, ed);
    if (blocked.length) {
      warn.textContent = 'Resmi tatil secimi var: ' + blocked.join(', ') + '. Bu aralikta rezervasyon yapilamaz.';
      warn.classList.remove('hidden');
      btn.disabled = true;
      btn.classList.add('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed');
      return true;
    }
    warn.classList.add('hidden');
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.classList.remove('opacity-50', 'cursor-not-allowed');
    return false;
  }
  function loadForwardAvailableItems() {
    var d1 = document.getElementById('fe-start-date').value;
    var t1 = document.getElementById('fe-start-time').value;
    var d2 = document.getElementById('fe-end-date').value;
    var t2 = document.getElementById('fe-end-time').value;
    var sd = d1 && t1 ? (d1 + 'T' + t1) : '';
    var ed = d2 && t2 ? (d2 + 'T' + t2) : '';
    if (updateForwardHolidayWarning_()) { showToast('Resmi tatillerde rezervasyon kapalıdır.', 'error'); return; }
    if (!sd || !ed) { showToast('Önce teslim ve iade tarihi ile saatleri seçin.', 'error'); return; }
    if (new Date(ed).getTime() <= new Date(sd).getTime()) { showToast('İade, teslimden sonra olmalı.', 'error'); return; }
    showToast('Müsait ekipmanlar yükleniyor…', 'info');
    adminApiRequest('/admin/equipment/forward-available', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: { start_at: sd, end_at: ed }
    }).then(function(r) {
      forwardPool = r.list || [];
      filterForwardEquip();
      showToast('Müsait ekipman: ' + String((r.list || []).length || 0), 'success');
    }).catch(function(e) {
      showToast((e && e.message) || 'Hata', 'error');
    });
  }
  function filterForwardEquip() {
    var q = document.getElementById('fe-q').value.toLowerCase();
    var list = document.getElementById('fe-list');
    if (!list) return;
    list.innerHTML = '';
    (forwardPool || []).filter(function(i) {
      var ty = String(i.type || '').toLowerCase();
      var code = String(i.code || '').toLowerCase();
      return (i.name && i.name.toLowerCase().includes(q)) || (code && code.includes(q)) || (ty && ty.includes(q));
    }).forEach(function(item) {
      var tyFe = item.type ? '<p class="text-[9px] text-gray-500 mt-0.5">' + escAdm(item.type) + '</p>' : '';
      list.innerHTML += '<div onclick="addToForwardCart(\'' + item.id.replace(/'/g, "\\'") + '\')" class="p-4 bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm cursor-pointer hover:border-[#e30613] transition"><h3 class="text-xs font-bold text-gray-800">' + escAdm(item.name) + '</h3><p class="text-[9px] font-mono text-gray-400">' + escAdm(publicEquipmentId_(item.code, item.id)) + '</p>' + tyFe + '</div>';
    });
    if (!list.innerHTML) {
      list.innerHTML = '<p class="text-center text-gray-400 text-xs mt-8">Bu filtrede ekipman bulunamadı.</p>';
    }
  }
  function addToForwardCart(id) { if (forwardCart.indexOf(id) >= 0) return; forwardCart.push(id); renderForwardCart(); }
  function removeFromForwardCart(id) { forwardCart = forwardCart.filter(function(x) { return x !== id; }); renderForwardCart(); }
  function renderForwardCart() {
    var el = document.getElementById('fe-cart');
    if (!el) return;
    el.innerHTML = forwardCart.length ? '' : '<p class="text-center text-gray-400 text-xs mt-6">Sepet boş</p>';
    forwardCart.forEach(function(id) {
      var item = allEq.find(function(i) { return i.id === id; });
      if (item) el.innerHTML += '<div class="flex justify-between items-center bg-white p-3 rounded-xl border border-gray-200"><div class="min-w-0"><p class="text-[11px] font-bold truncate">' + escAdm(item.name) + '</p><p class="text-[9px] font-mono text-gray-400">' + escAdm(publicEquipmentId_(item.code, id)) + '</p></div><button type="button" onclick="removeFromForwardCart(\'' + id.replace(/'/g, "\\'") + '\')" class="text-red-400 font-bold px-2">×</button></div>';
    });
  }
  function submitForwardReservation() {
    var userKey = document.getElementById('fe-email').value.trim();
    var d1 = document.getElementById('fe-start-date').value;
    var t1 = document.getElementById('fe-start-time').value;
    var d2 = document.getElementById('fe-end-date').value;
    var t2 = document.getElementById('fe-end-time').value;
    var sd = d1 && t1 ? (d1 + 'T' + t1) : '';
    var ed = d2 && t2 ? (d2 + 'T' + t2) : '';
    if (updateForwardHolidayWarning_()) { showToast('Resmi tatillerde rezervasyon kapalıdır.', 'error'); return; }
    var endPeriod = document.getElementById('fe-end-period-date') ? document.getElementById('fe-end-period-date').value : '';
    var period = document.getElementById('fe-period').value;
    var purpose = document.getElementById('fe-purpose').value.trim();
    if (!userKey || !forwardCart.length || !sd || !ed) { showToast('E-posta/öğrenci no, sepet ve teslim/iade zamanları gerekli.', 'error'); return; }
    if (period !== 'once' && !endPeriod) { showToast('Tekrarlı rezervasyonda tekrar bitiş tarihi zorunlu.', 'error'); return; }
    if (new Date(ed).getTime() <= new Date(sd).getTime()) { showToast('İade, teslimden sonra olmalı.', 'error'); return; }
    if (period !== 'once') { showToast('Yeni API sürümünde tekrar eden ekipman rezervasyonu şimdilik kapalı.', 'error'); return; }
    showToast('Oluşturuluyor…', 'info');
    Promise.allSettled((forwardCart || []).map(function(itemId) {
      return adminApiRequest('/equipment-reservations', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: {
          equipment_item_id: String(itemId || ''),
          start_at: sd,
          end_at: ed,
          note: purpose || 'Admin ileri tarihli rezervasyon'
        }
      });
    })).then(function(results) {
      var okCount = results.filter(function(r) { return r.status === 'fulfilled'; }).length;
      var fail = results.find(function(r) { return r.status === 'rejected'; });
      if (okCount > 0) showToast('Tamam: ' + okCount + ' rezervasyon oluşturuldu.');
      if (fail && fail.status === 'rejected') {
        showToast((fail.reason && fail.reason.message) || 'Bazı kalemler oluşturulamadı.', 'error');
      } else {
        loadForwardEquipPage();
      }
    }).catch(function(e) { showToast((e && e.message) || 'Hata', 'error'); });
  }

  function loadOverdueList() {
    var box = document.getElementById('overdue-container');
    if (!box) return;
    box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400 text-sm">Yükleniyor…</p>';
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(rows) {
      if (!rows || !rows.length) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400">Gecikmiş kayıt yok.</p>'; return; }
      var html = '<div class="space-y-2">';
      rows.forEach(function(r) {
        var rid = escAdm(r.id);
        html += '<label class="flex items-center gap-3 bg-white p-4 rounded-2xl border border-gray-100"><input type="checkbox" class="fe-overdue-cb w-4 h-4" value="' + rid + '"><div class="flex-1"><p class="font-bold text-sm">' + escAdm(r.name) + ' <span class="font-mono text-[10px] text-gray-400">' + rid + '</span></p><p class="text-xs text-gray-600">' + escAdm(r.studentName || r.studentId || '') + '</p><p class="text-[10px] text-red-600">İade: ' + escAdm(r.due) + '</p></div></label>';
      });
      html += '</div><button type="button" onclick="sendOverdueReminders()" class="mt-4 w-full bg-amber-600 text-white font-black py-3 rounded-xl text-xs">Seçilenlere hatırlatma e-postası</button>';
      box.innerHTML = html;
    }).getAdminOverdueEquipmentList(currentAuthToken);
  }
  function sendOverdueReminders() {
    var ids = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.fe-overdue-cb:checked')).map(function(c) { return c.value; });
    if (!ids.length) { showToast('En az bir kayıt seçin.', 'error'); return; }
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) {
      if (r && r.success) showToast('Gönderildi: ' + (r.sent || 0));
      else showToast((r && r.error) || 'Hata', 'error');
    }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { showToast(err.message || 'Hata', 'error'); }).adminSendOverdueReminderEmails(ids, currentAuthToken);
  }

  function loadPenaltiesAdmin() {
    var box = document.getElementById('penalties-container');
    if (!box) return;
    box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400 text-sm">Yükleniyor…</p>';
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(list) {
      if (!list || !list.length) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400">Kayıt yok.</p>'; return; }
      var html = '<div class="overflow-x-auto bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100"><table class="w-full text-left text-xs"><thead class="bg-gray-50"><tr><th class="px-4 py-3">Kullanıcı</th><th class="px-4 py-3">Aşama</th><th class="px-4 py-3">Durum</th><th class="px-4 py-3">Sebep</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
      list.forEach(function(p) {
        html += '<tr class="border-t border-gray-100"><td class="px-4 py-2 font-mono text-[10px]">' + escAdm(p.user_id) + '<br><span class="text-gray-600">' + escAdm(p.user_name) + '</span></td><td class="px-4 py-2">' + escAdm(p.stageLabel) + '</td><td class="px-4 py-2">' + (p.active ? (p.isSuspended ? 'Askıda' : 'Uyarı') : 'Pasif') + '</td><td class="px-4 py-2 max-w-xs truncate" title="' + escAdm(p.reason) + '">' + escAdm(p.reason) + '</td></tr>';
      });
      html += '</tbody></table></div>';
      box.innerHTML = html;
    }).getAdminPenaltiesList(currentAuthToken);
  }

  function runUserLookup() {
    var q = document.getElementById('user-lookup-q').value.trim();
    var out = document.getElementById('user-lookup-result');
    if (!q) { showToast('Arama boş.', 'error'); return; }
    if (q.length < 3) { out.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400 text-sm">En az 3 karakter girin.</p>'; return; }
    out.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400 text-sm">Aranıyor…</p>';
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res.error) { out.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600 text-sm">' + escAdm(res.error) + '</p>'; return; }
      if (!res.matches || !res.matches.length) { out.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400">Sonuç yok.</p>'; return; }
      out.innerHTML = res.matches.map(function(m) {
        var p = m.profile || {};
        var sid = m.studentIdDisplay || p.student_no || p.id || '';
        var h = (m.equipmentHistory || []).slice(-15).reverse().map(function(r) {
          return '<div class="py-1 text-[10px] border-b border-gray-50"><span class="font-mono">' + escAdm(r.resId) + '</span> · ' + escAdm(r.eqName) + ' · <span class="text-gray-500">' + escAdm(r.status) + '</span></div>';
        }).join('');
        var pe = (m.pendingEquipmentApprovals || []).map(function(x) {
          return '<div class="text-[10px] py-1 border-b border-amber-100">' + escAdm(x.eqName) + ' · ' + escAdm(x.resId) + ' · <span class="text-amber-700">' + escAdm(x.status) + '</span></div>';
        }).join('');
        var ps = (m.pendingStudioApprovals || []).map(function(x) {
          return '<div class="text-[10px] py-1 border-b border-indigo-100">' + escAdm(x.studio) + ' · ' + escAdm(x.id) + '</div>';
        }).join('');
        var r15 = (m.equipmentRecent15d || []).map(function(x) {
          return '<div class="text-[10px] py-1 border-b border-gray-50">' + escAdm(x.eqName) + ' · ' + escAdm(x.status) + '</div>';
        }).join('');
        var loan = (m.loansOnHand || []).map(function(L) {
          return '<div class="text-[10px] py-1 border-b border-gray-50">' + escAdm(L.name) + ' <span class="font-mono">' + escAdm(L.eqId) + '</span> · iade: ' + escAdm(L.due) + (L.overdue ? ' <span class="text-red-600 font-black">GEÇİKMİŞ</span>' : '') + '</div>';
        }).join('');
        var resp = (m.responsibleForEquipment || []).map(function(x) {
          return '<div class="text-[10px] py-1 font-mono">' + escAdm(x.id) + ' · ' + escAdm(x.name) + '</div>';
        }).join('');
        var profRows = [
          ['Ad Soyad', p.name],
          ['E-posta', p.email],
          ['Telefon', p.phone || '—'],
          ['Öğrenci / Kimlik no', sid || p.id],
          ['Rol', p.role],
          ['Seviye', p.level],
          ['Bölüm', p.bolum || p.department],
          ['Departman', p.department],
          ['Yetki (ham)', p.yetkiRaw]
        ];
        var profHtml = '<div class="mt-3 p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-xl border border-gray-100"><p class="text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase mb-2">Profil</p><div class="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-2 text-[11px]">';
        profRows.forEach(function(row) {
          if (!row[1] && row[1] !== 0) return;
          profHtml += '<p><span class="font-bold text-gray-500">' + escAdm(row[0]) + ':</span> ' + escAdm(row[1]) + '</p>';
        });
        profHtml += '</div></div>';
        var histArr = m.equipmentHistory || [];
        var lastMove = histArr.length ? histArr[0] : null;
        var lastEqLine = lastMove ? ('<div class="mt-3 p-3 bg-blue-50/80 rounded-xl border border-blue-100"><p class="text-[10px] font-black text-blue-900 uppercase mb-1">Son ekipman hareketi</p><p class="text-xs">' + escAdm(lastMove.eqName || '') + ' <span class="font-mono text-[10px]">(' + escAdm(lastMove.eqId) + ')</span></p><p class="text-[10px] text-gray-600 mt-1">Rez: <span class="font-mono">' + escAdm(lastMove.resId) + '</span> · ' + escAdm(lastMove.status) + '</p></div>') : '';
        return '<div class="mb-6 p-5 bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm"><p class="font-black text-lg">' + escAdm(p.name || '-') + '</p><p class="text-xs font-mono text-gray-500">' + escAdm(p.email || '') + '</p><p class="text-[10px] text-gray-400 mt-1">' + escAdm(m.userTypeLabel || '') + '</p>' + profHtml + lastEqLine
          + (pe ? '<div class="mt-3 text-[10px] font-black text-amber-800 uppercase">Bekleyen ekipman onayları</div><div class="max-h-28 overflow-y-auto mt-1">' + pe + '</div>' : '')
          + (ps ? '<div class="mt-3 text-[10px] font-black text-indigo-800 uppercase">Bekleyen stüdyo</div><div class="max-h-28 overflow-y-auto mt-1">' + ps + '</div>' : '')
          + '<div class="mt-3 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">Üzerindeki ekipman</div><div class="max-h-28 overflow-y-auto mt-1">' + (loan || '<p class="text-xs text-gray-400">Yok</p>') + '</div>'
          + (r15 ? '<div class="mt-3 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-400 uppercase">Son 15 gün (ekipman)</div><div class="max-h-32 overflow-y-auto mt-1">' + r15 + '</div>' : '')
          + (resp ? '<div class="mt-3 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">Sorumlu olduğu ekipman</div><div class="max-h-28 overflow-y-auto mt-1">' + resp + '</div>' : '')
          + '<div class="mt-3 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-400 uppercase">Son rezervasyonlar</div><div class="max-h-40 overflow-y-auto mt-1">' + (h || '<p class="text-gray-400 text-xs">Yok</p>') + '</div></div>';
      }).join('');
    }).withFailureHandler(function(e) { out.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600">' + escAdm(e.message) + '</p>'; }).adminUserLookup(q, currentAuthToken);
  }

  function loadAdminTicketsList() {
    var box = document.getElementById('tickets-container');
    if (!box) return;
    if (!ensureAdminToken_()) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600 text-sm">Oturum jetonu gerekli.</p>'; return; }
    box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400 text-sm">Yükleniyor…</p>';
    adminApiRequest('/admin/tickets').then(function(res) {
      var list = res.list || [];
      if (!list.length) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400">Talep yok.</p>'; return; }
      box.innerHTML = list.map(function(t) {
        var pending = String(t.status || '').toLowerCase().indexOf('bekle') >= 0 || String(t.status || '').toLowerCase() === 'pending';
        var tnoJs = String(t.ticket_no || '').replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
        var btns = pending ? '<div class="flex gap-2 mt-4"><button type="button" onclick="adminTicketAct(\'' + tnoJs + '\',\'approve\')" class="flex-1 bg-green-600 text-white text-[10px] font-black py-2 rounded-lg">Onayla</button><button type="button" onclick="adminTicketAct(\'' + tnoJs + '\',\'reject\')" class="flex-1 bg-red-100 text-red-700 text-[10px] font-black py-2 rounded-lg">Reddet</button></div>' : '';
        var desc = String(t.description || '');
        return '<div class="bg-white p-5 rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 mb-4 shadow-sm">' +
          '<p class="font-mono text-[10px] text-gray-400 mb-1">' + escAdm(t.ticket_no) + ' · ' + escAdm(t.created_at || '') + '</p>' +
          '<p class="font-black text-sm text-gray-900">' + escAdm(t.ticket_type || t.request_type || '') + '</p>' +
          '<div class="mt-3 grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-x-4 gap-y-2 text-[11px] text-gray-700">' +
          '<p><span class="font-black text-gray-500">İsim:</span> ' + escAdm(t.name) + '</p>' +
          '<p><span class="font-black text-gray-500">E-posta:</span> ' + escAdm(t.email) + '</p>' +
          '<p><span class="font-black text-gray-500">Dahili:</span> ' + escAdm(t.phone_ext || '—') + '</p>' +
          '<p><span class="font-black text-gray-500">Birim:</span> ' + escAdm(t.department || '—') + '</p>' +
          '<p><span class="font-black text-gray-500">Personel türü:</span> ' + escAdm(t.staff_type || '—') + '</p>' +
          '<p><span class="font-black text-gray-500">Talep türü:</span> ' + escAdm(t.request_type || '—') + '</p>' +
          '<p class="sm:col-span-2"><span class="font-black text-gray-500">Kullanım tarihi (sheet):</span> ' + escAdm(t.use_date || '—') + '</p>' +
          '<p class="sm:col-span-2"><span class="font-black text-gray-500">Saat aralığı:</span> ' + escAdm(t.start_dt || '—') + ' → ' + escAdm(t.end_dt || '—') + '</p>' +
          '<p class="sm:col-span-2"><span class="font-black text-gray-500">Mekân / lokasyon:</span> ' + escAdm(t.location || '—') + '</p>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="mt-3 p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-xl border border-gray-100"><p class="text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">Talep içeriği</p><p class="text-xs text-gray-800 whitespace-pre-wrap">' + escAdm(desc) + '</p></div>' +
          '<p class="text-[10px] mt-2"><span class="font-black text-gray-600">Durum:</span> ' + escAdm(t.status || '') + '</p>' +
          btns + '</div>';
      }).join('');
    }).catch(function(e) {
      box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600">' + escAdm((e && e.message) || 'Hata') + '</p>';
    });
  }
  function adminTicketAct(ticketNo, act) {
    if (!ensureAdminToken_()) return;
    if (act === 'reject') {
      openAdminUiDialog({
        title: 'Ticket Reddet',
        desc: 'Red gerekçesi zorunludur.',
        tone: 'danger',
        input: true,
        required: true,
        requiredMessage: 'Gerekçe gerekli.',
        placeholder: 'Red gerekçesi',
        okText: 'Reddet'
      }, function(rs) {
        adminApiRequest('/admin/tickets/reject', {
          method: 'POST',
          body: { ticket_no: ticketNo, reason: String(rs).trim() }
        }).then(function() {
          showToast('Reddedildi.');
          loadAdminTicketsList();
        }).catch(function(e) {
          showToast((e && e.message) || 'Hata', 'error');
        });
      });
      return;
    }
    openAdminUiDialog({
      title: 'Ticket Onayla',
      desc: 'Onay notu ekleyebilirsiniz (opsiyonel).',
      tone: 'success',
      input: true,
      required: false,
      placeholder: 'Onay notu (opsiyonel)',
      okText: 'Onayla'
    }, function(note) {
      adminApiRequest('/admin/tickets/approve', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: { ticket_no: ticketNo, note: note || '' }
      }).then(function() {
        showToast('Onaylandı.');
        loadAdminTicketsList();
      }).catch(function(e) {
        showToast((e && e.message) || 'Hata', 'error');
      });
    });
  }

  function loadAdminBizeList() {
    var box = document.getElementById('bize-container');
    if (!box) return;
    if (!ensureAdminToken_()) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600 text-sm">Oturum jetonu gerekli.</p>'; return; }
    box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400 text-sm">Yükleniyor…</p>';
    adminApiRequest('/admin/contact-messages').then(function(res) {
      var list = res.list || [];
      if (!list.length) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400">Mesaj yok.</p>'; return; }
      box.innerHTML = list.map(function(r) {
        var bzDom = String(r.id || '').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]/g, '_');
        var bzJs = String(r.id || '').replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
        return '<div class="bg-white p-4 rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 mb-3"><p class="text-[10px] font-mono text-gray-400">' + escAdm(r.id) + ' · ' + escAdm(r.created_at) + '</p><p class="font-bold text-sm">' + escAdm(r.user_name) + ' &lt;' + escAdm(r.user_email) + '&gt;</p><p class="text-xs text-gray-600 mt-2 whitespace-pre-wrap">' + escAdm(r.message) + '</p><p class="text-[10px] text-gray-400 mt-1">' + escAdm(r.status || '') + '</p>' + (r.admin_reply ? '<p class="text-xs text-green-800 mt-2">Yanıt: ' + escAdm(r.admin_reply) + '</p>' : '<div class="mt-2 flex gap-2"><textarea id="bize-reply-' + bzDom + '" rows="2" class="flex-1 text-xs border rounded-lg p-2" placeholder="Yanıt"></textarea><button type="button" onclick="submitBizeReply(\'' + bzJs + '\')" class="px-3 py-2 bg-[#e30613] text-white text-[10px] font-black rounded-lg">Gönder</button></div>') + '</div>';
      }).join('');
    }).catch(function(e) {
      box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600">' + escAdm((e && e.message) || 'Hata') + '</p>';
    });
  }
  function submitBizeReply(rowId) {
    var ta = document.getElementById('bize-reply-' + String(rowId || '').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]/g, '_'));
    var txt = ta ? ta.value.trim() : '';
    if (!txt) { showToast('Yanıt yazın.', 'error'); return; }
    adminApiRequest('/admin/contact-messages/reply', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: { row_id: String(rowId || ''), reply_text: txt }
    }).then(function() {
      showToast('Gönderildi.');
      loadAdminBizeList();
    }).catch(function(e) {
      showToast((e && e.message) || 'Hata', 'error');
    });
  }

  function loadAdminReports() {
    var box = document.getElementById('reports-container');
    if (!box) return;
    if (!ensureAdminToken_()) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600 text-sm">Oturum jetonu gerekli.</p>'; return; }
    box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400 text-sm">Yükleniyor…</p>';
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) {
      if (r.error) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600">' + escAdm(r.error) + '</p>'; return; }
      var inv = r.inventory || {};
      var ov = r.overdue || [];
      var t = r.tickets || {};
      var ts = t.status || {};
      var dep = t.byDepartment || [];
      var byType = t.byType || [];
      var trend = t.trend || [];
      var studio = r.studio || {};
      var studioRows = studio.by_studio || [];
      var equip = r.equipmentDemand || {};
      var topEq = equip.top_items || [];
      var topCat = equip.by_category || [];
      var maxTrend = 1;
      trend.forEach(function(x) { maxTrend = Math.max(maxTrend, Number(x.count || 0)); });
      function card(title, value, sub, tone) {
        var c = tone || 'slate';
        var bg = c === 'red' ? 'bg-red-50 border-red-200' : (c === 'green' ? 'bg-green-50 border-green-200' : (c === 'amber' ? 'bg-amber-50 border-amber-200' : 'bg-slate-50 border-slate-200'));
        return '<div class="rounded-2xl border ' + bg + ' p-4"><p class="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-wide text-gray-500">' + escAdm(title) + '</p><p class="text-2xl font-black text-gray-900 mt-1">' + escAdm(String(value)) + '</p><p class="text-[11px] text-gray-600 mt-1">' + escAdm(sub || '') + '</p></div>';
      }
      function miniBar(v, mx) {
        var w = mx <= 0 ? 0 : Math.max(3, Math.round((Number(v || 0) / mx) * 100));
        return '<div class="h-2 bg-gray-100 rounded-full overflow-hidden"><div class="h-2 bg-[#e30613] rounded-full" style="width:' + w + '%"></div></div>';
      }
      var depRows = dep.slice(0, 12).map(function(d) {
        return '<tr class="border-b border-gray-100"><td class="py-2 pr-2 text-xs text-gray-800">' + escAdm(d.department) + '</td><td class="py-2 pr-2 text-xs font-bold text-gray-900">' + escAdm(String(d.total || 0)) + '</td><td class="py-2 pr-2 text-xs text-green-700">' + escAdm(String(d.approved || 0)) + '</td><td class="py-2 pr-2 text-xs text-red-700">' + escAdm(String(d.rejected || 0)) + '</td><td class="py-2 text-xs text-gray-700">%' + escAdm(String(d.approval_rate || 0)) + '</td></tr>';
      }).join('');
      var typeRows = byType.slice(0, 10).map(function(x) {
        return '<div class="mb-2"><div class="flex justify-between text-xs mb-1"><span class="font-semibold text-gray-700">' + escAdm(x.type) + '</span><span class="font-black text-gray-900">' + escAdm(String(x.count || 0)) + '</span></div>' + miniBar(x.count, byType[0] ? Number(byType[0].count || 1) : 1) + '</div>';
      }).join('') || '<p class="text-xs text-gray-400">Veri yok.</p>';
      var trendRows = trend.slice(-14).map(function(x) {
        return '<div class="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1"><p class="w-20 text-[10px] text-gray-500">' + escAdm(String(x.day || '').slice(5)) + '</p><div class="flex-1">' + miniBar(x.count, maxTrend) + '</div><p class="w-6 text-right text-[10px] font-black text-gray-700">' + escAdm(String(x.count || 0)) + '</p></div>';
      }).join('') || '<p class="text-xs text-gray-400">Veri yok.</p>';
      var studioRowsHtml = studioRows.slice(0, 10).map(function(s) {
        return '<tr class="border-b border-gray-100"><td class="py-2 pr-2 text-xs text-gray-800">' + escAdm(s.studio) + '</td><td class="py-2 pr-2 text-xs font-bold text-gray-900">' + escAdm(String(s.total || 0)) + '</td><td class="py-2 pr-2 text-xs text-green-700">' + escAdm(String(s.approved || 0)) + '</td><td class="py-2 text-xs text-gray-600">' + escAdm(String(s.cancelled || 0)) + '</td></tr>';
      }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="4" class="py-3 text-xs text-gray-400">Veri yok.</td></tr>';
      var topEqRows = topEq.slice(0, 8).map(function(e) {
        return '<tr class="border-b border-gray-100"><td class="py-2 pr-2 text-xs text-gray-800">' + escAdm(e.name) + '</td><td class="py-2 text-xs font-bold text-gray-900">' + escAdm(String(e.count || 0)) + '</td></tr>';
      }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="2" class="py-3 text-xs text-gray-400">Veri yok.</td></tr>';
      var topCatRows = topCat.slice(0, 8).map(function(c) {
        return '<tr class="border-b border-gray-100"><td class="py-2 pr-2 text-xs text-gray-800">' + escAdm(c.category) + '</td><td class="py-2 text-xs font-bold text-gray-900">' + escAdm(String(c.count || 0)) + '</td></tr>';
      }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="2" class="py-3 text-xs text-gray-400">Veri yok.</td></tr>';
      box.innerHTML = '' +
        '<div class="space-y-4">' +
          '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-3">' +
            card('Ticket (30g)', ts.total || 0, 'Günlük ort: ' + (t.avgPerDay || 0), 'slate') +
            card('Bekleyen Ticket', ts.pending || 0, 'Aksiyon bekliyor', 'amber') +
            card('Onaylanan Ticket', ts.approved || 0, 'Tamamlanan işlem', 'green') +
            card('Gecikmiş Ekipman', ov.length, 'İade tarihi geçmiş', 'red') +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">' +
            '<div class="bg-white p-4 rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 lg:col-span-2"><h3 class="font-black text-sm mb-3">Birim Bazlı Ticket Dağılımı (30 gün)</h3><div class="overflow-x-auto"><table class="min-w-full"><thead><tr class="text-left text-[10px] uppercase text-gray-500 border-b border-gray-200"><th class="py-2 pr-2">Birim</th><th class="py-2 pr-2">Toplam</th><th class="py-2 pr-2">Onay</th><th class="py-2 pr-2">Red</th><th class="py-2">Onay %</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + depRows + '</tbody></table></div></div>' +
            '<div class="bg-white p-4 rounded-2xl border border-gray-100"><h3 class="font-black text-sm mb-3">Talep Türü</h3>' + typeRows + '</div>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">' +
            '<div class="bg-white p-4 rounded-2xl border border-gray-100"><h3 class="font-black text-sm mb-3">Günlük Ticket Trendi</h3>' + trendRows + '</div>' +
            '<div class="bg-white p-4 rounded-2xl border border-gray-100"><h3 class="font-black text-sm mb-3">Stüdyo Kullanımı (30 gün)</h3><div class="overflow-x-auto"><table class="min-w-full"><thead><tr class="text-left text-[10px] uppercase text-gray-500 border-b border-gray-200"><th class="py-2 pr-2">Stüdyo</th><th class="py-2 pr-2">Toplam</th><th class="py-2 pr-2">Onay</th><th class="py-2">İptal</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + studioRowsHtml + '</tbody></table></div></div>' +
            '<div class="bg-white p-4 rounded-2xl border border-gray-100"><h3 class="font-black text-sm mb-3">En Çok Talep Edilen</h3><p class="text-[10px] font-black uppercase text-gray-500 mb-1">Ekipman</p><table class="w-full mb-3"><tbody>' + topEqRows + '</tbody></table><p class="text-[10px] font-black uppercase text-gray-500 mb-1">Kategori</p><table class="w-full"><tbody>' + topCatRows + '</tbody></table></div>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="bg-white p-4 rounded-2xl border border-gray-100"><h3 class="font-black text-sm mb-2">Gecikmiş Ekipmanlar (' + ov.length + ')</h3><div class="overflow-x-auto"><table class="min-w-full"><thead><tr class="text-left text-[10px] uppercase text-gray-500 border-b border-gray-200"><th class="py-2 pr-2">Ekipman</th><th class="py-2 pr-2">Atanan</th><th class="py-2">Due Date</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + (ov.slice(0, 20).map(function(it) { return '<tr class="border-b border-gray-100"><td class="py-2 pr-2 text-xs">' + escAdm(it.name || it.id || '-') + '</td><td class="py-2 pr-2 text-xs">' + escAdm(it.assigned_name || it.assigned_to || '-') + '</td><td class="py-2 text-xs">' + escAdm(it.due_date || '-') + '</td></tr>'; }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="3" class="py-3 text-xs text-gray-400">Kayıt yok.</td></tr>') + '</tbody></table></div></div>' +
          '<details class="bg-white p-4 rounded-2xl border border-gray-100"><summary class="cursor-pointer text-xs font-black text-gray-600">Ham envanter özeti (debug)</summary><pre class="text-[10px] overflow-x-auto whitespace-pre-wrap text-gray-700 mt-3">' + escAdm(JSON.stringify(inv, null, 2)) + '</pre></details>' +
        '</div>';
    }).getAdminReportsSummaryBridge(currentAuthToken);
  }

  function runGoogleStudioSyncNow() {
    if (!ensureAdminToken_()) { showToast('Oturum jetonu gerekli.', 'error'); return; }
    showToast('Google takvim senkronu başlatıldı…');
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res && res.error) { showToast(res.error, 'error'); return; }
      var red = (res && res.red) ? res.red : {};
      var green = (res && res.green) ? res.green : {};
      var msg = 'Senkron tamamlandı · RED(C:' + (red.created || 0) + ', U:' + (red.updated || 0) + ') · GREEN(C:' + (green.created || 0) + ', U:' + (green.updated || 0) + ')';
      showToast(msg, 'success');
      loadAdminReports();
    }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      showToast((err && err.message) || 'Google sync hatası.', 'error');
    }).syncGoogleCalendarsToStudiosBridge(currentAuthToken);
  }

  function submitAdminSpecialAccess() {
    var emailEl = document.getElementById('sa-email');
    var studioEl = document.getElementById('sa-studio');
    var untilEl = document.getElementById('sa-until');
    var email = emailEl ? String(emailEl.value || '').trim().toLowerCase() : '';
    var studio = studioEl ? String(studioEl.value || '').trim().toUpperCase() : '';
    var until = untilEl ? String(untilEl.value || '').trim() : '';
    if (!email || email.indexOf('@') < 0) { showToast('Geçerli e-posta girin.', 'error'); return; }
    if (!studio) { showToast('Stüdyo seçin.', 'error'); return; }
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res && res.error) { showToast(res.error, 'error'); return; }
      showToast('Özel izin kaydedildi.', 'success');
      loadAdminSpecialAccessList();
    }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      showToast((err && err.message) || 'Hata', 'error');
    }).adminSpecialAccessUpsertBridge(currentAuthToken, email, studio, until);
  }

  function loadAdminSpecialEquipmentOptions() {
    var sel = document.getElementById('sea-equipment');
    if (!sel) return;
    if (!ensureAdminToken_()) { sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Oturum gerekli</option>'; return; }
    sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Yükleniyor…</option>';
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res && res.error) { sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Hata: ' + escAdm(res.error) + '</option>'; return; }
      var list = (res && res.list) ? res.list : [];
      if (!list.length) { sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Seviye 4-5 ekipman yok</option>'; return; }
      sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Ekipman seçin</option>' + list.map(function(it) {
        return '<option value="' + escAttr(String(it.id || '')) + '">' + escAdm(String(it.name || it.id || '')) + ' [' + escAdm(String(it.id || '')) + '] (L' + escAdm(String(it.eq_level || '')) + ')</option>';
      }).join('');
    }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Hata: ' + escAdm((err && err.message) || 'Bilinmeyen') + '</option>';
    }).adminSpecialEquipmentOptionsBridge(currentAuthToken);
  }

  function submitAdminSpecialEquipmentAccess() {
    var emailEl = document.getElementById('sea-email');
    var eqEl = document.getElementById('sea-equipment');
    var untilEl = document.getElementById('sea-until');
    var email = emailEl ? String(emailEl.value || '').trim().toLowerCase() : '';
    var equipmentId = eqEl ? String(eqEl.value || '').trim().toUpperCase() : '';
    var until = untilEl ? String(untilEl.value || '').trim() : '';
    if (!email || email.indexOf('@') < 0) { showToast('Geçerli e-posta girin.', 'error'); return; }
    if (!equipmentId) { showToast('Ekipman seçin.', 'error'); return; }
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res && res.error) { showToast(res.error, 'error'); return; }
      showToast('Ekipman özel izni kaydedildi.', 'success');
      loadAdminSpecialEquipmentAccessList();
    }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      showToast((err && err.message) || 'Hata', 'error');
    }).adminSpecialEquipmentAccessUpsertBridge(currentAuthToken, email, equipmentId, until);
  }

  function saveAdminSpecialEquipmentAccessUntil(emailEsc) {
    var email = String(emailEsc || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    var eqSel = document.getElementById('sea-row-eq-' + trafficSafeDomId(email));
    var untilInp = document.getElementById('sea-row-until-' + trafficSafeDomId(email));
    var equipmentId = eqSel ? String(eqSel.value || '').trim().toUpperCase() : '';
    var until = untilInp ? String(untilInp.value || '').trim() : '';
    if (!equipmentId) { showToast('Ekipman seçin.', 'error'); return; }
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res && res.error) { showToast(res.error, 'error'); return; }
      showToast('Ekipman özel izin kaydı güncellendi.', 'success');
      loadAdminSpecialEquipmentAccessList();
    }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      showToast((err && err.message) || 'Hata', 'error');
    }).adminSpecialEquipmentAccessUpsertBridge(currentAuthToken, email, equipmentId, until);
  }

  function deleteAdminSpecialEquipmentAccess(emailEsc) {
    var email = String(emailEsc || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    openAdminUiDialog({
      title: 'Ekipman Özel İzni Kaldır',
      desc: email + ' için ekipman özel izni silinsin mi?',
      tone: 'danger',
      input: false,
      okText: 'Sil'
    }, function() {
      google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
        if (res && res.error) { showToast(res.error, 'error'); return; }
        showToast('Ekipman özel izin silindi.', 'success');
        loadAdminSpecialEquipmentAccessList();
      }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
        showToast((err && err.message) || 'Hata', 'error');
      }).adminSpecialEquipmentAccessDeleteBridge(currentAuthToken, email);
    });
  }

  function saveAdminSpecialAccessUntil(emailEsc) {
    var email = String(emailEsc || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    var inp = document.getElementById('sa-row-until-' + trafficSafeDomId(email));
    var until = inp ? String(inp.value || '').trim() : '';
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res && res.error) { showToast(res.error, 'error'); return; }
      showToast('Bitiş tarihi güncellendi.', 'success');
      loadAdminSpecialAccessList();
    }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      showToast((err && err.message) || 'Hata', 'error');
    }).adminSpecialAccessUpsertBridge(currentAuthToken, email, (function() {
      var rowSel = document.getElementById('sa-row-studio-' + trafficSafeDomId(email));
      return rowSel ? rowSel.value : '';
    })(), until);
  }

  function deleteAdminSpecialAccess(emailEsc) {
    var email = String(emailEsc || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    openAdminUiDialog({
      title: 'Özel İzni Kaldır',
      desc: email + ' için özel izin tamamen silinsin mi?',
      tone: 'danger',
      input: false,
      okText: 'Sil'
    }, function() {
      google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
        if (res && res.error) { showToast(res.error, 'error'); return; }
        showToast('Özel izin silindi.', 'success');
        loadAdminSpecialAccessList();
      }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
        showToast((err && err.message) || 'Hata', 'error');
      }).adminSpecialAccessDeleteBridge(currentAuthToken, email);
    });
  }

  function loadAdminSpecialAccessList() {
    var box = document.getElementById('special-access-container');
    if (!box) return;
    if (!ensureAdminToken_()) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600 text-sm">Oturum jetonu gerekli.</p>'; return; }
    box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400 text-sm">Yükleniyor…</p>';
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res && res.error) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600">' + escAdm(res.error) + '</p>'; return; }
      var list = (res && res.list) ? res.list : [];
      if (!list.length) {
        box.innerHTML = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 p-8 text-center text-gray-400 text-sm">Aktif özel izin kaydı yok.</div>';
        return;
      }
      var rows = list.map(function(it) {
        var em = String(it.email || '').toLowerCase();
        var safe = trafficSafeDomId(em);
        var emJs = em.replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
        var studio = String(it.special_access || '').toUpperCase();
        var activeBadge = it.active ? '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-[10px] font-black bg-green-50 text-green-700 border border-green-200">Aktif</span>' : '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-[10px] font-black bg-gray-100 text-gray-500 border border-gray-200">Süresi geçmiş</span>';
        return '<tr class="border-b border-gray-100">' +
          '<td class="px-3 py-3 text-xs font-bold text-gray-800">' + escAdm(it.name || '—') + '<div class="text-[10px] text-gray-400 font-mono mt-1">' + escAdm(em) + '</div></td>' +
          '<td class="px-3 py-3 text-[11px] font-bold uppercase">' + escAdm(String(it.kind || '')) + '</td>' +
          '<td class="px-3 py-3"><select id="sa-row-studio-' + safe + '" class="text-xs border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-2 font-bold"><option value="GREEN"' + (studio === 'GREEN' ? ' selected' : '') + '>GREEN</option><option value="RED"' + (studio === 'RED' ? ' selected' : '') + '>RED</option><option value="PODCAST"' + (studio === 'PODCAST' ? ' selected' : '') + '>PODCAST</option><option value="DUBBING"' + (studio === 'DUBBING' ? ' selected' : '') + '>DUBBING</option></select></td>' +
          '<td class="px-3 py-3"><input type="date" id="sa-row-until-' + safe + '" value="' + escAttr(String(it.special_access_until || '')) + '" class="text-xs border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-2"></td>' +
          '<td class="px-3 py-3">' + activeBadge + '</td>' +
          '<td class="px-3 py-3"><div class="flex gap-2"><button type="button" onclick="saveAdminSpecialAccessUntil(\'' + emJs + '\')" class="px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-gray-900 text-white text-[10px] font-black">Kaydet</button><button type="button" onclick="deleteAdminSpecialAccess(\'' + emJs + '\')" class="px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-red-50 border border-red-200 text-red-700 text-[10px] font-black">Sil</button></div></td>' +
          '</tr>';
      }).join('');
      box.innerHTML = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 overflow-hidden"><div class="overflow-x-auto"><table class="w-full text-left"><thead class="bg-gray-50"><tr><th class="px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">Kullanıcı</th><th class="px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">Tip</th><th class="px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">Stüdyo</th><th class="px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">Bitiş</th><th class="px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">Durum</th><th class="px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">İşlem</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + rows + '</tbody></table></div></div>';
    }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600 text-sm">' + escAdm((err && err.message) || 'Hata') + '</p>';
    }).adminSpecialAccessListBridge(currentAuthToken);
  }

  function loadAdminSpecialEquipmentAccessList() {
    var box = document.getElementById('special-equipment-access-container');
    if (!box) return;
    if (!ensureAdminToken_()) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600 text-sm">Oturum jetonu gerekli.</p>'; return; }
    box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400 text-sm">Yükleniyor…</p>';
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(optRes) {
      var optList = (optRes && optRes.list) ? optRes.list : [];
      google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
        if (res && res.error) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600">' + escAdm(res.error) + '</p>'; return; }
        var list = (res && res.equipment_list) ? res.equipment_list : [];
        if (!list.length) {
          box.innerHTML = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 p-8 text-center text-gray-400 text-sm">Aktif ekipman özel izin kaydı yok.</div>';
          return;
        }
        function equipmentOptionsHtml(selectedId) {
          var cur = String(selectedId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
          var opts = '<option value="">Ekipman seçin</option>' + optList.map(function(it) {
            var id = String(it.id || '').trim().toUpperCase();
            var sel = id === cur ? ' selected' : '';
            var label = String(it.name || it.id || '') + ' [' + id + '] (L' + String(it.eq_level || '') + ')';
            return '<option value="' + escAttr(id) + '"' + sel + '>' + escAdm(label) + '</option>';
          }).join('');
          if (cur && optList.every(function(it) { return String(it.id || '').trim().toUpperCase() !== cur; })) {
            opts = '<option value="' + escAttr(cur) + '" selected>' + escAdm(cur + ' (listede yok)') + '</option>' + opts;
          }
          return opts;
        }
        var rows = list.map(function(it) {
          var em = String(it.email || '').toLowerCase();
          var safe = trafficSafeDomId(em);
          var emJs = em.replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
          var activeBadge = it.active ? '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-[10px] font-black bg-green-50 text-green-700 border border-green-200">Aktif</span>' : '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-[10px] font-black bg-gray-100 text-gray-500 border border-gray-200">Süresi geçmiş</span>';
          return '<tr class="border-b border-gray-100">' +
            '<td class="px-3 py-3 text-xs font-bold text-gray-800">' + escAdm(it.name || '—') + '<div class="text-[10px] text-gray-400 font-mono mt-1">' + escAdm(em) + '</div></td>' +
            '<td class="px-3 py-3"><select id="sea-row-eq-' + safe + '" class="w-full text-xs border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-2 font-semibold">' + equipmentOptionsHtml(it.special_equipment_access || '') + '</select></td>' +
            '<td class="px-3 py-3"><input type="date" id="sea-row-until-' + safe + '" value="' + escAttr(String(it.special_equipment_access_until || '')) + '" class="text-xs border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-2"></td>' +
            '<td class="px-3 py-3">' + activeBadge + '</td>' +
            '<td class="px-3 py-3"><div class="flex gap-2"><button type="button" onclick="saveAdminSpecialEquipmentAccessUntil(\'' + emJs + '\')" class="px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-gray-900 text-white text-[10px] font-black">Kaydet</button><button type="button" onclick="deleteAdminSpecialEquipmentAccess(\'' + emJs + '\')" class="px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-red-50 border border-red-200 text-red-700 text-[10px] font-black">Sil</button></div></td>' +
            '</tr>';
        }).join('');
        box.innerHTML = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 overflow-hidden"><div class="overflow-x-auto"><table class="w-full text-left"><thead class="bg-gray-50"><tr><th class="px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">Kullanıcı</th><th class="px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">Ekipman</th><th class="px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">Bitiş</th><th class="px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">Durum</th><th class="px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black text-gray-500 uppercase">İşlem</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + rows + '</tbody></table></div></div>';
      }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
        box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600 text-sm">' + escAdm((err && err.message) || 'Hata') + '</p>';
      }).adminSpecialAccessListBridge(currentAuthToken);
    }).withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600 text-sm">' + escAdm((err && err.message) || 'Ekipman listesi alınamadı') + '</p>';
    }).adminSpecialEquipmentOptionsBridge(currentAuthToken);
  }

  function loadIIWAdmin() {
    var box = document.getElementById('iiw-admin-container');
    if (!box) return;
    if (!ensureAdminToken_()) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600 text-sm">Oturum jetonu gerekli.</p>'; return; }
    box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400 text-sm">Yükleniyor…</p>';
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) {
      if (r.error) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-red-600">' + escAdm(r.error) + '</p>'; return; }
      var list = r.list || [];
      if (!list.length) { box.innerHTML = '<p class="text-gray-400">Kayıt yok.</p>'; return; }
      box.innerHTML = list.map(function(t) {
        var tid = String(t.id || '');
        var sid = trafficSafeDomId(tid);
        var tjs = tid.replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
        return '<div class="bg-white p-4 rounded-xl border border-gray-100 mb-3 text-xs"><p class="font-mono text-[10px] text-gray-400">' + escAdm(tid) + '</p><p class="font-bold">' + escAdm(t.studentName || t.studentId || '') + '</p><p class="text-gray-600 mt-2">' + escAdm(t.jobDetail || '') + '</p><div class="mt-3 flex flex-wrap gap-2 items-center"><input type="number" step="0.5" min="0" placeholder="Saat" id="iiw-h-' + sid + '" class="border rounded-lg px-2 py-1 w-24"><input type="email" placeholder="Öğrenci e-posta" id="iiw-e-' + sid + '" class="flex-1 min-w-[160px] border rounded-lg px-2 py-1 text-[10px]"><button type="button" onclick="submitIIWHoursAdmin(\'' + tjs + '\',\'' + sid + '\')" class="bg-gray-900 text-white px-3 py-2 rounded-lg text-[10px] font-black">Saat ekle</button></div></div>';
      }).join('');
    }).getIIWTasksAdminBridge(currentAuthToken);
  }

  function submitIIWHoursAdmin(taskId, safeId) {
    var hEl = document.getElementById('iiw-h-' + safeId);
    var eEl = document.getElementById('iiw-e-' + safeId);
    var h = hEl ? hEl.value : '';
    var em = eEl ? eEl.value.trim() : '';
    if (!em || !h) { showToast('E-posta ve saat gerekli.', 'error'); return; }
    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) {
      if (r && r.error) { showToast(r.error, 'error'); return; }
      if (r && r.success) { showToast('Kaydedildi. Toplam: ' + (r.total != null ? r.total : '')); loadIIWAdmin(); }
      else showToast('Kayıt bulunamadı veya hata.', 'error');
    }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { showToast(err.message || 'Hata', 'error'); }).saveIIWHoursAdminBridge(currentAuthToken, taskId, em, h);
  }
  </script>
</body>
